thus his **power** is exalted beyond measure,
his **virtue** vast, beyond all crossing.

With **Great Compassion** and **Great Aspiration**,
**Great Sageliness** and **Great Benevolence**,
he manifests a body of **boundless virtue**—
the **Great Heavenly Sovereign** (Yùhuáng Dàtīanzūn).
This title extols the **Jade Sovereign’s** great **virtue**.

With **sincere reverence**, he pays homage and ascends to the **Imperial Seat**,
dwelling high in the **Celestial Palace** of the **Pure and Mysterious Realm**.
He **pervasively wanders** through all **White Jade Capitals**,
pervasively traversing and inspecting all **Great Heavenly Palaces**—
the **White Jade Capitals** indeed.
He **universally manifests** within the **Ten Directions’ Golden Gates**—
universally pervading and widely manifesting in the **Golden Gates** of all **Great Heavenly Palaces** in the **Ten Directions**.

In **serene stillness**, he responds with **effortless adaptability**;
when he departs or arrives, he is **unconstrained and free**.
Great stillness yet able to conform—
whether departing or arriving, his **marvelous use** unfolds naturally,
achieving **Great Freedom**, never bound or constrained.
His **departures and arrivals**, extensions and flexions,
his **convergence and dispersion**, beginnings and endings—
all such.

Though **united**, he may be **divided**;
his **transformation and adaptation** are **perfect and fluid**, yet **ineffable**.
When **converged**, he may be **distinctly parted**—
his **divine transformations** and **marvelous changes**,
perfectly fluid and vast, lively and unrestrained,
ineffable and beyond measure,
**transformation and adaptation**.

As the **Buddha** said: *"With a mere gesture, he brings forth all"*—
nothing is not the **Dao**.
As the **Confucian** scholars said: *"He encounters sources on both sides."*

He **expounds** the **Dao** of **Pure Liberation**—
he **proclaims** the **True Purity** and **True Emptiness**,
the **Great Awakening** and **Perfect Freedom**.
He **delivers** those mired in **sorrow and suffering**.

**Naturally and spontaneously**, beyond all recognition.
The **Sovereign’s** marvelous transformations unfold naturally—
not within human perception or understanding.

Or, if one takes the **recognition** of what can be recognized as the **will**,
it is not so.
Or, if one takes it as **awakening recognition**,
it is also not so.

With **Great Compassion** and **Great Aspiration**,
**Great Sageliness** and **Great Benevolence**,
he manifests a body of **Pure and Natural Emptiness**—
the **Great Heavenly Sovereign** (Yùhuáng Dàtīanzūn).
This title extols the **Jade Sovereign’s** **holy virtue** in its **absolute purity**.

With **sincere reverence**, he pays homage and recalls:
In past lives, as a **princely heir**,
he endured **suffering** to witness the **profound mysteries** of the **Dao**.

Over **three thousand and more kalpas** of **cultivation and practice**,
it was as though accomplished in a single day.
For **infinite myriads of beings**, he **delivered and saved**,
his compassion extending broadly to the **Ten Directions**.

Though his **Dharma Body** arose from the **embryonic essence** of the **womb and viscera**,
his **Holy Form** emerged from the **transformation** of the **Dao’s source**.
The **Jade Sovereign’s** manifestation—
his **Dharma Body** and **Holy Form**, though born from the **embryonic foundation** of the **womb’s sac** and the **visceral spirit**,
truly are the **marvelous transformations** of the **Great Dao’s** origin.

**Unbroken and unextinguished**, he vanishes yet remains.
He never decays, forever unvanquished.
Vanished as though gone, yet **truly wondrously present**;
vanished as though stored, yet **truly void and ineffable**.

With **Great Compassion** and **Great Aspiration**,
**Great Sageliness** and **Great Benevolence**,
he manifests a **body of unshakable divine clarity**,
the **Supreme True Emptiness Dharma Body**—
the **Great Heavenly Sovereign** (Yùhuáng Dàtīanzūn).
This title extols the **Jade Sovereign’s** **holy fruit** in its **eternal truth**.

**Long kneeling in repentance**—
**long kneeling**, prostrate upon the earth,
with **sincere humility and utmost reverence**.
Or, if one says **long kneeling** refers to **prolonged bending of the knees**,
it is not so.

**Repentance**—
to **confess one’s own faults** and vow to **forever extinguish this evil**.
**Remorse**—
to **regret past transgressions** and vow to **self-reform**,
as when a **culprit surrenders** himself.

From **beginningless kalpas**,
we, your **subjects** (as those who recite the scriptures and are like the virtuous),
have been **covered by ignorance and afflictions**,
obscuring our **True Mind**.
Human nature is inherently **clear**,
yet through **phenomena and emotions**, the mind is stirred,
its own light **veiled and obscured**,
giving rise to **delusive thoughts**—
thus called **ignorance and afflictions**.
From **ignorant thoughts**, the mind is **troubled and restless**,
**hateful and vexed**, losing its **pure heart**—
thus said to **cover the True Mind**.
The **True Mind** remains constant,
though not lost, **ignorance and afflictions** cause it to **darken and be bound**,
as though **covered by things unseen**.

**Now cast off**, our **original truth** is revealed.

We have **habitually committed** the **Three Evil Karmas**—
**habitually**, not just **exclusively** practicing killing, theft, and licentiousness.
Even **killing thoughts**, **theft intentions**, or **licentious desires**
cannot be **utterly severed** in awareness—
thus, we **habitually** engage in evil.

This **body** is the **Three Evil Karmas**.

We **habitually employ** the **Four Evil Tongues**—
**two-faced speech**, spreading strife with **forked tongues**;
or **groundless fabrications**, uttering false words;
or **shriveled, insidious flattery**, decorating speech with **beautiful yet deceitful language**,
**perverting others’ ears** with **empty talk**, not based on truth.

We **slander** the **True and Authentic Great Vehicle Teachings**—
or, not hearing the **Great Dao**, we **erroneously condemn** and **defame**,
**slandering** the **Great Vehicle’s** **orthodox teachings** of **Confucianism, Daoism, and Buddhism**.

We **quarrel and disrupt**, **alienating kin and friends**—
**quarreling** is not **physical fighting**,
but **inciting false disputes** with **provocative words**,
disrupting **harmony among kin and friends**,
**separating** the **concord of families**.

The **three preceding lines** all describe the **Four Evil Tongues**.

We **indulge** in the **Three Poisons of Greed, Anger, and Delusion**—
or **desire without satisfaction**, greedily seeking without end;
or **resentment and vexation**, ceaseless **anger and hatred**.
Or **mired in delusion**, stubbornly fixated,
**stupid and unchanging**.

The **Three Poisons of Greed, Anger, and Delusion**—
some take the **dark** as a **disease**,
or the **past, present, and future** as the **three minds**—
all are not correct.

「**Praise** and **anger**, **love** and **aversion**, **desire**—these **seven defilements** **foster the Seven Arrogances**.

As **Liu Langran** says:
**Contentment** breeds **joy**; **provocation** breeds **anger**; **fulfillment of wishes** breeds **infatuation**; **contrary intentions** breed **disgust**.
The **three preceding defilements**—**joy**, **anger**, and **infatuation**—when **compounded** with the **four latter ones**, become the **Seven Arrogances**.

The first: **coveting worldly splendor**, not seeking the **Great Dao/Way**, is **Mad Arrogance**.
The second: **indulging in malevolent thoughts**, not believing in **karmic retribution**, is **Reckless Arrogance**.
The third: **lost in illusion and delusion**, not submitting to the **True Dharma**, is **Profane Arrogance**.
The fourth: **delighting in mundane passions**, not associating with the **virtuous**, is **Proud Arrogance**.
The fifth: **concealing resentment and jealousy**, not fearing the **sacred scriptures**, is **Negligent Arrogance**.
The sixth: **yielding to lust and craving**, not safeguarding the **body**, is **Slothful Arrogance**.
The seventh: **unrelenting aversion**, not attaining the **Pure Lands**, not revering the **Divine**, is **Contemptuous Arrogance**.

Some say the **seven emotions**—**joy**, **anger**, **sorrow**, **fear**, **love**, **aversion**, and **desire**—are the **Seven Arrogances**.
But all arise from **joy**, **anger**, **love**, and **aversion**, which **exacerbate the Three Poisons**—**greed**, **anger**, and **delusion**—and thus cannot be **counted among the Seven Arrogances**.
This view is incorrect; **Liu Langran’s** explanation is right. **Examine carefully**, those who study.

The **sinful roots** of **countless past lives** are **difficult to recall**.
The **evil deeds** and **sinful roots** accumulated across **endless kalpas** are **hard to trace or remember**.

The **stains of myriad lives** are **immeasurable**.
The **karmic defilements** of **countless existences**, the **pollutions** of **past lives**, are **beyond reckoning**, their number **unknown**.

**Repentance** to the **Supreme Sage of Boundless Compassion**—
**Sincere return**, **eternal devotion**.
**Relying on** the **Supreme Sage’s** **Great Compassion**, **supporting** the **Divine Benevolence**, in **silent gratitude** I pray for the **permanent eradication** of my **transgressions**.

*Compassion* may also be read as *Reverence*, but that is **too constrained**.

**Unveiling** the **True Mind**, **extending** **repentance**.
**Unveiling** the **authentic benevolent heart**, **humbling** myself in **sincere repentance** and **remorse**.

**All sins** of **ten thousand kalpas** and **myriad lives**—
**Ten thousand kalpas**, **myriad lives**—briefly enumerated to speak of **all past sins** and **defilements**.
I **pray** that through **repentance**, they **all be purged**.

**Offering** this **body and mind** to the **Supreme True One**—
**Offering** this **perceived form** and **mind** **eternally** to the **True Sage**, **solely devoting** to the **Supreme True One**.
I **solemnly pray** that **all sinful roots** be **fully forgiven**.
I **solemnly pray** that **all past sinful roots** be **granted absolution** without **knowledge or intent**.

With **utter sincerity**, I **take this vow**—
I **pray** that my **eyes** may **always behold** the **Jade Millipede’s** **radiant form**,
That my **ears** may **always hear** the **sacred teachings**,
That my **nose** may **always inhale** the **fragrance of all sublime perfumes**,
That my **tongue** may **always extol** the **Supreme Dao/Way**,
That my **body** may **never be defiled** by **licentious impurities**,
That my **mind** may **always retain** the **True Faith**.

I **vow** to **repay** the **Fourfold Debt of Gratitude**—
**Heaven and Earth**, **sustaining life**; **Sun and Moon**, **illuminating all**; **Kings and Lands**, **protecting existence**; **Parents**, **giving birth**.
I **vow** to **relieve** the **Threefold Sufferings** of **samsara**—
**Sufferings of form**, **birth and death**; **sufferings of sense**, **earthly afflictions**; **sufferings of mind**, **torment of the spirit**.
I **vow** to **broadly extend** **compassion** and **pity** for **all beings**,
Or, as some say, to **broadly extend** the **Emperor’s compassion**.
I **vow** to **widespreadly practice** **skillful means** to **liberate all sentient beings**.

**Supreme Jade Emperor of Great Compassion**—
*See previous reference*.
**Protecting** my **vows**, **fulfilling** them **completely**.

**Vows** now **concluded**.
*Finalization*.

**Repentance** to the **Three Jewels**.
*See previous reference*.

**The Supreme Daoist Mantra of the Great Immortal**, **the profound essence of the Primordial Void**.
**Great is Yuan Shi**—
**Great is Yuan Shi**, **beyond measure**.
*See later reference*.

*See previous reference*.

**Ascending to the True Celestial Nature**—
**Ascending to the True Celestial Nature**, **guiding and receiving** the **Divine Essence**.
Some say: **“Ascending the Seat to receive”**, but that is **too constrained**.

**The Mystic Seat delivers the Teachings**—
The **Daoist Body** **abides eternally**, **illuminating all ten directions**.
The **Seat** is not **mundane**; it **soars above the void**, **ruling the celestial pole**.
**The Void Seat’s teachings** **float in silence**, **transcendent and boundless**.
**The Mystic Seat is serene and soundless**.

**The Jade Emperor emits radiance**—
*See later reference*.

**Joyous celebration beyond speech.**
Joyous celebration **cannot be spoken of in words.**
This is **mind-to-mind transmission**—
This is the **true scripture**, the **essential transmission** of the **Most Sacred Master of the Teachings**.
Also called **Heavenly Root**.
This scripture is the **mysterious root of the Heavenly Dao**, not the **earthly thunder** of the *Fu* complex.
The **Great Perfect Mantra**—
*See later reference*.
**Jade Chapter, Cavernous Text**—
**Azure Jade Heavenly Chapter, Great Cavernous Sacred Text**.
Collected to form a book—
Collected from **Yuan Shi’s** secret utterances and the **clarified requests of the Immortals**, to compose the **Jade Emperor’s scripture**.
**Disseminating the Divine and True**—
**Broadcasting the Divine and True** to spread the **Sacred Teachings**; when the **classics are proclaimed**, this is the meaning.
Now, as a subject, I face east and recite—
I sit facing east and recite this scripture.
I wish to **align with Heaven eternally**,
To **permanently recite this scripture in harmony with Heaven**.
**Life and death alike attain fruition**—
**Whether living or dead, all attain the Dao’s fruition**.
**Forever crossing the River of Love**—
**Forever emerging from the River of Love**.
The **River of Love** is the hardest bond for beings to sever—
It is the **true suffering’s ford**—
Reciting this scripture ensures all **forever cross the River of Love**.
**Contemplate the Venerable Form**—
**Meditate on the Jade Emperor’s Venerable Form**.

**Proclaiming the Precious Name**—
Proclaim the Jade Emperor’s Precious Name.
With utmost sincerity, **submit to the Command** and pay homage to the **Most High**—*as previously seen*.

The **Supreme Heaven of Limitless Perfection**—
The **Supreme Void of Highest Mysterious Surge**, the **Limitless Perfection**—the **Supreme Heaven**.
The **Realm of Marvelous Existence and Mysterious Truth**—
The **Jade Emperor’s Celestial Palace**, where **mysterious symbols and auspicious radiance** shine—**not mere illusions or false forms**.
**Unending and unspoiled**, its depths are **hard to fathom**—thus it is called the **Realm of Marvelous Existence and Mysterious Truth**.

**Vast and boundless**, the **Purple-Gold Celestial Gate**—
**Vast and boundless**, the **Purple-Gold Auspicious Mysterious Form’s Golden Gate**.

The **Supreme Void’s Jade-Pure Palace**—
**Supreme Void**—not the **Celestial Enclosure of the Sun and Moon’s Heaven**, but the **Most High’s Mysterious Void’s Jade-Pure Palace**, where the Jade Emperor resides.
**Mysterious Auspicious Qi and Golden Light** stretch **forty billion ten-thousand li**, **majestic and unchanging**, **never decaying or sinking**, **free from all defilement**—no other heavens can compare, hence it is called the **Supreme Void’s Jade-Pure Palace**.

The **Limitless, Supreme Holy One**—
**Dao lofty without limit**, **rank exalted beyond compare**, the **Great Sage of Supreme Virtue**.

**Broadly radiating boundless light**—
**Vast without end**, the **Azure Fall’s Deep Mysteries** emit **greatest, boundless radiance**.

**Silent and boundless, without origin**—
Though **emanating great radiance**, **void and unfathomable**, **silent and unrecognizable**, **vastly formless without root or source**.

**The Mysterious Standard governing all Ten Directions**—
The **Dao’s True Body**, **majestic and sweeping**, as the **source of all Divinity**, the **Lord of Ten Thousand Heavens**, the **Holy Ancestor of Cataclysms**—this is the **Mysterious Standard governing all Ten Directions**.

**The Eternal, Silent True Constant Dao**—
**Deeply silent and still**, **ever-clear and ever-stable**, the **True Constant Dao that never alters**.

**The Boundless Great Miraculous Power**—
**Vast beyond measure**, **fathomless without trace**, the **Greatest Miraculous Power**.

**The Jade Sovereign, Great Heavenly Venerable One**—
**Supreme Emperor of the Void’s Highest Heaven**.
The **Jade Sovereign** is not merely the **Venerable of One Heaven**, but the **Lord of Ten Thousand Heavens**, the **Source of the Three Teachings**, the **Supreme Limitless Great Heavenly Venerable One**, the **Highest Emperor of the Mysterious Void’s Boundless Sky**.

**Recite these ten sacred phrases**, bowing **once per phrase**.
If unable to bow for each phrase, **bow once first**, then recite all.
Afterward, **nine bows**—merely reciting **"Jade Sovereign, Great Heavenly Venerable One, Supreme Emperor of the Highest Void"** suffices.

**Homage completed**, sit upright and recite the scripture.

**The Great Marshal Ma Lingguan** declares:
*"This scripture is the King of Laws—beneficial to gods, humans, ghosts, and spirits, never failing.*
*In the world, whether male or female, regardless of poverty or wealth, literacy or illiteracy—if one respects this scripture, hears it, even a woman may transform into a man, and all gain blessings and longevity.*
*Or if one prints, crafts, or donates it, or encourages others to hold and recite it, the merit is boundless.*
*Only with utmost sincerity—never with doubt or negligence.*
*Where this scripture resides, all deities protect it.*
*Heed my words, and the gods will eternally bless you.*
*Strive diligently, do not squander this fortunate bond."*

**Supreme Jade Emperor’s Original Scripture Collection**
**Volume One**

**Divine Prowess of the Celestial Palace of Qingwei (First Section)**

The **Ancestral Celestial Master** says:
The **Celestial Palace of Qingwei** transcends the Three Realms, purifying all defilements, its void and mystery luminous and wondrous, subtle beyond measure. Dwelling within the Three Pure Realms, it is the Great Celestial Palace, where the Jade Emperor resides. The **Primordial Origin** expounded this scripture here, governing this wondrous realm with supreme and mysterious efficacy, its transformations boundless and unfathomable. This scripture expounds its essence as the **highest section**; only divine insight and profound wisdom can comprehend it—hence, it is called **"Divine Prowess (First Section)."**

**Scholar’s Note:** Ancient texts define *divine* as "mysterious transformations beyond measure," and *prowess* as "pervasive without omission." It is the crown of the Five Sections and the essence of the Three Pure Realms. The **Dan Platform** aligns with this—once understood, the entire scripture becomes clear.

**Divine Prowess (First Chapter)**

At that time, the **Primordial Origin Celestial Venerable**—
*"At that time"* refers to the initial manifestation of the **Boundless Mirror**, the commencement of **Great Mystery’s** transformation, the auspicious confluence of all saints, the moment this scripture was to be expounded.

*Yuan* (元) means **great**, **first**; *Shǐ* (始) means **origin**. The enlightenment of all saints began with the **Primordial Origin**.

Thus, it is called the **Primordial Origin Celestial Venerable**.

**Within the Celestial Realm of Qingwei**—
*(Explanation of Qingwei Heaven provided earlier.)*

**Divine Prowess (First Chapter continued)**

**The Celestial Capital of Jade and the Golden Gate**
The **Celestial Sovereign of Purple Clarity and White Purity** spoke:
*"The abode of the Jade Emperor is built of white jade as its capital (京) and yellow gold as its gate (阙), not the mundane gold and jade of mortal realms, but divine manifestations of wondrous transformation—azure heavens resplendent with celestial splendor, adorning the sacred precincts of the court. Hence, it is called the **Celestial Capital of Jade and the Golden Gate**.*

**The Seven-Treasured Mystic Gardens**
The **Celestial Sovereign of White Purity** spoke:
*The Seven Treasures are: jade of emerald hue, stages of luminous jade, palaces of lapis lazuli, walls inscribed with dragon motifs, white jade citadels, vermilion gates, and golden radiance that pierces all darkness. Another account names them: glass, crystal, pearls, agate, coral, amber, and conch shells. The **Mystic Gardens** are the secret precincts of the **Double Mystery**.*

**The Jade Emperor’s Palace and Ascended Seat of Radiance**
**Zhang Liang** spoke:
*"In the Primordial Origin epoch, the Celestial Venerable ascended to preside over the Jade Emperor’s Palace, ascending the **Great Seat of Radiant Clarity and Mystic Sovereignty**.*

**With the countless assemblies of the Boundless**
He expounded the **Sacred Treasure of Pure and Undivided Oneness**."

**Zhang Liang** spoke:
*"When the Primordial Origin ascended the seat, the boundless true saints gathered in assembly. Thus, it is said: ‘With the countless assemblies of the Boundless,’ proclaiming the **Mystic Treasure of Divine Clarity**, pure and unstained, the supreme secret of **True Oneness**, unobstructed and unmixed, the **Undivided Law-Gate**."*

**The Ten Directions’ Gathering Explanation**
*"The human **Primordial Spirit** is the essence of life and destiny. The Great Celestial Venerable, within the Qingwei Heavenly Realm, inherently possesses this. The **Celestial Capital of Jade and the Golden Gate**, adorned with the Seven Treasures, is inherently possessed by all. The human body’s **yin-yang vital essence, spirit-qi, and refined essence** are the Seven Treasures of the self. Thus, the **Lingting Mystic Gardens** harmonize heaven and humanity.*

*When the Heavenly Sovereign is serene and composed, the **Seat of Radiant Clarity** may be ascended, and all limbs obey in unison. Concentrating the spirit and aligning with the Dao, one becomes the Celestial Venerable’s seat, joining the Boundless assemblies in proclaiming the **Sacred Treasure of Pure and Undivided Oneness**.*

*Yet the Dao has no fixed form—when one awakens with clarity, one attains the secret realm of subtlety, as straightforward as a great road. To enter it is natural.*

*Hence, it is called the **Law-Gate**."*

---
**Divine Prowess (Second Chapter)**

**At that time**—
*The moment when the Primordial Origin ascended the seat.*

**The Celestial Sovereign Emperor**
*"Emperor"* denotes unparalleled exaltation, hence the appellation.

**With the Celestial True Ones, the Flying Heavenly Great Saints, the Boundless Divine Kings, the Spirit Boys and Jade Girls—nine hundred million in number—observing strict purity and bearing sacred banners, standing in attendance.**

**Zhang Liang** spoke:
*"‘With’ means ‘together.’ ‘All’ refers to the multitude. The Jade Emperor, in concert with the celestial immortals and divine true ones, ascended in divine transformation and wondrous prowess. The **Flying Heavenly Great Saints**, the **Three Thousand Great Realms**, and the countless gods of the Boundless—those of the heavenly and earthly planes—along with the **Minor Yang Divine Qi** that responds to invocation, the **Spirit Boys** who attend with reverence, and the **Minor Yin Divine Qi** that transmits decrees, the **Jade Girls** who proclaim transformations—totaling nine hundred million divine beings.*

*Without revealing their divine radiance, they returned to the Primordial Origin’s essence, observing strict purity and holding sacred banners, standing beside the Primordial Origin’s Seat of Radiance."*

**The Heavenly Marshal Tian You** spoke:
*"Within the human body, there is the **True Sovereign, the Primordial Spirit**, unrestrained in its divine communication. There are also the **Flying Heavenly Great Saints**, whose spirit-qi guards the body. Even in the smallest interstices, there are the **Boundless Divine Kings**, the **Minor Yang’s Mystic Light**, the **Minor Yin’s Divine Motion**, and the **Spirit Boys and Jade Girls**. When the heart aligns with the Dao, the **Nine Hundred Million**—the great numbers of yang vigor—are also present, and the body’s spirits pay homage to the Primordial.*

*‘Observing strict purity’ means the mind is undivided; ‘holding sacred banners’ means the body is without sluggishness."*

**Master Guan’s Perspective** spoke:
*"Humans are akin to heaven and earth—when clear and unadulterated, the **Primordial Spirit** ascends to the pole. Indeed, it is like **Yan Hui’s heart-fasting** or the **legalist’s bearing of the banner**, singing in reverence without division, thus obeying the Heavenly Sovereign and attaining the Dao."*

---
**Divine Prowess (Third Chapter)**

**Thereupon,**

**Divine Prowess (Third Chapter)**

At this auspicious gathering,
The Jade Sovereign, knowing the hour was near, displayed the **Six Perfections** before the assembly, emitting a vast radiant light that illuminated all the **Primordial Dream Palaces** of the boundless heavens. Every realm trembled in response, and the ten directions of the infinite worlds became as transparent as **crystal and glass**, with no obstruction whatsoever.

**Master Zhuang** remarked:
*"The Jade Sovereign, aware that the time for the **Mystic Light’s** revelation had arrived and that the moment to propagate the **Law** and transmit the **Scriptures** was at hand, thus manifested the **Six Perfections** before the grand assembly. He emitted the most universal and luminous light, illuminating the boundless heavens, the **Dream Palaces** of all the celestial deities and divine spirits, and every sacred realm they inhabited. All were shaken and awestruck. The infinite worlds of all the **Sages and Buddhas** in the ten directions became as clear as **crystal and glass**, their light penetrating and revealing all without hindrance or concealment."*

**Master Zhang Wuzhang** explained:
*"The **Six Perfections**—**Vision-Perfection**, **Hearing-Perfection**, **Mind-Touch-Perfection**, **Mind-Meeting-Perfection**, **Foresight-Perfection**, and **Pre-illumination-Perfection**—are what the Buddhist tradition calls the **Six Divine Eyes** and such."*

**Master Zhuang** further clarified:
*"**Dream Palaces** are the abodes of the celestial emperors and deities—marvelous and resplendent in the heavens, not tainted by dust, never decaying, and unshakably firm. The mortal eye cannot perceive them, hence the term **Dream Palace**."*

*"Every sacred realm is the domain where the deities reside. These realms encompass all worlds—not merely human domains, but also celestial realms, which are also called **worlds**."*

*"Though **crystal** has form and light, it reveals all that it bears; **glass**, though flawless, leaves nothing unseen. The Jade Sovereign’s light penetrates all realms, illuminating even the most hidden—how could there be any obstruction? The comparison is made to help those who might not grasp the meaning directly."*

**Master Guan** observed:
*"Human nature is inherently luminous, yet when the **Primordial Spirit** strays from its master, obstructions arise. Sometimes one hears without seeing, sees without hearing, knows without speaking, or speaks without knowing. Sometimes one’s perception is clouded between self and others, or confused between past and present—this is the failure of the **Six Perfections**."*

*"If one penetrates the **Nature and Command**, and the **Primordial Spirit** governs its rightful place, then one’s illumination will encompass both heaven and humanity, revealing all within and without. The **Jade Reservoir**, the **Dan Platform**, the **Yellow Court**, and the **Mystic Domain**—these are the original sites of the body’s spirits, where the **Celestial Enclosure** naturally shines. All is illuminated without hindrance, just as **crystal and glass** reveal all without concealment."*

*"Indeed, the **Way** is inherently luminous, yet clarity is not easily attained. One must not be deceived by what is not yet known, nor confused by what is already known. Neither too early nor too late—true awakening is most difficult. If one can emulate the Jade Sovereign, observing the opportune moment to manifest light and renewing it daily without ceasing, then the **Great Illumination** will never dim, and the **Way** will endure."*

---

**Divine Prowess (Fourth Chapter)**

The **Sages of the Ten Directions**, riding upon **Five-Colored Jewel Wheels**, **Lingyu Spotted Jade Chariots**, **Nine-Colored Mystic Dragons**, and **Ten-Sublime Feathered Canopies**, arrived in procession.

**Master Lei Zu** noted:
*"The **Ten Directions** encompass the four cardinal points, the four diagonal corners, and the realms above and below. The **Sages** are the divine and holy assemblies of the ten directions."*

*"Witnessing the Jade Sovereign’s radiant light, they ascended their **Five-Colored** jewel-wheeled carriages, **Lingyu** jade chariots, **spotted emerald** banners, **Nine-Colored** mystic dragons, and **Ten-Sublime** feathered canopies."*

**Master Bai Yutian** elaborated:
*"The **Five Colors** are **blue, yellow, red, white, and black**. **Wheels** are the dual wheels of a chariot. **Chariot** refers to the vehicle itself. **Banner** is the collective term for imperial processional standards. The **Nine Colors** are **blue, red, yellow, white, black, purple, green, the Supreme Mystic hue, and the Golden-Luminous hue**. The **Mystic Dragon** bears the dragon’s form and light but no corporeal frame. **Ten-Sublime** means surpassing all extremes—divine and wondrous, like the feathered canopies of auspicious phoenixes and cranes."*

*"The **Scriptures** state: **Feathered Canopy** refers to a high-stemmed feathered fan. Another account says that when the divine and holy emperors travel, they bear **auspicious feathered standards** as their canopy. The latter explanation is more profound."*

**Master Guan** reflected:
*"Humans, endowed with the **Primordial Spirits** of the **Five Phases**—metal, wood, water, fire, and earth—each possess their own **treasures**. When the **Dao** is perfected, these treasures attend the **Law-Vehicle**. If one can silently pay homage to the **Heavenly Sovereign**, imitating the celestial order, then within one’s body, the spirits gather, and the **Rectified Qi** manifests in splendor. The **Jewel Wheels**, the **Lingyu True Chariots**, the **Emerald Banners**, the **Nine-Qi Mystic-Transformed Dragons**, and the **Ten-Sublime Unmatched Feathered Canopies**—these were all within one’s own person. Why should they belong only to the celestial and divine?"*

*"Alas, only the truly enlightened understand this."*

---

**Divine Prowess (Fifth Chapter)**

With **Qilin dancing** and **phoenixes singing**, their **harmonious hymns** resounded—**Divine Consorts** scattering **jewel blossoms**, **Golden Boys** wafting **auspicious mists**, reciting **profound hymns** as they floated through the void.

**Master Xu Qing Tian Shi** described:
*"As the **Sages** proceeded, the **Qilin** led in dance, and the **Auspicious Phoenix** harmonized in song, their melodious cries blending in perfect rhythm. The **Celestial Consorts** scattered **jewel flowers**, while the attending **Golden Boys** emitted **auspicious mists**. They chanted **profound hymns**, guarding the divine procession as they floated through the empty heavens toward the **Imperial Capital**."*

**The Ten-Direction Assembly** remarked:
*"When the divine emperors journey, **Spirit Boys** and **Flower-Gathering Maidens** sing in attendance, while the **Qilin** dances and the **Phoenix** sings, imitating the **Qilin’s** and **Phoenix’s** movements. Hence, it is said: *‘Their hymns resound in harmony.*’ This interpretation is overly forced."*

*"The divine procession includes **Qilin** and **Phoenixes**, akin to the **celestial steeds** that accompany the Emperor today. Moreover, the **Scriptures** state: *‘When the Heavenly Emperor travels, dragons soar and phoenixes dance.’* This reflects the **Supreme Harmony** of the celestial scene."*

*"It is also said: *‘Dragons and leopards long howl in the mountains and forests,’*—this is the **harmonious hymn** of the true **Qilin** and **Phoenix**. Otherwise, why would the **Sage Emperor Shun** compose music on **Qishan Mountain**, summoning the **Phoenix’s** rites and causing all beasts to dance?"*

*"Examining the **Scriptures** with this in mind, the earlier explanation is correct."*

「My humble view holds: When a person cultivates the Dao, silently aligning with the Imperial Will, honoring the Primordial Sovereign, the body embodies **Supreme Harmony**. The **Heavenly Resonance** sings in response, the **Mysterious Veins** settle in ease, and the demeanor is as refined as the **Qilin’s** dance or the **Luan-Feng’s** song—**séng-séng**, a joy to behold.

The **Yang Essence** radiates in splendor, the **Yin Luster** reveals itself in bloom, as though the **Divine Consorts** scatter flowers and the **Golden Boys** waft incense. The **Secret Music** and **Mysterious Melodies** are the **Heavenly-Human Praises**, the **Piercing Chapters**, resonating with the **Primordial Spirit**. It is as if one rides the void on the wind—this too is the **Holy Assembly** ascending in midair to the Imperial Gate.

This is the shared essence of all, yet only those of resolve may verify it.

**Chapter on Divine Penetration (Section 1):**
At this time, the **Brahman-Heavens**, all **Golden Immortals**, **Great Vehicle Bodhisattvas**, the **Fourfold Hosts**, and the **Eight Divisions**—bathed in this radiance—ascend upon **golden, jade, and flying-cloud palanquins**, their **Nine Haloed Auras** scattering wondrous brilliance. They gather in **Celestial Celebration**, the **Three Celestial Lights** exhaling fragrance, **Eightfold Harmonies** swirling in incense, circling the Dao’s path. A shower of **Wondrous Flowers** descends like clouds, covering the assembly before them.

**Zi Fang** expounds: At this time, all **Brahman-Heavens**, the **Enlightened Golden Immortals**, the **Great Awakened Ones** who have grasped the **True Great Vehicle Path**, the **Fourfold Hosts** of **celestial generals, male and female deities**, and the **Eight Divisions of Heavenly Beings**—bathed in this luminous glow—ascend upon **golden-hued, jade-carved palanquins borne by flying clouds**, adorned in **Nine-Haloed Robes**, their **Mysterious Scenery** effulgent. They celebrate the **Auspicious Sky**, the **Fourfold Gatherings**—the **Celestial Assembly of Merit**, the **Divine Assembly of Felicity**, the **Assembly of Timely Convergence**, and the **Assembly of Fated Alignment**—not solely the gathering of the **Fourfold Hosts**. The **Eightfold Harmonies** swirl around the Dao’s path, the **Holy Assembly** circling in reverence, and the **Wondrous Flowers**, like clouds descending, entirely cover the grand assembly. Or it may be said that the **Holy Hosts descend like clouds**, though this is overly forced.

**Ma Gu** elucidates:
- **Brahman-Heavens**: The **Supreme Precious Forest**, the **Jade Palaces** unseen in the mundane world, their hidden mysteries unfathomable. Hence, they are called **Brahman-Heavens**.
- **Golden Immortals**: Immortals of **Unbreakable Gold**.
- **Great Vehicle Bodhisattvas**: Such as **Guanyin the Great Sage** and others.
- **Fourfold Hosts**: **Immortal Hosts**, **General Hosts**, **Male Deities**, and **Female Deities**. Or it may include **Celestial Deities and Demons**, all encompassing. It does not refer to **secular monks and nuns**. For mortal bodies cannot easily ascend to the heavens, hence these four are not mentioned.
- **Eight Divisions**:
  - **Divine Division** (神部),
  - **General Division** (将部),
  - **Celestial Human and Heavenly Laborers Division** (天人天丁部),
  - **Vajra Division** (金刚部),
  - **Dragon King Division** (龙王部),
  - **Night-Light Female Attendants Division** (夜光女使部),
  - **Asura Division** (修罗部),
  - **Rākṣasa Division** (夜叉部).

- **Nine Haloes**: **Emerald Halo**, **Rainbow Halo**, **Purple Halo**, **Crimson Halo**, **Cloud Halo**, **Mist Halo**, **Auspicious Light Halo**, **Luminous Splendor Halo**, and **Universal Treasure Halo**. The **Nine-Colored Mysterious Light** flows with this wondrous scene—this is the radiance of their **Divine Robes**, though it may also signify the **Mysterious Comeliness** of their forms, not solely the garments they wear.
- **Celestial Celebration**: A **Joyous Day**, or the **Celebration of the Divine Sky**.
- **Fourfold Gatherings**: The **Assembly of Celestial Merit**, the **Assembly of Divine Felicity**, the **Assembly of Timely Convergence**, and the **Assembly of Fated Alignment**. Not solely the gathering of the **Fourfold Hosts**.
- **Circling the Dao’s path**: The **Eightfold Harmonies** swirling in reverence, or the **Holy Assembly** circling in reverence.
- **Like clouds descending, covering the assembly**: The **Wondrous Flowers** descending like clouds entirely cover the assembly. Or it may be said that the **Holy Hosts descend like clouds**, though this is overly forced.

My humble view holds: The **Spirits of the Human Body** are manifold. If the **Primordial Spirit** does not govern them, the myriad spirits will not manifest their **Numinous Virtue**. Only those who cultivate the **True Way**, silently paying homage to the **True Lord**, will see the **Ten Thousand Spirits** in reverent attendance. The **Mysterious Treasury’s Light** reveals its **Hundred Wonders**, each converging in display. When the **Primordial Spirit** gathers at the fore, all **Auspicious Omens** align, like **Auspicious Clouds** covering all—then I and the heavens are as one, undivided.

**Chapter on Divine Penetration (Section 2):**
At this time, the **Imperial Light** illuminates all the **Heavens**, descending to illuminate the **Ten Directions’ Boundless Worlds**, aligning with the **Playful Metropolis** realm. All mortal realms, even those near the **Nine Heavens**, are connected and intimately linked. Even the **Boundless Worlds below**, their **mountains, ridges, valleys, and ravines**, stretch flat as the palm—**Six Directions** are near, the **Three Realms** not distant.

The **Celestial Treasures’ Pavilions and Halls** dot the mortal realm like stars, **Precious Jade and Rare Gems** arrayed in splendor along the clouded paths. **Seven-Treasured Railings** mark the boundaries, **Jade Trees and Immortal Flowers** gleam with **Jewel-Like Luster**, their **Mysterious Splendor** radiating from the **Elixir Fields**, while **Lingzhi mushrooms and sacred grasses** spread in lush coverage.

**The True Person of Heaven** declares: At this time, the **Jade Emperor’s Light** shines upon the **Thirty-Six Heavens of this world** and the **Three Thousand Great Realms of the Heavens**, descending to illuminate all the **Boundless Worlds of the Ten Directions**, all rendered luminous, identical to the **Playful Metropolis** where the Jade Emperor resides. All mortal realms within these **Dharma Realms**, bathed in this light, face no obstruction—even those near the **Nine Solar Transformations of Heaven**. The **Heavens, Earth, and Mortal Realms** are interconnected, intimately linked. Even the **Boundless Worlds below**, with their towering mountains, jagged ridges, murky valleys, and ravines, stretch flat as the palm. The **Six Directions** are intimately connected, the **Three Pure Realms** not distant.

The **Heavenly Treasures’ Pavilions and Halls** appear in the mortal realm like stars, **Precious Jade and Rare Gems** arranged in splendor along the clouded thoroughfares. **Seven-Treasured Railings** demarcate the paths, **Jade-Branched Treasure Trees** and **Immortal Wondrous Flowers** gleam with **Jewel-Like Luster**, their **Mysterious Splendor** radiating from the **Elixir Fields**, while **Lingzhi mushrooms and sacred grasses** spread in lush, continuous coverage.

**Shi Xing’s Annotation on *Lin Kao*:** The **Human Sovereign’s** dwelling is called the **Capital**. The **Jade Emperor’s** abode surpasses all heavens, unseen by the world, hence **Playful Metropolis**. Normally, the **Heavens are clear and the Earth is murky**, the **Divine and the Mortal** disconnected—this is not intimacy. But when the **Imperial Light** shines through, the **Divine Mechanisms** link in wonder, and thus the **Heavens and Mortals** connect, growing intimate.

**Nine Heavens**: The **Nine Upper Realms of the Thirty-Six Heavens**, not merely nine.

The mountains rise high and grand—thus they are called mountains.
**Ling** are great hills, **mounds** the vast mounds.
**Pō** refers to uneven land, **bǎn** the jagged ridges of mountains.
Deep and long is called a **gully**.
Mountains flanking water are **ravines**.
Where water flows is a **stream**.
A great void in the mountain is a **valley**.
**Miǎn** means level and flat.
The earth, with its mountains, waters, valleys, and ravines, is inherently uneven.
Yet when the **Imperial Light** covers and illuminates, its wondrous intent permeates, making all worlds’ lands level.

**Qióng** is fine stone; **guī** refers to jade-like gems.
When they cluster in profusion, they are called **arrayed**.
**Yúnqú** are the celestial pathways at the heavens’ summit.
Horizontal barriers are called **rails**; vertical ones, **screens**—just as the world’s defenses are arranged.
**Chén** is the radiant brilliance of flowers.
**Zhūbǎo** are true pearls and gems.
**Dāntián** is the **Elixir Field**, the sacred **Dan Platform** of the **Playful Metropolis**.

**Shi Xing’s Annotation:** The human body contains **Heaven and Earth**; the **Yin and Yang** essence remains ununited, so the upper and lower are distant and estranged. But when the **Primordial Spirit** commands the **Light**, the **Heavenly Radiance** blazes forth, and **Earth-Heaven harmony** prevails, the high and low bend in accord, all drawing near in wondrous unity. The treasures inherent in the body, revealed in divine splendor, differ not from those above. The **Elixir Field**, where the **Spirit** resides, displays marvelous scenes—sacred grasses and **Lingzhi** flourish in lush abundance, while **Jewel-Like Flowers** bloom without need for distant seeking.

**Chapter on Divine Transformation:**
At that time, all in the lower realms see the **Heavenly Strings’** wondrous music from the **Pinjiao Heavens**, revolving with the **Imperial Light**, naturally resounding in harmony. They also see **Luan cranes** singing, **Ling phoenixes** harmonizing, their cries rising in rhythmic response; **Xuan dragons** dance, **Ling unicorns** coil, soaring and circling at the celestial summit. The **Heavenly Treasure Flowers** scatter and drift, filling every path.

Then, both **commoners and sages** are astonished, the hidden and dark illuminated. **Heavenly beings and mortals** rejoice and leap in delight. Even the unenlightened and **Dao-seekers** ascend, gazing upward at the **Effulgent Jewel Platforms** of countless **kalpas**, downward at the **Purple Clouds** veiling the **Mile-Cloth Boundaries**. All beings in these worlds attain **Dao-qi transformation**—the aged with wrinkled faces rejuvenate, their hair turning **deep indigo**, their complexions **crimson**. The young and vigorous, the infants, grow ever more radiant, their forms luminous and flawless. All sufferings vanish, all are liberated, serene and joyous. Across the land, songs of praise celebrate the **Great Peace**.

The **Emperor of Eternal Life** declared:
When the **Imperial Light** shines universally, all beneath the heavens see the **Heavenly Strings’** secret melodies from the **Pinjiao Heavens**, revolving with the **Imperial Light**, their sounds naturally resonant. They also see **Luan cranes** singing, **Ling phoenixes** harmonizing, their movements rhythmic and precise; **Xuan dragons** dance, **Ling unicorns** spiral, soaring and circling at the celestial summit. The **Heavenly Treasure Flowers** scatter and drift, filling every path.

At this moment, both **commoners and sages** are astonished, the hidden and dark illuminated. **Heavenly beings and mortals** rejoice and leap in delight. Even the unenlightened and **Dao-seekers** ascend, gazing upward at the **Effulgent Jewel Platforms** of countless **kalpas**, downward at the **Purple Clouds** veiling the **Mile-Cloth Boundaries**. All beings in these worlds attain **Dao-qi transformation**—the aged with wrinkled faces rejuvenate, their hair turning **deep indigo**, their complexions **crimson**. The young and vigorous, the infants, grow ever more radiant, their forms luminous and flawless. All sufferings vanish; the **Three Thousand Great Realms**, old and young alike, are all liberated, serene, and joyous. Across the land, songs of praise celebrate the **Great Peace**.

**Lei Men’s Envoy** said:
The **Heavenly Strings’** music is **gold**, the first of the **Eight Sounds**. Its **Dharma-tones** are **primordial gold**, uncorrupted. All harmonies blend without discord, the essence of **sound and rhythm**. Some say it is **naturally attuned**, a sound the world rarely hears—thus, **Pinjiao**. Others say the **Great Constructor** wields the **Great Balance**, and **Dao-transformation** flows naturally in **Great Harmony**; the **Heavenly Music’s** marvel is the **Great Constructor’s** work—hence, **Pinjiao**.

**Yǒngyuè huānxīn**—to leap and dance in joy, hands and feet moving in delight.
**Rèn** means **eight chi** (a measure of height).
The **Heavenly Jewel Platforms** endure through countless **kalpas**, unwearable—thus, **Effulgent Kalpa-Platforms**.
**Yǎnguān** is to lift one’s gaze; **fǔmiǎn** to lower one’s head and look.
**Zǐyún míluó**—the **Yellow-Lao Treasure Realm**—not merely what is seen beneath the **Jewel Platforms**, but also the **comprehensive vision** of ascent and descent.

**Gàn** is a deep **indigo** tinged with **crimson**; **gànfà** is what is now called **green temples**.

**Shi Xing’s Annotation:** The human body holds **Yin and Yang**; the **upper qi** is pure, the **lower qi** turbid. If the **qi** is stagnant and unharmonized, the **upper** remains unseen and unheard, leading to decay, weakness, and exhaustion—thus, the breath fades.

But when one aligns with the **Great Dao**, the **Primordial Secret** is revealed, the **Luminous Marvel** shines, and the **True Sounds** and **True Transformations** are heard and seen. The **Pinjiao melodies**, the **Ling phoenixes and cranes**, the **Xuan dragons and unicorns**—all display their wonders. **Jewel Flowers** drift in splendor, filling the world with beauty. The **Yin and Yang qi** harmonize in perfection, the **Spirit** astonished. All darkness merges into light, the upper and lower in perfect accord—thus, the **Heavenly beings and mortals** leap and dance in joy.

The **Yin** dissipates and returns; the **wondrous intent** ascends to the **Mystic**. Thus, even the **commoners and Dao-seekers** all ascend. Gazing upward at the **Jade Jewel Platforms**, downward at the **Boundless Mystic Realm**, the land is rich, the people at peace, the **qi** harmonized, the **Spirit** serene. The weak grow strong, the stagnant flow freely; the deficient become abundant. **Tendons and marrow** are transformed, **Great Harmony** preserved. The body thrives in perfect balance, rejoicing in this **wondrous transformation**.

The aged return to youth, the young grow ever more radiant—
the world sings in joy of the **Heavenly Emperor’s** virtue and **Great Harmony**!

Ah, this is the true **dharma**! The enlightened taste its sweetness.

At that time, the **Divine Perfections** manifest in nine chapters:
the **Mystic Wind** billows far and wide,
the **Ten Thousand Qi** (*wànqì*) surge with **Heavenly Grace**,
**Heaven trembles** and the earth **splits**—
**dry bones reanimate**, drowned corpses rise with **flying souls**,
all regaining their forms.

The **Yin** realm of **Yùdū** (*酆都*), encircled by iron walls,
its endless night of **Nine Abysses** (*jiǔyōu*)—
at that moment, all is shattered.
**Suffering souls** of the **Hell Realms** (*dìyù*) are reborn in **Pure Lands** (*zhūtian*).
The torments of **Three Evil Paths** (*sān’è dào*)—
**Hell, Hungry Ghosts** (*èguǐ*), and **Animal Realm** (*chùshēng*)—
are all dissolved.

Then, the countless guilty,
by this **radiant virtue** and **Dao-light** (*dàoguāng*),
are born anew in the **Ten Directions’ Great Celestial Palaces**.

**Wei Boyang** says:
When the world rejoices in **Great Harmony**,
the **Heavenly Emperor’s** virtue and **Mystic Wind** billow far,
the **Wondrous Qi** (*miàohuà wànqì*) surges,
and **Heavenly Grace** spreads.

**Heaven’s** **Yang** vitality flourishes, vigorous and robust—
**Heaven trembles** in its **Mystic Vehicle** (*xiányú*).
**Earth’s** **Yin** opens to **Great Destiny** (*chéngyùn*), gentle and yielding—
**Earth splits** in its **Soulful Depths** (*língyōu*).

**Dried bones** return to life, not merely **revived** (*jiǎgǔ zàiqǐ*),
and **drowned corpses** (*chénshī*)—
those whose **souls** have fled and **forms** decayed—
awaken to **Dao**, knowing the **True**, and **Yang** renews their bones.
Among mortals, these are the **Immortal Ones** (*rénzhōng zhī xiān*), whose bones regrow.

The **soul** (*pò*) in the living body
delights in death, feasting on sacrifices,
yet if one does not **realize the Dao** (*bù míngdào*),
**earthly attachments** (*chénshí*) bind them,
**Spirit** departs with the body, **souls** vanish and **soul-essence** (*pòjīng*) scatters.
Some cling to their own illusions,
others fall into **karmic prisons** (*yuànyù*).
When **soul-essence** rises and **fantasies** dissolve,
evil **karmic residues** (*èniè*) flee with the **soul**.

Yet the **Yin** realm of **Yùdū** (*tiěwéi Yùdū*), its iron walls unyielding,
all is broken by the **Heavenly Emperor’s** **Mystic Light** (*yùdū zhēnguāng*).
Where no **Heavenly Light** penetrates,
in the endless night of **Nine Abysses** (*jiǔyōu hēiyù*),
all is rent asunder by radiance.
The **Yin** realm’s iron walls collapse instantly—
**suffering souls** ascend to **Heaven**,
the torments of the **Three Evil Paths** dissolved.

Then, the guilty who receive this **radiant virtue**,
leaning on this **Dao-power** (*dàoli*),
are born anew in the **Ten Directions’ Great Celestial Palaces**.

For mortals in this world,
this is a treasure to ponder.

The **Divine Perfections** unfold in ten chapters:
At that time, the **Heavenly Emperor** divides His **Body of Law** (*fǎshēn*),
pervading all the **Great Celestial Palaces** (*dàtian gōng*).
Each palace naturally manifests—
**white jade** as the capital (*jīng*),
**gold** as the gates (*què*),
the **Seven Treasures’ Mystic Gardens** (*qībǎo xuányuàn*) resplendent with the **Great Light Hall** (*dàguāngmíng diàn*), its **radiant seat** (*guāngmíng zuò*) gleaming.
**Banners and flags** (*chuángjié fānshǎng*) unfurl,
**rare treasures and marvelous flowers** adorn every place.

Then, the **Heavenly Emperor** with His divided **Body of Law**,
throughout these realms—
in the **white jade capital** (*báiyù jīngzhōng*),
within the **golden gates** (*huángjīn quètíng*),
upon the **Seven Treasures’ Mystic Gardens** (*qībǎo zhuāngyán xuányuàn*),
all as He abides—
universally proclaims the **path of purity and liberation**.

**Zhōnglí Shìjūn** (*钟离帝君*) says:
When the **Great Light** is unleashed,
the **Heavenly Emperor** divides and manifests His **Body of Law**,
reaching all the **Great Celestial Palaces**.
Each palace naturally reveals itself—
**white jade capital**, **golden gates**,
the **Seven Treasures’** adorned **Mystic Gardens** (*qībǎo zhuāngyán xuányuàn*),
all as the **Heavenly Emperor’s** own dwelling.

The **Great Light’s Mystic Hall** (*Dàguāngmíng Xuándiàn*), fully adorned with the **Great Light’s Treasure Seat** (*Dàguāngmíng bǎozuò*), wields the **Mystic Law Banner** (*Xuánhuī fǎchuāng*), its **auspicious canopy** (*jiéyān huágài*) and **divine pavilions** (*fánshì*) unfurled—
with **exquisite celestial treasures** and **marvelous heavenly flowers**,
pervading all the **Great Celestial Palaces** (*Zhōngdà Tiānyōng*).

At that time, the **Heavenly Emperor** manifests His **wondrously divided Body of Law** (*miàofèn zhī shēn*), abiding throughout all the **Great Celestial Palaces**.
His **divine transformation** (*shénhuà*) fills the **White Jade Capital** (*Yùjīng*), the **Golden Gates** (*Jīnquè*), and the **Seven Treasures’ Mystic Gardens** (*Qībǎo Xuányuàn*).
He ascends the **Great Light’s Hall** (*Dàguāngmíng Diàn*) and takes His place upon the **Treasure Seat of Light** (*Guāngmíng Zuò*).
All the **celestial deities** (*zhūshén*) seated there are radiant with **divine light**.

The **Primordial Beginning Heavenly Emperor** (*Yuànshǐ Yùdì*) manifests the **Treasure Seat of Law** (*Fǎbǎo Zuò*).
Its light is most wondrous, boundless in grandeur,
ineffable in divinity, surpassing all measure—
exceeding even the **Buddhist Law King’s Seat** (*Fójiā fǎwáng zuò*).
Therefore, the **Heavenly Emperor**, in His **divinized Body of Law** (*huàshēn*), ascends this seat
to universally proclaim across the **Ten Directions** (*shífāng*)
the **true pure** (*zhēnqīng*) and **true clean** (*zhēnqìng*) **path of awakening and transcendence** (*wùjiě chāotuō zhī dào*).

**Manifestation** (*yǎn*)—
**manifestation and illumination** (*yǎnmíng*), **setting forth its meaning** (*chén qí yì*).

**Limited Perspective** (*Guǎnjiàn*) says:
The **Primordial Spirit** (*yuánshén*) of humankind—
**spiritually penetrating**, unrestrained,
reaching everywhere without hindrance—
is fundamentally akin to the **Heavenly Emperor’s wondrous transformation** (*miàohuà*).
The **Purple Treasury** (*Zǐfǔ*) and **Elixir Platform** (*Dāntái*)—
are fundamentally the same as the **celestial halls of the deities** (*shén gōng*).
The **Auspicious Reishi** (*Ruìzhī*) and **Numinous Medicines** (*Língyào*)—
are fundamentally the same as the **heavenly marvelous flowers** (*tiānshàng qíhuā*).

Yet, humans are ensnared by worldly gains (*shìlì*),
their **Primordial Spirit** (*yuánshén*) losing its master (*shǐzhǔ*).
Thus, they cannot **circulate freely and penetrate thoroughly** (*zhōuliú chègòu*),
**manifesting numinous power wherever they touch** (*chùchù chénglíng*).
They forfeit their **true purity and tranquility** (*qīngjìng zhēn*), unable to attain the **path of liberation** (*jiětuō zhī dào*).

If one **preserves the True** (*bǎozhēn hé dào*) and **reverently honors the Divine Sovereign** (*mòlǐ shénwáng*),
then **spiritual movement becomes unrestrained** (*língyùn pǔtōng*),
pervading the entire body, filling all space—
just as the **Heavenly Emperor’s divided Body of Law** (*fènshēn*) fills the **Great Celestial Palaces**.

When **the mortal form attains marvelous transformation** (*fánshēn dámiào*),
**exquisite treasures manifest naturally** (*zhìbǎo chéngqí*),
the **Pearl Towers** (*Zhūlóu*), **Treasure Halls** (*Bǎodiàn*), **Jade Palaces** (*Qiónggōng*), and **Yao Platforms** (*Yáotái*)—
these are the **White Jade Capital**, the **Golden Gates**, and the **Seven Treasures’ Mystic Gardens** (*Qībǎo Xuányuàn*) of heaven.

The **Divine Halls** (*Shén gōng*) and **Elixir Platforms** (*Dāntái*)—
these are the **Great Light’s Hall** (*Dàguāngmíng Diàn*) and the **Treasure Seat of Light** (*Guāngmíng Zuò*).

When **qi is harmonized** (*qì hé*) and **pulses are unobstructed** (*mài chàng*),
**divine light moves** (*guāng dòng*) and **celestial clouds rise** (*xiá yáng*),
this is the **Mystic Law Banner**, the **auspicious canopy**, and the **divine pavilions** (*fǎchuāng jiéyān fánshì*).

The **numinous growth of sacred herbs** (*shénzhī zhī xiù*)—
again, these are the **heavenly marvelous flowers** (*tiānshàng qíhuā*).

When the **Primordial Spirit** (*yuánshén*) **ascends in divine power** (*shén yù*) and **governs the Elixir Platform** (*zhǎi dāntái*),
**spreading luminous secrets** (*fūlíng xiǎnmì*)—
this is the **Heavenly Emperor’s divided Body of Law** (*fènshēn*), ascending simultaneously to each seat and proclaiming the **Law** (*shuōfǎ*).

My **true nature** (*zhēnxìng*)—
**enduring through kalpas** (*lìjiè*) without decay,
**undual and unadulterated** (*wú'èr wúzá*),
**unrestrained and unobstructed** (*wújū wújìan*),
**fundamentally pure and undefiled** (*běn qīngjìng bùrǎn*),
**naturally liberated** (*tuōluò zìrán*),
**greatly illuminated without dimness** (*dàmíng bùmèi*)—

can **ascend in divine power** (*shén yù*) and **spread luminous secrets** (*fūlíng xiǎnmì*),
then **every part of my body becomes mystically transformed** (*biàn yīshēn jiē xuánhuà*).
**Circulating through the Three Thousand Worlds** (*zhōu sāniàn wújū wǒ*), **comprehending causality** (*míngliǎo yīnyuán*),
**unveiling ultimate reality** (*bùmèi shíjì*),
**radiant throughout** (*biǎolǐ yíngchè*),
**exhausting divine mysteries** (*qióngshén dáhuà*)—
this is the **Heavenly Emperor’s teaching of liberation and transcendence** (*jiětuō qīngjìng zhī dào*), **illuminating all worlds** (*jiàohuà gé shìjiè*).

**Those who attain** (*Dá zhě*) **taste this meaning** (*wèi zhī*), **naturally recognize its truth** (*zì shí cǐ yì*).

**Eleven Chapters on Divine Penetration** (*Shéntōng Pǐn Shíyī Zhāng*):

At that time, the **Heavenly Emperor**, in His **divinized Body of Law** (*huàshēn*), manifests throughout all the **Great Celestial Palaces**.
He is attended by **infinite numbers of Heavenly True Ones** (*Wújiànliàng Tiānshàng Zhūzhēn Dàsì*), **Sages of Marvelous Practice** (*miàoxíng zhēnrén*), **Numinous Consorts and Jade Maidens** (*língfēi yùnǚ*), who stand and array themselves at His sides.

These **Jade Maidens** (*Qǐyùnǚ*)—
their **complexion and bearing** (*yánróng xiōngróng*) are **exquisitely beautiful** (*mèimiào*),
**upright and adorned** (*duānlì qí tè*), **marvelously unique** (*qíhuā xiāozé*).
With **heavenly treasures and divine marvels** (*tiānzhēn shényì zhībǎo*), they **adorn the Emperor’s sacred form** (*zhuāngyán shēnxiàng*).
Their **speech and voice** (*yányīn*) are **clear and penetrating** (*qīngmíng tōngchè*), **pleasing to all** (*zhòngsuǒ lèwén*).

These **Jade Maidens**—
their bodies further emit **subtle, numinous, and liberating fragrances** (*wēimiào jiětuō zìrán zhīxiāng*).
This fragrance is **aromatic and fragrant** (*fēnfú yùfú*), pervading all the **heavenly realms of supreme bliss** (*jiéshénmiào kuàilè zhī jìngtǔ*)
and all the **great earthly worlds of auspicious gatherings** (*zhōngdà dì shìjiè yīqiè fúhuì zhī chù*).

**Queen Mother of the West** (*Wángmǔ*) says:
At that time, the **Heavenly Emperor**, in His **divinized Body of Law** (*huàshēn*), manifests throughout all the **Great Celestial Palaces**.
He is attended by **infinite numbers of Heavenly True Ones** (*Wújìnliàng Tiānshàng Zhūzhēn Shéntōng Dàsì*), **Sages of Marvelous Practice and Divine Transformation** (*língyùn biànhuà miàoxíng zhuāngyán zhēnrén*), **Numinous Consorts** (*língtōng xiānfēi*), and **Protecting Saints’ Jade Maidens** (*hùshèng yùnǚ*), who stand and array themselves at His sides.

These **Jade Maidens**—
their **visage and form** (*yánmiàn xíngróng*) are **beautiful and surpassingly unique** (*xiōuměi qímiào duānzhèng huálì shénqí tèmài*).
With **heavenly treasures and divine marvels** (*tiānzhēn shényì zhībǎo*), they **adorn the Emperor’s sacred form** (*zhuāngyán shēnxiàng*).
Their **speech and voice** (*yányīn yīnshēng*) are **clear and penetrating** (*qīngmíng tōngchè*), **most pleasing to all** (*dàzhòng suǒ lè tīngwén*).
Their bodies further emit **subtle, numinous, and liberating fragrances** (*Xuánwēi shénmiào dàjiětuō zìrán zhī xīnxiāng*).
This fragrance is **aromatic and fragrant** (*fēnfú yùfú*), pervading all the **heavenly realms of supreme bliss** (*zhōng Tiānyōng jíshénmiào kuàilè zhī jìngtǔ*)
and all the **great earthly worlds of auspicious gatherings** (*bìng biànjí zhōngdà dì shìjiè yīqiè fúhuì zhī chù*).

**Examining the Meaning** (*Kǎoyì yún*) says:
**Marvelous Practice** (*Miàoxíng*)—
humans possess **various virtues** (*zhūshàn*), yet they do not **forcefully contrive** (*bù jiǎ qiángwéi*).
Their **merits and virtues** (*gōngdé*) are **exhaustless** (*bùqióng*), fundamentally arising from **naturalness** (*zìrán*) and thus becoming **True Ones** (*zhēnrén*).
Then, their **divine penetrations** (*shéntōng*) are **boundless** (*mòliàng*).
Hence, it is called **Marvelous Practice** (*miàoxíng*).

**Numinous Consorts and Jade Maidens** (*Língfēi Yùnǚ*)—
are **divine transformations** (*miàohuà*) of the **yin-dharma subtle qi** (*yīnfàn miàoqì*).
They **guard and protect the Emperor’s True Nature** (*gǒngwèi Dìzhēn*).
All **celestial maidens** (*Tiānshàng shénnǚ*) are thus named.
**Without desire or entanglement** (*wúyù wúlèi*), they differ from **demonic maidens** (*mófù*).

With **virtue and power** (*dé gōng*) both complete,
**noble, beautiful, and exalted** (*guìměi zūnlíng*),
**pure and unadulterated, forever without obstruction** (*chúnjié yǒngwú jiànzá*),
they are called **Numinous Consorts and Jade Maidens** (*Língfēi Yùnǚ*).
This is not solely referring to the **Emperor’s consort** (*Dìhòu*).

These **Jade Maidens**—
their **complexion and bearing** (*yánróng xiōngróng*) are **exquisitely beautiful** (*mèimiào*).
**Maiden** (*xiōu*)—beauty.
**Upright** (*duān*)—solemn and proper.
**Adorned** (*lì*)—luxuriant and radiant.
**Unique** (*qí*)—divinely marvelous, rarely seen.
**Surpassing** (*tè*)—transcending all beauty, **unmatched in the world** (*shìwú bǐlún*).

With **heavenly treasures adorning their sacred form** (*tiānzhēn zhuāngyán shēnxiàng*),
these **celestial maidens** (*Tiānshàng fēi*)—
**mystic light** (*Xuánguāng*) and **divine transformation** (*shénhuà*)—
**exquisite treasures adorning their form** (*miàobǎo zhuāngyán*), their **physique and bearing** (*qítǐ qíróng*)
are **unseen in the world** (*shìsuǒ wèijiàn*).

Their **speech and voice** (*yányīn*) are **clear and penetrating** (*qīngmíng tōngchè*).
**Speech** (*yán*)—speech and language.
**Voice** (*yīn*)—sound and tone.

**Clear** (*qīng*)—distinct and lucid.
**Penetrating** (*chè*)—pervasive and resonant throughout.

**Subtle and wondrous liberation** (*wéimiào jiětuō*)—natural fragrance:
The **celestial maidens** (*fēi*) attain enlightenment, achieving **great liberation** (*dà jiětuō*).
Their **mystic mechanisms** (*xuánjī*) are unfathomable, their **divine subtlety** (*shénmiào*) immeasurable.
No artificial contrivance is needed—**naturally fragrant** (*zìrán xīnxiāng*).
Yet the source of this fragrance is unknown—hence, **subtle and wondrous** (*wéimiào*).

This fragrance is **aromatic and rich** (*fēnfù*):
**Aromatic** (*fēn*)—beautiful qi spreading and dispersing.
**Rich** (*fù*)—profoundly fragrant and abundant.

It pervades all **celestial realms of supreme bliss** (*jiémào lètǔ*):
**Pervasive** (*zhōu*)—comprehensive and all-encompassing.
**Extensive** (*biàn*)—broadly manifest.
**Supreme** (*jí*)—most exalted.

In the **great celestial palaces** (*dà tiān gōng*), where **jade maidens** (*yùnǚ*) serve as **manifestations of the Jade Emperor** (*yùdì huàshēn*), this fragrance does not cease at one place but spreads throughout all **worlds and heavens**, creating **blissful realms without suffering** (*wúkǔ lètǔ*).

The **great earth** (*dàdì*)—speaking of mountains, rivers, and worlds.
A **blessed realm** (*fúchù*)—wherever there is a world, there is birth and formation, hence **blessed realm**.

Some say that through **reverence and sincere faith** (*gōngjìng jīngxìn*), one may then hear this **marvelous fragrance** (*yìxiāng*).
All worlds receive the **radiance of the Jade Emperor** (*yùdì guāng*), generating faith, and thus encounter the **celestial maidens’ wondrous fragrance** (*língfēi yùnǚ miàoxiāng*), hence **blessed realm**.
This is also correct.

All beings of the **Six Paths** (*liùdào*), upon hearing this fragrance, universally attain **enlightenment and liberation** (*kāiduò zhīhuì*).
The **Six Paths** (*liùdào*)—**heavenly path** (*tiāndào*), **human path** (*réndào*), **demonic path** (*módào*), **hellish path** (*dìyùdào*), **hungry ghost path** (*èguǐdào*), **animal path** (*chùshēngdào*).

If those in the **heavenly path** (*tiāndào*), including all celestial beings (*tiānrén*), hear this fragrance, their **five decayed and four ugly forms** (*wǔshuāi sìchǒng*) are permanently eliminated, and their **celestial blessings** (*tiānfú*) are enhanced.

If those in the **human path** (*réndào*), including kings, ministers, and common folk, hear this fragrance, they attain the **longevity bliss of humans and heavens** (*rén tiān chángshòu zhīlè*).
If their bodies perish and they transcend, they attain the **path of shell-shedding and corpse-resurrection** (*tuōké sǐjiě zhīdào*).

If those in the **demonic path** (*módào*), all demons, hear this fragrance, they find rest in celestial palaces, free from the suffering of battle and strife.

If those in the **hellish path** (*dìyùdào*), all guilty souls, hear this fragrance, they escape hell’s torments and attain the bliss of a **pure land** (*jìngtǔ*).

If those in the **hungry ghost path** (*èguǐdào*), all hungry ghosts, hear this fragrance, they become sated, free from hunger and thirst.

If those in the **animal path** (*chùshēngdào*), all suffering beasts, hear this fragrance, they escape animal suffering and attain the bliss of **wisdom and clarity** (*zhìhuì cōngmíng*).

The **Sage of Rescue from Suffering** (*Jiùkǔ Tiānzūn*) says:
All beings in the **Six Paths**, upon hearing the **celestial maidens’ natural fragrance** (*língfēi zìrán zhīxiāng*), universally receive the grace of **enlightenment and liberation** (*kāihuà bádù*).

The **Six Paths** (*liùdào*)—paths like roads, where beings undergo **cyclical rebirth** (*lúnzhuǎn*) within six realms, hence **Six Paths**.

First, the **heavenly path** (*tiāndào*): Heaven has **thirty-six names**, with the highest four heavens called **seed-citizens** (*zhǒngmín*), where **seven treasures and nine august celestial beings** reside. The **Buddhist teachings** call this the **non-regressing realm** (*bùtuì zhuǎn zhīdì*).

Below the **seed-citizens**, there are the **four exalted secret heavens** (*sìchóng mìtiān*), which the **Buddhist teachings** call the **four Brahma heavens** (*sìfàn tiān*).

Below the **exalted secret heavens**, there are the **four forgetful-form heavens** (*sìwàng xiàng tiān*), which the **Buddhist teachings** call the **four *jhāna* heavens** (*sìqián tiān*), i.e., the **formless realm** (*wúsè jiè*).

Below the **forgetful-form heavens**, there are the **eighteen heavens of the form realm** (*sèjiè shíbā tiān*).

Below the **eighteen heavens of the form realm**, there are the **six heavens of the desire realm** (*yùjiè liù tiān*).

One world contains **thirty-six heavens**, all worlds being the same.

The **four kinds of celestial citizens** (*sìzhǒng mín tiān*)—**void and wondrous existence** (*xūwú miàoyǒu*), **mystic transformation and divine spirit** (*miàohuà xuánshén*)—are **eternally uncorrupted**, inhabited only by **highest sages and true immortals**, with no celestial beings. They are not counted among the **heavenly paths**.

The **four exalted secret heavens**—**slightly defiled yet pure**, **partially transformed yet not divine**, **not yet attaining the Great Vehicle**.
Though they belong to the **human path** (*réndào*), even the **great eon** cannot spare them from decline.

The **formless realm** (*wúsè jiè*), **form realm** (*sèjiè*), and **desire realm** (*yùjiè*)—
All **celestial beings** (*tiānrén*) are **tall and majestic**, their forms like **white silver**, not dependent on sunlight or moonlight for illumination, yet **self-luminous**.
The **day-moon heavens** (*rìyuè tiān*) have beings **five *li*** in height; higher realms increase gradually, reaching **a hundred *yojanas*** in stature (*yóushù zhīgāo*), with one *yojana* being **forty *li***.

The **Dao scriptures** say: **"Exceeding the abode"** (*yúshè*), they wear **heavenly robes** (*tiān yī*) weighing **six *catty*, two *qian*, and five *fen***.
Their heads are crowned with **natural pearl diadems** (*zìrán zhūguān*), their eyes do not blink (*mù bù shùn*), their heads do not bow (*tóu bù fǔ*), they stand without leaning (*lì bù yǐ*), their eyes shed no tears (*yǎn wú lèi*), and their bodies know no fatigue (*shēn wú kùnpi*).
If they fail to awaken to the **Great Vehicle** (*dàchéng*), when their **celestial blessings** (*tiānfú*) are exhausted, their **pearl diadems shatter**, their eyes weep in rain (*mù shùn yǔ lèi*), their bodies bend and weary (*shēn qū xíng pi*), and the **five decays and four ugly forms** (*wǔshuāi sìchǒng*) manifest.

If one receives the **natural fragrance** (*zìrán xiāng*) of the Dao, with **sincere faith** (*jīngxìn*) and **reverent devotion** (*gōngjìng*), and awakens to its **subtle and wondrous origin** (*miào xiāng zhī yóu*), they will **suddenly attain harmony** (*dùn qì dàdào*) with the Great Way, not needing to seek this fragrance from without, and thus achieve **enlightenment** (*liáo wò*). This is called **the able hearer** (*néng wén*).

The **five decays and four ugly forms** (*wǔshuāi sìchǒng*) are **permanently eliminated** (*yǒng dé xiāochú*). **永** (*yǒng*) means **eternal** (*eternal*). **终** (*zhōng*) means **final** (*final*). When one is **finally freed** (*zhōng miǎn*) from the suffering of decay and ugliness, their **celestial blessings** (*tiānfú*) are **turned to increase** (*zhuǎn zēng*). **转转进益** (*zhuǎn zhuǎn jìn yì*), their blessings grow without bound—**never exhausted** (*bù tuì jìn*).

Human paths vary: there are **youth and age, male and female** (*yīnyáng lǎoshào*), there are **noble and ignoble, poor and rich** (*guìbiàn pínfù*), and there are **sages and fools, wise and dull** (*shèngxián zhìyú*). Without attaining the Great Way, their **lifespan is limited** (*shòu suàn bù cháng*), and death comes **with great difficulty** (*sǐ zhī shèn nán*). Their **corpse cannot transform** (*shī bù néng huà*).

In every realm, **emperors, ministers, and all officials—great and small—along with the countless common people** (*zǎoshì zhūmín*). A **million** (*qiān wàn*) is called a **myriad** (*zǎo*), and **庶** (*shì*) means **the masses** (*the masses*). **兆庶** (*zǎoshì*) refers to all people, **extreme in number** (*extreme in number*).

If one can receive the **natural fragrance** (*zìrán xiāng*) and **awaken to the Great Way** (*liáo wò dàdào*), they will also **skillfully perceive its refined subtlety** (*xīn miào*), and thus attain the **joy of boundless longevity** (*wú guǎi chángshòu zhī lè*) in the Dao of humans and heavens. Even if they perish, they will **mysteriously escape the mortal coil** (*mì miào tuō qì ké*), **transcend the body** (*shī jiě xiān huà*), and achieve **immortal transformation** (*xiān huà*).

**脱壳** (*Tuō ké*) means **to shed the physical shell**—whether through **sitting ascension** (*zuò tuō*) or **standing ascension** (*lì wáng*), or by **seizing another’s rebirth** (*tóu tāi duó shè*). **尸解** (*Shī jiě*) means **corpse dissolution**—either when **this body dies** (*cǐ yǐ sǐ*) and another **manifests in the world** (*xiǎn shēn yú shìjiān*), with both **corpse and soul departing** (*shī hún bìng qù*); or when one **feigns death and ascends** (*jiǎ sǐ ér shēng*).

For all **paths of demons** (*móudào*), the demonic kinds vary. **唂嘶啰与** (*wū sī luó yǔ*)—like the **Asuras** (*xiūluó*) and **Rakshasas** (*guǐní*)—**contend with the Heavenly Sovereign** (*tiān dì zhēng héng*), **disturbing celestial officials** (*dòu luàn tiān guān*).

All demonic paths either **delight in warfare** (*hào zhànzhēng*), **create illusions and terrors** (*zuò huàn lì*), or dwell in **restlessness and perpetual turmoil** (*jū chù bù ān, cháng wú xiūxī*). If such demons hear the **natural wondrous fragrance** (*zìrán miào xiāng*), and **awaken to the Dao’s true nature** (*néng wò dàozhēn*), then they will **abandon evil and follow righteousness** (*gǎi xié cóng zhèng*), dwell in **tranquility** (*jū chù ānrán*), and **guard their inherent stations** (*shǒu qí sù wèi*). In the **separate celestial ranks** (*tiān bié guān*), they will no longer **take pleasure in contention, disturbance, or warfare** (*lè fēn zhēng, dòu luàn zhànfá zhī kǔ*), and thus **each attains rest and respite** (*gè dé xiūxī*).

Those who suffer in **battle and war** (*dòu zhàn kǔ*)—**wounded in contention** (*dòu luàn bì shāng*), **killed in battle** (*zhànfá bì shā*)—**mutually triumph and defeat** (*hù shèng hù bài*), **becoming foes in endless cycle** (*jiāo wéi kòu chóu*)—thus it is said they suffer. **Each attains rest** (*gè dé xiūxī*), for though their **spirit does not harm demons** (*shén suī bù qīn móu*), if they are **disturbed by demons** (*wéi móu suǒ luàn*), they will **respond and subdue them** (*yìng biàn fú móu*).

Now, when these demons hear the fragrance and awaken to its subtlety, dwelling in peace without strife, their **spirit also finds no cause for action** (*shén yì wú shì*). **Spirit and demons alike are at rest** (*shén móu xī ān*), hence it is said that **each attains rest and respite** (*gè dé xiūxī*).

In all realms, the **hells** (*dìyù*)—though not limited to one name—are called **Changdu** (*Qīngdū*), **Blood Lake** (*Xuèhú*), **Blood Pass** (*Xuèxiá*), **Frigid Ice** (*Hánbīng*), **Flame Chariot** (*Huǒchē*), **Mountain of Knives** (*Dāoshān*), **Forest of Swords** (*Jiànshù*), **River of Love** (*Àihé*), **Restraining Mind** (*Zhìxīn*), **Iron Bed** (*Tiěchuáng*), **Blade of Wind** (*Fēngdāo*), **Iron Hounds** (*Tiěgǒu*), **Bronze Serpents** (*Tóngshé*), **Crucible of Boiling Iron** (*Liáo huò*), **Sawing Asunder** (*Jújiě*), **Grinding** (*Mó*), **Flaying and Picking** (*Bōtì*), **Plow of Mud** (*Ní lí*), **Tongue-Tearing** (*Bá shé*), and **thus up to the thirty-six hells** (*yǐjí sānshíliù yù*).

All **suffering souls** (*shòuzuì zhūhún*) in these hells are **inherently difficult to free** (*běn nán lí dìyù qīuxíng zhī kǔ*). If they hear this **natural fragrance** (*zìrán xiāng*), they will **awaken and transcend** (*néng liáo wò, suí dé chāotuō*), **escaping the hells’ torments** (*chūlí dìyù zhūkǔ*), and **reborn in a land of pure bliss** (*dé shēng qīngjìng lètǔ*).

For **hungry ghosts** (*èguǐ*) and **exhausted souls** (*lìjié qiónghún*) long bound in the **ghostly realm** (*guǐjí*), some have **narrow necks and swollen bellies** (*xì jǐng dà fù*), others **great heads with shrunken waists** (*shǒu dà fù xiǎo*), or **constricted throats** (*yān hóu bì sè*), or **consume charcoal and smoke** (*shí tàn yīn yān*), or **dine on molten copper** (*cān róng tóng*), or **swallow iron pellets** (*dàn tiě wán*), enduring **countless lifetimes without taste of water** (*lěi shì bù wén jiāngshuǐ*), **never encountering food** (*bù yù yǐnshí*), **starving and parched in agony** (*è nèi kě tòng*), though they **ever fret and lament** (*suī cháng yōu ào*).

In every realm, **all such hungry ghosts** (*rúshì èguǐ dào zhōng yīqiè èguǐ*)—if they hear this **natural fragrance** (*zìrán xiāng*), and **awaken to the Dao** (*néng wò dàodào*), then the **flavor of the Way fills their being** (*dào wèi chōng fù*), and they **attain satiety** (*jí dé bǎo mǎn*), **dispelling hunger and thirst** (*xiāochú jī kě*), **unblocking throat and palate** (*kāi míng hóu yān*), and **forever free from torment** (*yǒng wú è nǎo*).

For **beastly paths** (*chùshēng dào*), **all transformations—wet, dry, sluggish, or lively** (*mǎo huà shī yǒu zhuó dòng*)—are included, not just **birds and beasts** (*bù zhuān yán qín shòu*). Though **beasts are nurtured and ridden** (*chùshēng zhě suī xùyǎng yú tiān dì zhī wèn*) and **lack wisdom** (*wú yǒu zhìhuì*), their **karmic retribution is manifold and bitter** (*yèbào duō kǔ suī kǔ nán tuō*). Yet if all **beasts in every realm** (*gè shìjiè yīqiè chùshēng*) hear this **natural wondrous fragrance** (*zìrán miào xiāng*), and **awaken to the Dao** (*jí néng wò dàodào*), they will **attain this liberation** (*dé cǐ jiětuō*), their **karmic retribution exhausted** (*yèbào jí jìn*), and **escape the suffering of beasts** (*tuōlí chùshēng zhī kǔ*), attaining instead the **joy of keen wisdom** (*dé cōngmíng zhìhuì zhī lè*).

Beasts are **not without intelligence** (*chùshēng fēi wú zhì*), but they **cannot speak of the Dao** (*bù néng yán dàodào*), **cannot embody its truth** (*bù néng tǐ dàodào*), and their **forms differ, their spirits distinct** (*xíng yì shén shū*). Some are **domesticated and ridden** (*huàn yǎng chéng yù*), others **hunted and slaughtered** (*yúliè shā shí*), **falling into traps** (*tóu diàn jǐng*), **filled for the kitchen** (*chōng páochú*), **devoured raw and blood-drenched** (*rú máo yǐn xiě, pí gǔ suī jìn*), their **skins and bones consumed** (*zuì kǔ nán yán*). Hearing the fragrance, they **attain wisdom** (*jí dé zhìhuì*), all through the **Sovereign’s radiant law** (*dìguāng fǎlì yě*).

The **limited perspective** (*guǎn jiàn*) says: The **two preceding sections** (*shàng liǎng jié*) share a **single intent** (*jù yī yì*). The **original spirit** (*yuánshēn*) of the human body **oversees yin and yang** (*zǒng yù yīnyáng*), embodying the **true and wondrous conduct** (*zhēn shèng miào xíng*), the **divine consort and royal daughter** (*líng fēi wáng nǚ suī yǒu*). Within the **Great Harmony** (*tàihé*), the **spirit, qi, essence, and blood** (*shén qì jīng xuè*) all contain this **marvelous fragrance** (*jiētuō zìrán xiāng*), **liberating by nature** (*miào miào nán qióng yě*), **subtle and boundless** (*wēimiào nán qióng yě*).

When **qi is imbalanced** (*qì zhī piānzhèng*), it is **not from inherent madness or folly** (*fēi kuángyú shìfèn*), yet they too **fall into the Six Paths** (*yǒu liùdào*). Only when the **Heavenly Sovereign’s governance is unbalanced** (*tiān jūn bù tài*), are they **constrained by the Five Phases** (*wéi wǔxíng suǒ jū*); or when **thoughts are not severed** (*niàn tóu bù duàn*), **flitting and chaotic** (*fēnfēn rǎorǎo*), are they **controlled by yin and yang** (*wéi yīnyáng suǒ zhì*).

These too are **those who endure the Six Paths’ revolving torments** (*shì yě shòu liùdào lún zhuǎn zhě yě*). If one **beholds their own body’s beauty** (*dǔ jǐ shēn liùdīng yùnǚ zhī měi*), **hears the Great Harmony’s natural fragrance** (*wén tàihé jiětuō zìrán zhī xiāng*), and **comprehends the Great Way** (*míng chè dàdào*), then their **original spirit remains ever resplendent** (*shǐ yuánshēn cháng huàn*), and they **behold the Sovereign’s radiance** (*jí shǐ dǐguāng ér xiān huà*), **transcending dust and mundanity** (*yǒng tuō chén fán, bù wéi shēn jū*), and thus **forever freed from the Six Paths’ suffering** (*shì yě yǒng tuō liùdào zhī kǔ yě*).

Those who **attain** (*dá*) will **taste its meaning** (*zhī wèi yǎn*), **recognizing the two sections’ intent** (*zì shí liǎng jié zhī yì*).

**The Twelve Chapters on Spiritual Penetration** (*Shéntōng pǐn shí'èr zhāng*)
At that time, **all the assembled beings of Heavenly Retribution** (*zhūshìng tiānzuì zhūhún*), having **obtained rebirth in this Victorious Heavenly Palace** (*yuán dé shēng shì shèng tiān gōng yě*), **owing to their reception of the Compassionate Light** (*yuán dé chéng cíguāng shè shòu zhī gǔ*), **immediately awaken** (*biàn dé jiào wò*), **each clearly understanding the causes of guilt and blessing** (*gè gè míng liǎo zuìfú yīnyuán*), and **with their attendants** (*yǔ zhū quànshǔ*), they **perform celestial arts and music** (*zuò tiān jì yīn jì*), **their devotion fervent** (*qí yī qiè*). **伎** (*jì*) means **art** (*art*). Some texts read **伎** (*jì*) as **乐** (*yìng lè*).
