The **倚切** (*yī qiè*) and **渠纪切** (*qú jì qiè*) pronunciations align with **与** (*yǔ*), so **伎** (*jì*) should follow the **乐** (*lè*) meaning.
They **rejoice and come before the Sovereign** (*lè lái yì dì qián*).

「This is when all the guilty beings, each filled with sorrow, simultaneously raised their voices to speak: *"Your servants have traversed countless kalpas—both great and small—without ever seeing the Three Lights of sun, moon, and stars. We have always dwelled in the depths of darkness, plunged into the Three Evil Paths of hell, hungry ghosts, and animals, enduring endless suffering and torment."*

Now, as we have received the **Emperor’s** (*Yuánshǐ Dì*) **compassionate illumination** (*cíguāng*), **divine grace** (*mìhuà*) has transformed us into **True Fragrance** (*zhēn xiāng*), and due to the **Emperor’s boundless virtue and luminous compassion** (*Dàcí guāngmíng*) **that encompasses and guides us** (*shè shòu zhī gǔ*), we have all **awakened to the Great Dao** (*Dàdào*), **each now comprehending the profound causes of guilt and blessing** (*zuìfú yīnyuán*).

**Encompass** (*shè*), here, means **to receive, guide, and uphold** (*jiēyǐn bǎochí*). **Guide** (*shòu*), here, means **to summon the soul and spirit** (*jiēyǐn húnshén*), **inviting them to return to their true nature** (*chào zhī guīzhēn*). When the **Emperor releases His compassionate light** (*cíguāng*), it **miraculously manifests as True Fragrance** (*zhēn xiāng*), **encompassing and guiding all guilty beings** (*zuìzhòng*), who **immediately awaken** (*jiào*), **grasping their true nature** (*zhī qí suǒyǐrán*), and **penetratingly understand** (*chè tōng*).

The guilty beings, having **awakened and comprehended**, **escape the Three Evil Paths** (*sǔn qí sān èdào qù*), **each now clearly and thoroughly understanding** (*gè gè míng tōng liǎo chè*), **deeply knowing the causes of guilt and blessing** (*zuìfú yīnyuán*). **Cause** (*yīn*) refers to **root** (*fēnggēn*), meaning that **where there is cause, there is effect** (*yǒu yīn zé yǒu guǒ*). **Connection** (*yuán*) refers to **proximity** (*yóulái*), meaning that **where there is connection, there is karma** (*yǒu yuán zé yǒu yè*). Once the guilty beings **clearly understand the causes and effects of their guilt and virtue** (*zuìyè fúdé yīnguǒ yuángù*), along with their **kindred and companions** (*qīnchūn zhùshǔ*), they **perform celestial arts and wondrous music** (*tiān jì miàolè*) before the **Emperor’s throne** (*yì Dì qián*).

**Celestial arts** (*tiān jì*), when **interpreted through the term "art"** (*yì*), signifies **their perfection and boundless mastery** (*qiánwéi bùtōng*). **To come before** (*lái yì*), here, means **to arrive** (*zhì*). These are the guilty beings who have been **reborn in heaven**, each now **filled with sorrow** (*bāohán zhuó*), as they **utter their voices in lamentation** (*jù fā shēngyán*): *"Your servants, through countless kalpas past and present, have never seen the Three Lights—sun, moon, and stars—always dwelling in the gloom of darkness, fallen into the Three Evil Paths of hell, hungry ghosts, and animals, enduring much suffering and anguish."*

**To bow humbly** (*fú*), here, means **to prostrate oneself on the ground** (*jūshēn fǔfú dìxià*). **To receive** (*méng*), here, means **to accept from above and below** (*yǎngshòu yǐngbèi*). The phrase *"as we have received"* (*fú méng*) is used **to express lowly submission to the exalted** (*wēicéng yǐngzūn*), and should be understood as such. Later, when the text says *"received"* (*méng*), it follows this same convention.

The **Emperor’s compassionate light** (*cíguāng*) **permeates all with boundless wisdom** (*pùxíng dàomìàorén dé biànyì*), **allowing us to benefit greatly** (*dé biànyì*). Once this **compassionate light is released** (*fàng*), **He takes pity and rescues us** (*liánmǐn jiùbá wǒdéng*), **enabling all to be reborn in heaven** (*jiēdé shēng yú tiānshàng*). These **evil deeds and their suffering karmic retributions** (*èkǔ yèbào*) are **all eradicated and exhausted** (*xījiē chúmiè liǎojìn*), **with no lingering bonds or hindrances** (*wú zhōngxì hùliǎn*), and **all attain rebirth in the heavens** (*jiēdé wǎngshēng zhūtiān*), **paying homage to the Jade Sovereign Emperor** (*yǎngcháo Yùhuáng Dìshàng*), **each arriving at the Dao’s boundless origin** (*gè gè zhì Dàodào qiánmiàn*).

When the **reborn heavenly beings and all guilty ones** (*shēngtiān zuìzhòng*) **finish speaking these words**, they **prostrate themselves and return to their original positions** (*qǐshǒu fùguī yuánshì lì*).

**The Fool’s Reflection** (*Yú’àn*): **"Humans are born with yin and yang** (*rén bǐng yīnyáng*), **inherently the same as heaven and earth** (*yǔ tiāndì běnlái xiāngtóng*). Yet, **ensnared by desires and greed** (*nì yú lìyù*), they **defile and sink their true hearts** (*wū xiàn zhēnxīn*), **persisting in evil without repentance** (*cháng è bù quān*), and **consider the wheel of retribution** (*bàoyìng zhuánlún*) as nonexistent—**this is ignorance of the causes of guilt and blessing** (*bùzhī zuìfú yīnyuán*). Thus, **the harmony of the Dao is lost** (*miào hé zhēnyì wúyǒu*), and they are **ensnared by the mundane constraints** (*bì yú chénsú zhī gāng*), **clinging to lust, anger, delusion, and jealousy** (*tānchīn chǐmìng*), **lost in madness, sorrow, and fleeting joy** (*kuángluàn bēixǐ*), **obsessed with desires and seeking fame** (*shìyù qiúmíng*), **never realizing the true path** (*bùjiàn liǎoqī*). This is why they **always dwell in darkness** (*chángchǔ hēi’àn*), **like the beings of hell, hungry ghosts, and animals** (*rú dìyù èguǐ chùshēng zhī zài sān èdào zhōng*), **enduring torment day and night** (*zhòuyè áojiān*), **just as the guilty beings suffer greatly** (*yì yú zhūzuìzhòng duōshòu kǔnǎo yībān*).

This is the **state of those whose evil deeds are not exhausted** (*èyè bùjìn*), **bound by lingering karmic ties** (*yǒu xì hù bùdé shēngtiān*), **who cannot be reborn in heaven** (*zhī zuìzhòng*). When the **True Spirit governs** (*yuánshén yù*), **heavenly light shines forth** (*tiān guāng fā*), the **yin-qi and impure thoughts of the body** (*yīnqì zázhì èqù*) all **return to pure qi** (*shēng zhēngqì*), **ascending to the Nine Yang Realms** (*shēng jiǔyáng jìnghuì*). **Knowing the distinctions between goodness, evil, mundanity, and sainthood** (*zhī shàng è fánshèng zhī guān*), they **move swiftly with the Dao’s influence** (*jié yú yǐngxiǎng*), **and retribution becomes manifest** (*bàoyìng zhāorán*).

This is the **release of the Supreme Harmony’s rhythm** (*xì Tàihé zhī yùn*), **revealing the sacred essence** (*chéng língmì*), **and honoring the Primordial Emperor** (*lǐ Yuánhuáng*), **which is when the guilty beings, having received the Emperor’s compassionate light** (*chéng Dì cíguāng shèshòu*), **each now understand the causes of guilt and blessing** (*gè míng zuìfú yīnyuán*), **and with their kindred and companions** (*yǔ zhū quànshǔ*), **perform celestial arts and music** (*zuò tiān jì miàolè*), **coming before the Emperor’s throne** (*lái yì Dì qián*).

When **yin-qi dissipates** (*yīnqì xiāo*), **impure thoughts are forgotten** (*zázhì wàng*), **and evil paths are purified** (*èqù jìng*), **transforming evil into goodness** (*yì è wéi shàn*), **returning to spirit and fate** (*guīshén guīmìng*), **repenting and awakening to self-correction** (*huǐwù chéngchuàng*), they **know that evil deeds bring misfortune** (*zìzhī zuò è bùxiáng*). **Without awakening to the Great Dao** (*bùjiào Dàdào*), they are **like those facing a wall or sitting in a well** (*rú tóng miànqiáng zuòjǐng*), **truly seeing nothing** (*zhēng wú suǒjiàn*). **Obscured by the paths of the Three and Two** (*bì yú cān sān èr èr zhī tú*), they **fall into endless worry and fear** (*suì duō yōujù*).

Only when the **True Spirit governs the Pure Palace** (*yuánshén yù qióngtái*), **descending truth and summoning essence** (*jiàngzhēn yǐnlíng*), **miraculously emitting the mysterious radiance** (*miào fā xuānhuī*), **transforming yin into the boundless field** (*huà yīn quánchǎng*), **and thoroughly escaping mundanity** (*liǎo tuō chénfán*), **are they forever free from entanglements** (*yǒngwú zhōngliǚ*), **their hearts aligned with the Dao** (*xīntóng yú Dào*), **silently paying homage to the Emperor** (*mò cháo Dìshàng*). This is when the **guilty beings, filled with sorrow** (*zuìzhòng bāohán*), **speak of their suffering through countless kalpas of darkness** (*zìyán lièjié yōu’àn zhī kǔ*), **having received the Emperor’s light and been rescued by His compassion** (*fú méng Dì guāng liánmǐn jiùbá*), **freed from evil deeds** (*miǎn èyè*), **with no lingering bonds** (*wú xìhù*), **and attain rebirth in heaven** (*wǎngshēng cháo Dìshàng*), **arriving at the Dao’s origin** (*zhì Dàodào qiánmiàn*).

This is the **essence of the heavenly transformation** (*běn tiānshàng zhìshén miàohuà*). **Taking it from the self** (*jìn qǔ zhūshēn*), it means **that the Dao inherently exists within the body** (*dào běn zài shēn*), **and encourages humans to reflect and practice in truth** (*rén fǎn guān shíjìàn ěr*). Therefore, the four sentences above—**"prostrating themselves and returning to their original positions"** (*qǐshǒu fùguī yuánshì lì*)—do not require further elaboration.

**The Enlightened** (*Dázhě*) **will ponder this deeply** (*xiáng yán*). **End of Volume Two of the *Imperial Daoist Canon’s Commentary*** (*Huángjīng zhùjiě juàn zhī èr jìng*). **Volume Three of the *Imperial Daoist Canon’s Commentary*** (*Huángjīng zhùjiě juàn zhī sān*).

「The **Heavenly Master of the Fifty-First Daoist Generation** (*Zì Hàn wǔshí dài Tiānshī Dà Zhēnrén Zhāng Guóxīng* **校**) **—** the **Chancellor of the Way** (*Zhuàngyuán Fāngwài yǐn Jiāngxī Jìshuǐ Luó Hóngxiān* **阅**) **—** and **Little Master Zhao of Jinan** (*Shāndōng Jìnán xiǎo Zhàozhūn Zhōu Xuányán* **集**), together compiled the **Thirteenth Chapter on Divine Pervasiveness** (*Shéntōng pǐn shísān zhāng*).

At that time, the **Jade Sovereign** (*Yùdì*) emitted a **Great Mysterious Sound** (*Dà Miàoyīn*), proclaiming to the **sacred assemblies of the Ten Directions** (*Shí fāng zhū tiān shèngzhòng*): **"You all must listen closely** (*Rú qí dì tīng*), for these **multitudes of transgressors** (*zhè zhū zuìzhòng*), from **countless kalpas** (*kuàng jié yǐlái*) onward, though **endowed with the nature of ignorance** (*zòng wú míngxìng*), have **committed the Ten Evils** (*zào shí èyè*), been **pervasively stained by the Six Dusts** (*liù chén biàn rǎn*), and **ensnared by the Three Poisons** (*sān yè yíng chán*). They indulged their thoughts and desires, never once **awakening to their faults** (*céng wú juéwù*), accumulating **hidden sins** (*yīn zuì*) and **manifest transgressions** (*yáng guò*) daily and monthly, ever deeper.

They **abandoned the Dao and defied the True** (*bèidào wéizhēn*), followed **evil paths and discarded the Rectitude** (*shùn xié qì zhèng*), every **thought and intention** (*jǔxīn yùnniàn*) generating **karmic entanglements and offenses** (*dòng jié qiān yóu*). Thus, when their lives ended, their bodies **fell into the Three Realms of Suffering** (*sān tú*, i.e., **Hell, Hungry Ghosts, and Beasts** (*dìyù, èguǐ, chùshēng*)), unable to **attain liberation** (*bùdé jiětuō*).

**Had it not been for today**, when they **encountered this wondrous Dharma assembly** (*yù shì fǎ yàn*), how could they **escape the cycle of suffering** (*hé yóu chūlí*)?

The **Great Sovereign of the Purple Micro** (*Zǐwēi Dàdì*) declared: **"When the Radiant Light of Great Compassion was being received**, the Jade Sovereign emitted this Great Mysterious Sound. This Great Mysterious Sound—**pure, resonant, and luminous** (*qīng chè xiǎng míng*), **pervading the Three Thousand Great Realms** (*biàn jí sānqiān Dàjiè*)—was heard by all, **unmatched in its wondrousness** (*zhì miào zhuó lún*). Hence, it is called the **Mysterious Sound** (*Miàoyīn*). The Jade Sovereign instructed the **sacred assemblies of the Ten Directions** (*shí fāng gè shìjiè zhū tiān dì shèngzhēn shénzhòng*):

**"You all must listen closely** (*Rú qí dì tīng*). **You**, here—**listen with utmost clarity and sincerity** (*dì*, **详审真听** *xiáng shèn zhēn tīng*). The Jade Sovereign taught the sacred assemblies to **listen closely to His instruction** (*dì tīng jǐ zhī xùn*), and thus spoke of these **multitudes of transgressors** (*zhè zhū sān è zuìzhòng*) from **countless kalpas** (*kuàng jié yǐlái*) onward.

**Transgressors** (*zuìzhòng*) from **endless kalpas** (*lì jié yǐzhì cǐ shí*), though **indulging in ignorance’s nature** (*zòng fàng wú míng zhī xìng*),—**the nature inherently luminous and aware** (*xìng běn líng míng*), yet **lost in lustful desires and chaotic delusion** (*zòngqíng zìyù, kuáng huì bèiluàn*), **acting without restraint** (*rènxīn xiǎngwéi*), **forsaking their original pure and enlightened essence** (*bùfù běnrán língjué miàotǐ*)—are thus called **nature of ignorance** (*wú míngxìng*).

They **accumulated the Ten Evils** (*shí èyè jī quān*), which are:
- **Three Evils of the Body** (*shēn sān èyè*): **killing** (*shāshēng*), **stealing** (*tōudào*), and **licentiousness** (*yéyín*);
- **Three Evils of the Heart** (*xīn sān èyè*): **greed** (*tān*), **anger** (*zhēn*), and **delusion** (*chī*);
- **Four Evils of the Mouth** (*kǒu sì èyè*): **two-tongued speech** (*liǎngshé*), **malicious slander** (*è mà*), **flirtatious words** (*qǐyǔ*), and **falsehood** (*wàng yán*).

The **Ten Evils**, **accumulated and compounded** (*shí èyè jī quān*), led to **karmic fruition and retribution** (*zào èyè bào*), hence called **evil deeds** (*èyè*).

They were **pervasively stained by the Six Dusts** (*liù chén biàn rǎn*). The **Six Dusts** (*liù chén*) are the **six impure sense faculties** (*yǎn, ěr, bí, shé, shēn, yì liù gēn bù jìng*)—**eyes, ears, nose, tongue, body, and mind** (*wèi zhī liù chén*). Some say the **Six Dusts** are **wealth, beauty, fame, food, sleep, and private desires** (*cái, sè, míng, shí, shuì, zìbiàn sīxīn*), which is also acceptable.

**Within and without the body**, all were **defiled by dust** (*jiē shòu chén wū*), **not a single spot remaining pure** (*wú xiē qīngjìng*), hence the phrase **"pervasively stained"** (*biàn rǎn*).

They were **ensnared by the Three Poisons** (*sān yè yíng chán*). The **Three Poisons** (*sān yè*) are the **three defiling deeds of body, speech, and mind** (*shēn, kǒu, xīn zhī sān dú èyè*). Some say the **Three Poisons** are **past karmic deeds, present transgressions, and future karmic accumulation** (*wǎng yīn sùyè, jiànzài qiān yè, wèilái chōng yè*), which is also acceptable.

**Ensnared** (*yíng chán*) means **twisting and binding** (*xuán, fàn zhī yì*). Their **accumulated deeds weighed heavily** (*jī yè zhòng lèi*), like **ropes binding a person**, preventing them from **freeing themselves** (*bùdé tuōshēn*), hence **"ensnared"** (*yíng chán*).

They **indulged their thoughts without restraint** (*sì fàng yìsī*), **unable to curb themselves**, **following their own desires**, **never reflecting or repenting**, **committing hidden sins** (*yōuyín guò'è zhī yīn zuì*)—**known only to themselves** (*rén bù jiànwén, zìjǐ dú zhī*)—and **manifest transgressions** (*yáng guò*)—**visible to all** (*zhòng suǒ wénjiàn, bùnéng yǎnshì*), **errors uncorrected** (*cuòwù bù gǎi*).

Day by day, month by month, their **evil deeds deepened** (*rìrì jiànjī, yuèyuè yì shēn*), as they **abandoned the Dao and defied the True** (*bèidào wéizhēn*), **yielding to false paths and forsaking Rectitude** (*shùn xiétú, qì zhèngdào*). Every **thought and intention** (*jǔxīn yùnniàn*), every **karmic impulse** (*dòng jié*), **generated entanglements and offenses** (*quān yóu*), leading to their **final demise** (*mìngzhōng wángguò zhī hòu*), where their bodies **fell into the Three Realms of Suffering** (*sān tú*, i.e., **Hell, Hungry Ghosts, and Beasts** *dìyù, èguǐ, chùshēng*)—**unable to attain liberation and transcendence** (*bùdé jiěwù chāotuō*).

**Had it not been for this day**, when they **encountered this wondrous Dharma assembly** (*yù shì miàofǎ huì yàn*), how could they **escape the suffering of their deeds** (*hé yóu chūlí yèkǔ*)?

**In my humble opinion** (*Yú àn*): **The vital essence and spirit** (*rénshēn shénqì*) are **divided into yin and yang, purity and turbidity** (*fèn yīn yáng qīng zhuó*). Those who **follow yin inclinations** (*rèn yīn qù*), **indulge in turbid evil** (*zòng zhuó'è*), **yield to false thoughts** (*shùn xiéniàn*), and **abandon true intentions** (*qì zhēnyì*), thus **brewing karmic offenses** (*nàngchéng qiān'è*), find it **difficult to escape suffering** (*nán tuō yèkǔ*).

The **longer they accumulate evil**, the **less they understand the origins of their karmic retribution** (*bùzhī qí yèbào yóulái*), hence their **failure to awaken** (*suǒyǐ bùjuéwù*).

**When the Original Spirit is settled** (*Yuánshén dìngjū*), **wondrous intentions resonate** (*miào yì zhènfū*), **the body receives the divine** (*zhōushēn chénglíng*), and **harmony is achieved with the Mysterious and Profound** (*mòqì zhòng xuán*), **yang flourishes and yin wanes** (*yáng zhǎng yīn xiāo*), **transgressions are abandoned and sins extinguished** (*xiè qiān miè zuì*), **uniting with the True Dao** (*yú dào hézhēn*)—all **stem from the Great Awakening of Mysterious Understanding** (*shì miào juéwù Dàdì*), **recognizing the karmic causes of transgressions** (*shí quān yè guò zhī yuán yīn*).

The **ancients emphasized attaining knowledge as the gateway** (*gǔ rén yǐ zhìzhī wéi rùmén*), **truly insightful** (*liáng yǒu jiàn yǐ*). **Moreover, human nature is undivided** (*kuàng rénxìng wú èr shuō*), **good and evil arising from the mind alone** (*shàn'è jiē yóu xīn*). **The nature of ignorance is the Dharma-nature itself** (*wú míngxìng jí fǎxìng yě*). Thus, **obscured by ignorance, one becomes ordinary** (*zhē yǐn wéi fán*), **while awakening reveals the sacred** (*liǎo wù wéi shèng*).

**The distinction between the ordinary and the sacred hinges on a hair’s breadth** (*shèng kuáng zhī fèn, jiàn bù róng fā*). **If humans can curb their desires and return to their true nature** (*rén néng shèqíng guīxìng*), **settle their fate with divine spirit** (*mìngdìng shénlíng*), **grasp the subtle balance of reason and desire** (*dá lǐ yù zhī jǐ*), and **know the self-origin of dusty evil** (*zhī chén'è zhī zì*), they **suddenly free themselves from suffering** (*dùn tuō yèkǔ*), **harmonize in silence with the Mysterious and Profound** (*mòqì zhòng xuán*), and thus **the Jade Sovereign’s Mysterious Sound instructs the Ten Directions** (*yù shì fǎ yàn*), **those burdened by ignorance’s nature** (*zòngxìng zào'è*), **encountering the Dharma assembly** (*yù fǎ huì yàn*) and **escaping the Three Evil Paths** (*chūlí sān èdào*).

**If one regards the nature of ignorance as a burden** (*rú yǐ wú míngxìng wéi lèi*), **seeking the True while separating from it** (*lí cǐ qiú zhēn*), **this is to divide into two paths** (*shì fèn èr tú*), **and thus one cannot attain the Mysterious and Profound in unity** (*bùdé huì yī dá miào*).

**Students must ponder this deeply** (*xuézhě wán zhī, zì zhī chāofán zhī yào*).

---

**The Fourteenth Chapter on Divine Pervasiveness** (*Shéntōng pǐn shísì zhāng*): At that time, the **sacred assemblies of the Ten Directions**, transformed by the **Jade Sovereign’s divine form** (*zhū tiān huàshēn Yùdì*), **without moving from their places** (*bùdòng qí suǒ*), **transported and united the celestial and human** (*yí jiē tiān rén*), **all arriving beneath the assembly of the Original Beginning** (*jiē lìng dé zhì Qīngwēi Tiāngōng, zuìshàng Yùqīng shèngjìng, Yuánshǐ Dàozǔ huì xià*).

**These multitudes were unaware** (*zhè zhū zhòng děng, bùjué bùzhī*). At that moment, the **Heavenly Sovereign and the assembled multitudes** (*tiān zūn jí huì zhòng děng*), **seeing the Jade Sovereign’s divine form** (*jiàn shì shí fāng Yùdì huàshēn*), **all gathered before the Heavenly Sovereign** (*pǔ jiē lái jí Tiānzūn huì qián*), **like a boundless mirror of light** (*rú wúbiān míngjìng*), **reflecting all images** (*zhào zhū yǐngxiàng*), **mutually interpenetrating**.

At that time, the **great multitudes** (*shí zhū dàzhòng*), **prostrating and gazing in awe** (*qǐshǒu zhān yǎng Yùdì huàshēn*), **the most sacred and exalted among the sacred** (*shèngzhōng zuì zūn*), **increased their pure faith** (*zhǎngzhǎng qīngxìn*), **deepening their joyful resolve** (*yì jiā zhìlè*). Their **hearts were steadfast, without retreat** (*xīn wú tuì zhuǎn*), **rising with great firmness** (*qǐ dà jiāngù*).

The **Heavenly Sovereign, the Great Emperor** (*Tiānhuáng Dàdì*) proclaimed: **"When the Radiant Light of Great Compassion was being received**, the **divine forms of the various Heavenly Palaces** (*gè dà tiāngōng huàshēn zhī Yùdì*), **the Jade Sovereigns**, **employed their Great Divine Pervasiveness** (*jí yǐ dà shéntōng*), **majestic and unmoving** (*wēiwēi bùdòng*). **Their divine light, wondrous and transformative**, **transported and united the celestial and human** (*shè qí suǒ shén guāng miào yí jiē zhū tiān zhū rén*), **all arriving beneath the Heavenly Sovereign’s assembly** (*jiē lìng dé zhì Qīngwēi Tiāngōng, zuìshàng Yùqīng shèngjìng, Yuánshǐ Dàozǔ huì xià*).

The **Yùqīng** is the most exalted and unparalleled realm—**the Great Pure, Quiet, and Secret Heaven**. The **Sacred [□] Realm** is where the **Ultimate Truth** reigns, where **emptiness and wondrous manifestation** coalesce; even the gods find it difficult to reach. It is the **land of no retreat**.

Beneath the **Primordial Origin Assembly**, only the **Great Sage** and those of **auspicious karmic connection** may **pay homage and gaze upon** the Sovereign. When the **sutra was being expounded**, all celestial and human beings gathered, and through the **Jade Sovereign’s divine transformation and compassionate guidance**, they were **transported and united** to arrive here.

Thus, these celestial and human assemblies **unwittingly and without knowing how**, found themselves beneath the **Primordial Origin Assembly**. At that time, the **Celestial Sovereign** was none other than the **Primordial Origin Celestial Sovereign**. Some may assume these were the **various Heavenly Emperors**, but this is incorrect. At that moment, the **Primordial Origin** and the gathered assembly **witnessed all the Jade Sovereigns’ transformed bodies from the Ten Directions**, **universally assembled** before the **Grand Primordial Assembly**, **displayed without obstruction**, like an **infinite, boundless mirror of radiant light**, illuminating all forms and shadows, **mutually containing and embracing without hindrance**, **encompassing none in exclusion**.

At that time, the **Great Assembly** prostrated themselves fully, **bowing their heads to the ground**, gazing upward in reverence at the **Jade Sovereign’s divine transformation**—the **most exalted and sacred of all**. The Jade Sovereign is the **Sage Teacher of all Buddhas**, the **Lord of Ten Thousand Heavens**, hence the **most exalted**. This **augments pure, sincere faith**, **deepens resolute aspiration and joy**, **reaffirms commitment to the Dao and returns to the True**, **unwavering in resolve before it can be called sincere**, **truly rejoicing in the Great Dao before it can be called devotion**.

The assembly **beheld the Jade Sovereign’s wondrous transformation**, their hearts **delighted and sincerely submissive**, hence the **increased aspiration and joy**, their **whole hearts devoted in reliance**. There was **no thought of retreat, destruction, or deviation**; they **arose with the greatest firmness and unwavering sincerity**. A **retreating heart is not firm**; a **wandering heart is not steadfast**. Without firmness and steadfastness, there is **no pure faith, no resolute joy**. Only by **gazing upon the Jade Sovereign with no thought of retreat** does one **awaken the greatest unchanging, indestructible true resolve**, **eternally devoted to the Great Dao**.

**In my humble observation**: Human **qi and spirit** share the same source, yet their transformations differ. If the **heart does not align with the Dao**, even through **guiding and directing**, it remains **not the true path**. Thus, the **spirit does not condense**, the **numinous does not manifest**, and **mysterious transformations cannot emerge**.

If the **Primordial Spirit condenses into Truth**, **wondrously encompassing all existence**, allowing one to **silently pay homage to the True Emperor**, to **meet in the Mysterious Palace of the Spirit**, **True Suchness unfettered**, **requiring no contrivance**, then the **Jade Sovereign’s divine transformations**—the **Great Divine Pervasiveness**—**unmoving, guiding and uniting the celestial and human**, arrive at the **Primordial Origin’s Pure and Secret Assembly**.

When **qi and essence converge in mystical union**, **silently conforming to the Imperial Will**, **unaware and unknowing**, the **Primordial Spirit moves the numinous**, **illuminating all wondrous manifestations**, **without restriction or leakage**, then the **Great Assembly, unaware, ascends to the upper realms**. The **Primordial Origin** and the assembly **behold the Sovereign’s transformed bodies**, all gathered like **a great radiant mirror**, their lights **brilliantly illuminating**, their forms **mutually contained without obstruction**.

When **qi and essence merge with the spirit**, **uniting in secret to return to the True**, **without defilement or deceit**, **joyfully at ease**, **once obtained, eternally retained**, **never destroyed or lost**, then the **Great Assembly gazes upon the Jade Sovereign’s transformed body**, **knowing its most exalted nature**, **augments pure faith**, **deepens resolute joy**, **has no thought of retreat**, and **arises with the greatest firmness**.

**Students who deeply embody this** will **see its marvels**.

In the **Chapter on Divine Pervasiveness (Shéntōng)**, the **celestial and human beings** who drew near **suddenly attained heavenly birth**, **glimpsing the Celestial Sovereign’s supreme assembly**, the **Dao’s pure and first realm**, **adorned by the merit of non-action**, **leaping with joy**, they **paid homage in reverence**, exclaiming, **"Never before have we witnessed such a wondrous assembly!"**

At that time, the **Jade Sovereigns’ transformed bodies from the Ten Directions** **all returned to their singular form**, seated upon the **Law Seat**. The **pure assembly** at the **Law Feast** all wished to **hear the Jade Sovereign’s original conduct and realization**, yet **dared not ask**.

Zhang Guo remarked: **"When the Jade Sovereign’s transformed bodies universally gathered**, the **celestial and human beings** who drew near **received the Sovereign’s compassionate light**, their **spirits ascending to the Supreme Mysterious**, **attaining birth in the Pure and Secret Heaven**. Suddenly, they **beheld the Great Celestial Sovereign**, the **most supreme and auspicious assembly**, the **greatly beneficial Dao’s assembly**.

An **assembly** is merely where **common folk gather**; if the **benefits of the assembly are limited**, it cannot be called a **supreme assembly**. When the **Primordial Origin expounded the Jade Scripture**, the **Jade Sovereign displayed compassionate light**, and **all beings from the various Dharma Realms universally gathered**, **gods, ghosts, and mortals eternally benefiting from great advantage**. This **opened the great destiny of the Three Teachings**, **proclaimed the profound essence of Ten Thousand Laws**. It was the **most excellent and supreme Law Feast**. Across countless kalpas, no assembly could compare—**its merit was supreme, never to be destroyed or lost**, hence the **supreme assembly**.

At the assembly, the **Primordial Origin praised the Jade Sovereign’s virtue**, **transmitted the Law of Ultimate Truth**, the **supreme single vehicle**, **universally liberating all beings to awakening**, hence the **Dao’s assembly**. This **supreme assembly** was **utterly free of defilement**, **pure, subtle, and wondrously clear**—the **first and foremost in purity**. The **Jade Sovereign’s marvelous transformation** emerged **naturally**, **universally saving and eternally benefiting** through **profound, effortless function**. The **Sand Realm** was **enlightened by grace**, **eternally bathed in blessings across kalpas**.

The **Jade Sovereign never had intent**; the **Primordial Origin never took action**. The **Ten Thousand Heavens yielded their merit**; the **Buddhas relinquished their virtue**. Through **auspicious karmic connection and wondrous assembly**, the **transformative function shone universally**, **adorned by the merit of True Non-Action**. The **celestial and human**, witnessing this, **rejoiced beyond measure**, **truly unaware of dancing with hands or stamping with feet**, yet **leaping with joy**.

At that moment, the **Great Assembly prostrated themselves fully**, **paid homage**, declaring, **"Throughout countless kalpas, we have never witnessed such a wondrous supreme assembly!"**

At that time, the **Jade Sovereigns’ transformed bodies from the Ten Directions** **all returned to their singular form**, seated upon the **Great Radiant Law Seat**. The **pure assembly** at the **Law Feast**—those **riding the Sovereign’s light**, **ascending while ancient dust vanished**, **utterly free of defilement**—**witnessed the Jade Sovereign’s transformed body displayed across all great heavenly palaces and worlds**, **all illuminated by radiant light**.

At this moment, before the **Primordial Sovereign’s Assembly**, the **Jade Sovereigns** once more **assumed their singular form**, neither lacking in their divided transformations nor excessive in their unity—**suddenly dividing, suddenly gathering**, their divine mysteries **unfathomable**, their origins **unknown**.

With such **divine powers**, the **Fourfold Assembly** contemplated this and **all wished to hear** the **Jade Sovereign’s fundamental practice and cultivation**, the **path to attaining sainthood**—yet **none dared to presume and ask**.

**The humble scholar reflects:** Within a single human body, **qi** and **spirit** circulate and guard, **meridians and sinews** interweave and connect, **exterior and interior** mutually depend, **void and subtle** respond with marvelous efficacy, **movement and stillness** sustain each other. **One origin divides into myriad forms**, while **myriad forms return to one source**.

Yet **humans, bound by materiality and obscured by greed**, indulge in **delusive desires and false imaginings**, causing **clarity to dim** and **subtlety to stagnate**. Occasionally, **those who study the Dao to benefit the world** may **exhibit petty wisdom and private virtue**, **feigning merit and grace**—their kindness and benevolence **limited in extent**, how could they **truly embody the Dao**?

If one **begins well but ends poorly**, **commences virtuously yet fails to complete**, or **forcibly contrives divisions and handles**, though **seeming enlightened**, they **do not grasp the Dao’s profundity**. Those who **truly comprehend and awaken**, whose **illumination is universal and pure**, whose **stillness and response are both steadfast**—they **neither welcome nor reject with disturbance**; their **spirit flows naturally, silent and in accord**, without **laboring to push and turn**.

When the **Dao’s subtle mechanisms are preserved**, and **human hearts retreat to listen**, **turbulence clarifies**, **obstruction dissolves**, **true self-awakening is attained**, **joy arises effortlessly**, **free from bonds and veils**, **ever-renewing in wonder**—then **all heavenly beings and humans** are born into **heavenly realms**, **beholding the Celestial Worthy’s Assembly**, **pure and transcendent**, **effortless virtue manifesting in splendor**, and **leaping with delight to pay homage**, declaring, **"Never before have we seen this!"**

**Gathering myriad into one**, the **Celestial Sovereign ascends the throne**, and **thus the Jade Sovereigns of the Ten Directions return to their singular form**, seated upon the **Law Seat**.

If the **pure assembly** wishes to hear of the **Sovereign’s practice**, yet **none dare to question presumptuously**, then the **Sutra’s origins and roots** are **naturally revealed**—**not to be spoken of as one’s own**.

Those who **study the Dao** will **perceive its wonders** in secret.

**Chapter Sixteen: The Divine Powers**

Thus, the **Celestial Worthy** proclaimed to the **Fourfold Assembly**:

**"In the distant past, there was a realm** called **Light-Strict Mannerly Joy**. Its **king was named Pure Virtue** (*Jìngdé*).

At that time, the **king had a queen**, named **Treasure Moonlight**. The **king had no heir**, and one day, he **pondered thus**: *‘I may speak as “the Sovereign” (帝, *dì*), or as “I” (朕, *zhèn*). This is the king’s own speech. It cannot be “the Sovereign.” In past kalpas, I have never spoken as “I.” It must be “我” (I, *wǒ*). Now as I grow old, yet **no crown prince exists**. If my body **should perish or collapse**—*‘崩’* (*bēng*) means death, as when a mountain **shatters in great upheaval**—**to whom will the ancestral temples and the realm be entrusted?** The **temple of the soil god** (*shè*) and the **temple of the grain god** (*jì*)—**the state depends on its people**, and **people depend on the land and grain for sustenance**. The **soil and grain deities** are **of utmost importance**, hence when a king **rules the land**, he **must speak of the ancestral temples and the realm**.

**Every realm has a great ancestral temple** (*tàimìao*), where the **first ancestor**, the **second ancestor** (who transmits the direct lineage), the **third ancestor**, the **fourth ancestor**, the **great-great-grandfather**, the **highest ancestor**, the **great-grandfather**, and the **grandfather** are enshrined. The **first ancestor** stands in the center, with the **left ancestral halls** (*Zhāo*) and the **right ancestral halls** (*Mù*) arranged on either side, totaling **nine ancestral temples**. **Humans cherish their descendants**; how much more so a **king who rules the land**—**their fate is vastly different**.

Thus, the **king worried**: *‘If I have no heir, to whom will the ancestral temples be entrusted?’* After **such contemplation**, he **immediately issued an edict**, commanding the **Daoist assemblies and pure ones** in all **palaces and temples** to **follow the Dao’s teachings**, **recite the scriptures of expiation**, **hang the sacred banners and jewels**, **maintain purity and solemnity**, and **abundantly prepare offerings**. At **each of the six periods of the day**, they **burn incense and chant the Dao**, **visiting every temple**, praying to the **immortal sages and celestial worthies**. After **half a year**, the **king’s devotion grew yet more sincere**, **never wavering from his original resolve** to establish the **Dao Assembly** and pray for expiation.

**The humble scholar reflects:** **Human life** in this body **inherits the principles of Heaven and Earth**, **takes form from Heaven and Earth’s qi**, and **receives the essence of father and mother**. Thus, **this physical existence** is **endowed with vitality**. It **receives the luminous influence of sun and moon** as **clarity**, **depends on the king’s water and land** for **sustenance**, **follows the sage’s institutions** for **order and protection**, and **learns from enlightened teachers and friends** for **advancement and growth**.

With **the Dao**, one **stands in harmony with Heaven and Earth**, **nurtures all beings**, **enters sainthood and transcends mortality**, **free from the bonds of life and death**. Without **the Dao**, all **endeavors crumble**, **one’s name fades into obscurity**, **karma accumulates in error**, and **retribution never ceases**. **Ascending to sainthood**, one’s **body perishes yet essence remains**, **dwelling with the Dao eternally**—**even descendants continue**, **sacrifices never halt**. **As a mortal**, one **has no progeny**, **cutting off ancestral rites**.

The **difference between sainthood and mortality** is **so stark**."

The threshold between sainthood and mortality—how vast is the divide?

If one knows the weight of this body’s bonds, that life and death are fleeting yet grave, and does not squander this form, if one recognizes the fourfold debts of gratitude and the gravity of the five constants, if one fulfills one’s duties, clarifies the myriad things, cultivates with reverence, advances in learning to know, and remains steadfast and resolute—heeding virtue and acting upon it without delay—if one examines oneself day and night, preserving integrity from start to finish, unashamed even before the scrutiny of heaven, and never faltering in sincerity, then one aligns with Heaven and Earth in virtue, with the sun and moon in luminosity, with the four seasons in order, and with spirits in fortune and misfortune. Thus, one awaits sainthood without doubt, never slacking for an instant, living in harmony and dying in peace, returning to the primordial transformation, leaving behind a legacy that grows ever brighter—even as the Light-Strong King’s Confession, whose devotion never wavered.

---

**Chapter Seventeen: Divine Manifestations**

Suddenly, in a single night, the Queen of Precious Moonlight dreamed of the Most High Dao Lord and the assembled Perfect Ones, their forms radiant as gold, their voices pure as jade, their essence untainted and luminous. They rode upon a five-colored dragon carriage, surrounded by banners of dazzling splendor, their seals and flags casting protective shadows. A canopy of resplendent clouds enveloped them.

At that time, the Most High Dao Lord sat serenely upon the dragon carriage, cradling an infant. The child’s every pore emitted a hundred billion rays of light, illuminating the royal palaces in hues of priceless treasures, with banners and flags leading the way as they floated through the void.

Seeing this, the Queen’s heart filled with joy. She knelt in reverence before the Dao Lord and humbly petitioned: *"My lord, the king has no heir. I pray you grant this child to be the sovereign of our realm. May your boundless compassion hear my plea and bestow this child upon me."*

The Dao Lord replied: *"I grant this child to you."*

The Queen bowed in gratitude and took the child. Upon waking, she found herself with child. After a year, on the ninth day of the first month in the Year of the Fire Horse, at noon, a son was born in the royal palace.

The Venerable Lord Guangsheng declared: *"The Light-Strong King’s prayer for an heir was answered—his resolve never faltered."*

---

Suddenly, in one night, the Queen of Precious Moonlight dreamed of the Most High Lord of Supreme Treasure Dao and the assembled Perfect Saints, their forms gleaming with golden radiance, their bodies smooth as jade, their divine light pure and unblemished. They rode upon a five-colored dragon-borne palanquin, attended by banners of radiant splendor and flags of dazzling glory, their seals casting protective shadows beneath a canopy of luminous cloud-mist.

At that time, the Most High Dao Lord sat composedly within the five-colored dragon carriage, holding a divine infant. From every pore of the child’s body, a hundred billion wondrous lights emanated, illuminating the royal halls in the splendor of a hundred treasures. Banners and flags led the way, floating through the void.

Seeing the Dao Lord holding the divine child, the Queen’s heart filled with delight. She knelt in reverence and respectfully addressed the Dao Lord: *"My lord, the king has no heir. I humbly beseech you to grant this holy child as the sovereign of our land. May your great compassion pity the king’s childlessness and grant my request, bestowing this child upon me."*

The Dao Lord answered the Queen: *"I specially grant this child to you."*

The Queen then paid her respects and thanked the Dao Lord before receiving the child. Upon waking from the dream, she found herself with child. After a year of pregnancy, on the ninth day of the first month in the Year of the Fire Horse, at noon, a son was born in the palace of the Light-Strong King of Wondrous Joy.

**A Note from the Unworthy:**
Mankind’s birth is endowed with essence and form, with the principles of duty and life. The body bears the weight of the cosmic order, and life carries the dual responsibility of heaven and earth. Noble and luminous, it is both spiritually enlightened and free. Yet the body is not mere flesh, nor is life a trivial matter.

By nature, one is of golden essence and jade-like form, pure and unstained. But if one remains in darkness, indulges in delusion, and scorns this precious gift, unable to grasp the divine mystery, to nurture the sacred embryo, then one squanders the family’s most precious treasure—this very body—rendering it useless. Even if one has some self-regard, if one does not comprehend the Dao, if one’s practice is insincere, feigning virtue while indulging in vice, then though one may appear golden without, one is but rotting rags within.

Thus, one’s very self cannot be preserved, and though endowed with noble heavenly rank, one’s virtues remain unmanifest. How then can one fulfill one’s form and perfect one’s nature, ensuring that this true master does not decline?

If one awakens to the profound roots of life and death, aligns with the secrets of heaven and man, penetrates the mysteries of yin and yang, and delves deeply into the workings of creation—if one recognizes one’s ancestral roots, acknowledges one’s parents, sees that which gave birth to one rooted in the receptive, and understands that which nurtured one rooted in the creative—if one refines the golden essence, purifies the jade-like form, attains wonder in the boundless, and comprehends the mysterious in the void, then with the spirit of emptiness one may conceive the truth of marvelous existence, forming a sacred embryo and giving birth to a saintly child. Thus, those who gave birth to one do not labor in vain, and those who nurtured one are not forgotten. With bones of gold and flesh of jade, one transcends form and spirit, withering yet reborn, enduring without end—even as the Queen of Precious Moonlight dreamed of the Most High Dao Lord and the Pure Ones, receiving the holy child as the sovereign of the realm.

Mankind is one. Awakening brings divinity; ignorance brings ruin. To perceive the Queen of Precious Moonlight’s prayer for a child is to awaken to the Dao.

---

**Chapter Eighteen: Divine Manifestations**

At the time of his birth, his body radiated a dazzling light, filling the kingdom with its brilliance. His appearance was exquisite beyond measure, and all who beheld him found no satisfaction in gazing upon him.

From infancy, he was quick-witted and wise; as he grew, he became compassionate and benevolent. Within his realm, he distributed all treasures and wealth from the royal stores, relieving the destitute, the widowed, the orphaned, the aged, the sick, the hungry, and all suffering beings.

**Chapter Eighteen: Divine Manifestations**

With virtue, love, and humility, songs of the Dao resounded; his influence reached the distant lands, and all under heaven revered and followed him, submitting to the **Daoist** Prince of Virtue. The **Highest Dao Lord** rejoiced in his father’s descent.

When the Jade Emperor was born, his body emitted a radiant light of precious treasures, illuminating the **Pure and Radiant Realm** of the Light-Strength Kingdom. His form and appearance were wondrously beautiful, and those who gazed upon him never tired of beholding him.

In his tender youth, he was keen and wise; as he matured, he became compassionate, merciful, and virtuous. Within his own kingdom, from the imperial treasuries and granaries, he freely dispersed all riches and wealth—whether in abundance or measure, without hesitation or stinginess—until all were exhausted, as if scattering them without restraint.

Yet if one were to hoard wealth for oneself, it would mean neglecting one’s sovereign, one’s kin, and one’s state. The Jade Emperor, born with divine knowledge, was the **Most Exalted Sage** of perfect conduct—how could he commit such excess?

The imperial treasuries were not bestowed upon those who already possessed fortune. Instead, they went to the penniless and destitute, those trapped in despair or peril, the widowed husband, the widow, the orphaned child, the childless elder, those without mother or father to lean upon, and in years of famine when grain was scarce or vegetables unripe. To those afflicted with illness, decay, injury, or deformity—all beings in hardship—he granted relief and aid, his virtue flowing from the sincerest depths, not merely as outward show.

With boundless kindness and compassion, gentle and modest, his blessings extended across the land, his virtue praised in song. From the borderlands to the distant wilderness, his influence spread, and all under heaven looked to him in reverence, submitting to the **Daoist** Prince of Virtue.

*"Submit"* means to join with him. The *Analects* says: *"If one day you practice self-restraint and return to the Dao, all under heaven will submit to virtue."* Indeed, seeking the Dao brings swift attainment, and its effects are vast.

The Jade Emperor was born with divine marvels, and as he grew, his boundless compassion and virtue made all under heaven submit to him. His father rejoiced all the more.

---

**Chapter Nineteen: Divine Manifestations**

Later, the king suddenly passed away. The **Daoist** Prince, now ruler, cast his gaze upon the transient nature of life—*"floating life"*, for human existence is like a cloud in the sky or a floating leaf on water, fleeting and unable to endure. He issued decrees to his ministers, declaring that the throne should be passed to one who followed the Dao.

Thus, he abandoned his kingdom and retreated to the **Universal Clarity Fragrant Mountain** to cultivate the **Great Dao**. His merit was fulfilled, and he transcended the mundane world, ascending to the heavens.

The **Fighting Mother** said: When the **Daoist** Prince of Virtue ruled the **Wondrous Joy Kingdom**, and all under heaven submitted to virtue, the king suddenly died.

The **Daoist** Prince took the throne, governing the affairs of his kingdom. He cast his gaze upon the transient nature of life—*"floating life"*, for human existence is like a cloud in the sky or a floating leaf on water, fleeting and unable to endure. Having reflected thus, he commanded his ministers, declaring that the imperial treasure should be passed to one who followed the Dao and practiced goodness.

Or it may be said: He entrusted the throne to his ministers, who were to inherit it by following the Dao and doing good. The intent remains the same.

Having entrusted the throne to the virtuous, he abandoned his kingdom and concealed himself within the **Universal Clarity Fragrant Mountain**, cultivating the **Great Dao**. The **Universal Clarity Fragrant Mountain**, according to ancient records, is the **Stonehead Mountain** of the Eastern Sea. The other mountains where the Jade Emperor left traces and expounded teachings are not the same as this Fragrant Mountain.

Once the **Daoist** Prince entered the mountain to cultivate, his merit was fulfilled, and he transcended the mundane world, ascending to the heavens.

---

The **Daoist** Prince, though born as a mortal, possessed the **True Vital Qi** of life. With this **True Qi**, one may become human. This **True Qi**, when in the heavens and earth, is the **Wondrous Principle**; when in the body, it is the **Boundless Virtue**.

The **True Qi** is profound and luminous, its light self-arising, illuminating past and present, encompassing all of **Dharma-Realm**. If one fully embodies this principle, one need not suffer hardship or peril, nor face the world’s revulsion. Yet if one abandons it in the heavens, neglects it in the body, and fails to preserve the **True Nature of Inherited Virtue**, one cannot nurture the **True Qi** to give birth to **Divine Transformation**, nor refine the **Mysterious Mechanism** to achieve **Spiritual Manifestation**. Instead, one remains obscured and dim, filled with resentment and jealousy, greedy for gain and fame, hoarding without end, unconcerned with **Daoist Morality**, unmoved by the suffering of the poor, arrogant and self-praised, inviting slander and defamation. This is to harm the **True Qi**, weaken the **Boundless Virtue**, and sink oneself into the realm of the common and ignorant, unable to attain sainthood.

If, however, one preserves the **Great Harmony**, concentrates the **Secret Intent**, and the **Sage Embryo** radiates **Precious Light**, the **Divine Infant** emits **Wondrous Scenery**, gradually unfolding **Profound Deities**, with **Spiritual Manifestation** unimpeded—if one regards **worldly power and advantage** as mud and **honors and glory** as dust, using one’s abundance to aid others’ lack, benefiting all beings and extending mercy universally, accepting the rise and fall of one’s fate without ceasing—then one’s **merit and virtue** are boundless. One’s **Great Virtue and Divine Transformation** endure forever, earning the name of **Daoist Sage**, and all of **Dharma-Realm** is bathed in compassion.

The gods rejoice, and mortals are pleased, offering service to the **Most Exalted Virtue**. Thus, the child of the heavens and earth appears in the world as a wondrous being, and even his parents are honored and delighted.

This is the divine marvel of the Jade Emperor’s birth.

As he grew, his compassion and virtue were boundless, and all under heaven submitted to him. His father rejoiced all the more.

---

How rare it is to find those who honor noble birth, yet how common the plight of poverty! Moreover, men are but drunken in dreams, lost in delusion and unaware.

Thus, those who practice the **Dao** are scarcely heard of—how much rarer still to become an **Immortal**!

Yet if one awakens to the truth that life is but a transient sojourn, as fleeting as the mayfly, and breaks free from the dust of mundane concerns, earnestly seeking the **Supreme Mystery**, penetrating its depths with clarity and resolve—without seeking swift results, yet knowing that when the time comes, transformation will unfold naturally—then one’s path will bear the name of **Immortal**.

Though ancestors may pass, their legacy endures through the **Most Exalted Sage’s** arrival in **Luó**, ensuring they are not forgotten.

Was it not the **Wondrous Bliss Prince**, abandoning his royal station to cultivate the **Dao**, who attained transcendence and delivered others?

Ah! The human body is like **Kunlun Mountain**—when the **Old Yang** is exhausted, a single **Yang** is reborn, transcending all boundaries. Through secret cultivation of the **True Essence**, time brings **Immortal Transformation**. Even the faintest aspiration toward **Immortalhood** mirrors the **Emperor’s** path.

This must be savored deeply.

---

**Chapter on Divine Powers (Twenty Sections)**

After this **kalpa** had passed, spanning eight hundred **kalpas**, he repeatedly abandoned his kingdom for the sake of all beings, severing familial bonds to study the **Dao**.

Following these **kalpas**, he spent another eight hundred practicing medicinal alchemy to heal the sick, rescuing suffering beings and granting them peace.

When this **kalpa** ended, he spent another eight hundred **kalpas** employing vast **skillful means**, unveiling the **Daoist Canons**, reciting **Sacred Scriptures**, and propagating the **True Teaching** to its fullest extent, displaying **Divine Virtue** and aiding both state and people—from the hidden to the manifest.

After these **kalpas**, he endured another eight hundred, sacrificing his body and life without hesitation, enduring humiliation and insult, offering his own flesh and blood in **Patience and Tolerance**.

Thus, through **ascetic practice** spanning **three thousand two hundred kalpas**, he attained the rank of **Golden Immortal**, named **Pure and Natural Awakened Ruler of **Dharma****, teaching all **Bodhisattvas** the sudden enlightenment of the **Great Vehicle’s True Doctrine**, gradually entering the **Mysterious and Void Supreme Dao**.

After further cultivation spanning **ten million kalpas**, he attained the rank of **Jade Emperor**.

When these words were spoken, the **Pure Assembly** of **Dharma** in unison exclaimed in wonder, for such **Sagely Virtue** had never been heard before.

**True Lord** spoke: *"In the **Jade Emperor’s** early life, after ascending the royal throne to cultivate, once these **kalpas** had passed, he spent another eight hundred as a prince. Each time he assumed the throne, it was for the sake of guiding and transforming beings, severing all ties of kinship to study the **True Dao**."*

**Kalpas** vary in scale—sixty years constitute a **Dust-Kalpa**, five hundred years a **Pure and Auspicious Assembly-Kalpa**, three thousand years a **Leap-Kalpa**; eighteen thousand years mark a **Small Kalpa**, while one hundred twenty-nine thousand six hundred years define a **Wheel-Kalpa**. When these accumulate into myriad **kalpas**, they form a **Great Kalpa**.

Though eight hundred **kalpas** may encompass both small and great, the emphasis lies in their enduring duration—roughly eight hundred **kalpas** in number.

After severing attachments to study the **Dao**, he spent another eight hundred **kalpas** administering medicinal elixirs, healing ailments, and rescuing suffering beings, granting them prosperity and joy.

When these **kalpas** concluded, he spent another eight hundred employing vast **skillful means**, unveiling the **Daoist Canon’s** sacred texts, reciting **Profound and Sacred Scriptures**, expanding the **True and Great Teaching**, and disseminating **Divine Scripture’s** virtues—assisting the state and saving the people, from the obscure to the luminous.

Some say *"from the hidden to the manifest"*—from the **Dark Realm** to the **Bright World**, encompassing all beneath heaven and earth.

This meaning is also coherent.

After these **kalpas**, he endured another eight hundred, sacrificing his life without regret, enduring humiliation and insult, offering his own flesh and blood—yet taking others’ wealth as if it were his own, for men’s gifts are like the sacrifice of blood and flesh.

In a past **kalpa**, the **Jade Emperor** endured humiliation, accepting others’ wealth even in dire poverty and suffering, when insults were heaped upon him. Though others could not bear such hardship, he felt no retreat or remorse—this was his **Sacrifice of Body and Life**, his **Patience and Tolerance**, his offering of **flesh and blood**.

Losing one’s parents is a trial even the common man finds unbearable, yet this was necessary to achieve what others could not.

Having attained **Supreme Sageship**, the **Emperor’s** act of accepting **flesh and blood** was also inevitable.

Yet the **Sage** transforms and guides the ignorant—nothing is beyond his capacity. Through **Divine Manifestations** and **Mysterious Transformations**, his true form remains unharmed.

Let the discerning understand the **Divine Harmony**; do not be bound by mere words.

From the eight hundred **kalpas** of severing attachments to study the **Dao**, through healing with medicine, teaching scriptures to deliver beings, and enduring humiliation while accepting offerings—such **ascetic practices** and **mysterious deeds** spanned **three thousand two hundred kalpas** before he attained the rank of **Golden Immortal**, bearing the fruit of **Unspoiled Perfection**, named **Pure and Natural Mysterious Awakened **Dharma** King**, teaching all **Bodhisattvas** and **Great **Sages** the sudden enlightenment of the **Great Vehicle’s True Doctrine**, gradually entering the **Void, Profound, True, and Mysterious Supreme Dao**.

The term **"Thus-Come-One"** signifies that all beings possess **Nature**—endowed with ten thousand virtues. Yet those who abandon this **Nature** fail to preserve heaven’s bestowal, their **True Suchness** obscured to the extreme, and they fall into mundane deeds.

Before his cultivation, the **Jade Emperor** abandoned the **Wondrous Bliss** royal station and spent another **three thousand two hundred kalpas**, his **virtues and transformations** boundless, never retreating, unattached and unstained, the **Great Awakened **Dharma** King**, encompassing heaven and earth, shaping all things—yet leaving none behind. Those who restore their **body and **Nature** to wholeness surpass even this by ten thousandfold; such is the **"Thus-Come-One."**

After such **great cultivation**, another ten million **kalpas** passed before he attained the rank of **Jade Emperor**, **Teacher of Ten Thousand **Heavens**.

When **Primordial Heavenly Venerable** spoke these words, the **Pure Assembly** of **Dharma** in unison exclaimed in wonder, for such **Sagely Virtue** had never been witnessed before.

**Reflection:** Man’s life is governed by **Yin** and **Yang**, his thoughts by **Principle** and **Desire**.

**Yin** and **Yang** are interdependent, alternately waxing and waning;
**Principle** and **Desire** cannot coexist—when **Desire** stirs, **Yin** congeals; when **Principle** is pure, **Yang** flourishes.
Flourishing and reaching **Transformation**, one enters the **Divine and Mysterious**.

What is placed is universally fitting, yet nothing is applied without effect.
The **Pure Yang** is the supreme virtue, yet the indolent cannot attain it.

The **Jade Emperor**, moved by pity, expounded profound truths, abandoning his royal throne without hesitation. Through eight hundred **kalpas**, he renounced his realm, severed ties of affection, and studied the **Great Dao**—this **mysterious conduct** is boundless and supreme.

Moreover, the **Original Spirit** governs the **Soul’s Pavilion**, commands the five senses, and directs all ministers.
Among the six **desires** and seven **emotions**, affection is the heaviest.
To exhaust **desire** and return to **Principle**, to subdue **emotions** and restore **Nature**, to strip away all superficial adornments and alone grasp the **Mysterious and Secret**—this is also the **Celestial Sovereign’s** abandonment of his throne to seek the **Way**.

He administered **elixirs** to save lives, ensuring their peace and comfort.
The **Jade Emperor** again traversed eight hundred **kalpas** to benefit the world.

Man’s **earthly toil** and **fantasies** blind him to true intent, leading him to old age and death without enlightenment—this is the world’s greatest affliction.
To refine the **Original Spirit**, **Essential Qi**, and the three grades of **elixir**, condensing them into **Secret Essence**, restoring **Yang** and transforming bones, living without deception and dying without loss—this is also the **inner alchemy** of saving lives through **elixirs**.

He expounded **sutras** to aid the realm, benefiting both the living and the dead.
The **Emperor** again traversed eight hundred **kalpas**.

When man attains the **Mysterious** and penetrates the **Secret**, transforming **Yin** and **Yang** with marvelous skill, ascending to the **Highest Immortal**, rescuing ghosts and spirits—his body also embodies the silent transmission of **True Scriptures** to benefit the **Dark and Bright**.

He abandoned his life, discarded flesh and blood.
The **Emperor** again traversed eight hundred **kalpas**.

When man’s heart remains undisturbed, casting off impurity, his body also embodies the **sacrifice of life**, enduring suffering, and abandoning flesh and blood.

From **kalpa** to **kalpa**, with devout cultivation unchanging, pure and unstained, his transformations arise naturally, enabling all to awaken—his merit is boundless.
Thus, as the **Jade Emperor** cultivated from over three thousand **kalpas** to a hundred million, such **unparalleled marvels** are rare indeed.

---
**Chapter Twenty-One: Divine Abilities**

At that moment, among the assembly, a **Jade Maiden** named **Yèguāng** rose from her seat.
She adjusted her robes and crown with solemn grace, knelt long before the **Dao**, and addressed the **Heavenly Venerable**:

*"Your servant, in past lives, through what merit did I attain the honor of serving at Your presence, personally offering reverence and supply for countless **kalpas**?
The **Three Pure** realms—**Golden Gates** and **Jade Capital**—are serene, tranquil, and unbounded, filled with joy and ease. I have wandered the **Holy Domain**, savoring the **Sound of Law** like relishing flavors, yet never before witnessed such **rare and wondrous** deeds.

**Ghost Valley Master** said:
When the pure assembly marveled at the **Jade Emperor’s** words, I stood among the attendants. A **Jade Maiden**, named **Yèguāng**, arose from her seat, her robes and crown perfectly adorned.
Though her attire was already pure and solemn, rising only heightened her dignity—thus, ‘adjusted her robes and crown with solemn grace.’

She moved with measured steps, kneeling long before the **Dao Ancestor**, and respectfully reported to the **Primordial Heavenly Venerable**:
‘Your servant, **Yèguāng**, in past lives, through what cause did I attain the fortune of gazing upon and serving in the presence of the **Celestial Sovereign**?’

Some might say **Yèguāng** refers to the **Jade Light** of the **Three Pure** realms, or question the origin of the **Jade Emperor’s** radiance, assuming it was the **Primordial’s** attendant.
This is incorrect.
The **Celestial Emperor** often attended the **Three Pure** realms during sermons, yet his **Jade Light** was not always visible.
Thus, the **Jade Maiden** spoke as such—there is no doubt she was the **Celestial Emperor’s** attendant.

Your servant has served at Your presence not once, personally offering reverent supply for **a hundred million kalpas**.
The **Three Pure** mystical realms—**Golden Gates**, **Jade Capital**—are silent, pure, and effortless, filled with unbounded joy and supreme ease. I have delighted in divine wanderings, nourishing my senses with the **Sound of Law**.

‘Savoring the **Sound of Law**’—the **True Secrets** of the **Pure and Lofty** are the highest **Dharma**, with inexhaustible flavors, not easily perceived.
Though the **Jade Maiden** was divine, she was still a **saintly stream** being—how could she fully comprehend?
Thus, she listened to the **Law’s sound** and pondered its depths, as one who swallows fine food and savors its taste.

This refers to her past reflections, not today’s hearing of the **Primordial’s** words.
If interpreted as today’s event, it misses the original intent.

**Yèguāng**, dwelling in the **Holy Realm** for ages, long serving at Your presence, found great delight.
Listening to the **Law’s sound**, she witnessed all marvels without fail, understanding them all—
as the **Jade Emperor** universally radiated compassion, transforming and receiving beings at will, gathering and dispersing effortlessly, generating auspicious wonders, cultivating **True Essence** through **kalpas**, his merit boundless, guiding **saintly streams** to supreme awakening.

Through countless **kalpas**, she observed and discerned past ages, yet never before witnessed such **wondrous and unheard-of** deeds.

**Reflection:** A woman’s **Yin-qi** is no different from an **Immortal Maiden**.
Her **jade-like bones** and **ice-cold spirit** naturally possess grace and elegance.
Yet, stained by dust and defilement, obscured by long-standing filth, her **Yin-Dharma essence** sinks into impure thoughts and evil deeds;
her **Six Ding-Yin spirits** become restless **hungry ghosts**.
Her thoughts are endless, her days filled with restless striving—
her meals and rest are never settled.
Her movements are frantic, unable to ascend to **Heaven**, to serve the **Mysterious Origin**.

She indulges in reckless desires, craving luxuries and fame, binding herself with vanity, burdening herself with **earthly toil**, unable to attain ease and joy.
She follows the **Wheel of Rebirth**, descending into the **mundane world** without end.
She does not hear the **True Dao** or **Mysterious Law**, daily indulging in **desires**, constantly assailed by **demons**, with no chance of **transformation**.
If **Pure Yang** secretly transforms, nurturing **Yin-essence** into **truth**—
her **pale moon** radiates boundless brilliance, her **jade body** reveals divine **transformation** without end;
her entire being becomes supremely **numinous**,
her **transformative essence** flows effortlessly, her **mysterious essence** gleams pure.
She bows in silence to the **Primordial**, worshipping the **Celestial Emperor** in stillness.
Her **Nature and Dao** are ever-clear, her heart obeys the command."

The realm of the **Crimson Terrace** and **Purple Palace**,
the palace of the **Seven Treasures** and **Five Enlightenments**,
is **serene and luminously empty**, where **effortless joy** prevails.
There, the **Divine** wanders through **mysterious domains**,
tasting the **resonant sounds of celestial jade**—
a sight of **rare wonders** in the world,
a **true supreme delight** beyond compare.

Then the **Radiant-Night Jade Maiden** arose from her seat,
adjusted her **garments and crown**,
and with **refined steps** knelt before the **Dao/Way**,
addressing the **Heavenly Sovereign**,
inquiring about her **ancient causes**,
and requesting the **Heavenly Emperor’s** **Mysterious Transformation**—
a **rare and wondrous** matter indeed.

For **Yin and Yang**, the **principle** and **Qi**,
are what all humans share.
Those who attain the **Dao** manifest **Yin-essence** as the **Jade Maiden’s** **Divine Communication**,
while those without the **Dao** descend into **darkly mundane states**,
so the **True Practice** must be made clear.

**Divine Communication** consists of **twenty-two chapters**:
*"The Radiant-Night Jade Maiden* did not discern how within the **Great Light**,
the **Ten Directions of All Heavens** appeared,
transforming into **Sacred Domains**,
where the **Heavenly Emperor’s** **Mysterious Responsive** **Divine Transformation** **Law-Body** manifested,
along with **Heavenly Sovereigns**, **Great Saints**, **Mysterious Virtue Immortals**, and **Jade Consorts** as their **attendants**.
These **Jade Maidens** possessed **lofty and dignified** appearances,
**exquisite and refined** forms,
and emitted **unparalleled divine fragrance**—
none could compare to them.

Further, the **Heavenly Emperor’s** **Divine Communication** **Mysteriously Transferred** them,
and now they all gather in the **Qingwei Heaven**—
a **pure and subtle celestial realm**.

The *Radiant-Night Jade Maiden* did not yet comprehend
how these **attendants**—the **Jade Maidens**—
by what **wondrous cause and fortunate karmic connection**,
attained such **supreme and matchless** **forms of beauty**?

For **supreme forms of beauty**—
the **Jade Maidens’** **Mysterious Transformation** **forms**—
transcend all others, with none to rival them.
In this world, there are the **Six Paths**,
among which the **Three Evil Paths**—**Hell**, **Hungry Ghosts**, and **Beastly Existence**—
lack any **beauty of form**.

The **human form**, born from the **confluence of vital essence and blood**,
scatters **Qi** and loses **Spirit**—
its filth is beyond description.
And even when alive,
it faces **decline and aging**, **illness and suffering**,
so all beauty is but a **fleeting dream**.

Thus, the **body is called an illusion**—
how could it be **supreme beauty**?

Beyond these, the **demonic maidens** of all **demonic paths**,
though their **appearances** are strange and wondrous,
and they possess the **Five Supernormal Powers**,
can **transform** and fulfill their **retributive karmic debts**,
yet they remain **self-inflicted calamities**.
How could they be called **supreme beauty**?

Only these **Jade Consorts** and **Jade Maidens**—
their **strange and peerless** **forms and refined virtues**—
surpass the **Three Realms**,
their **celestial fragrance** **Mysteriously Transformed**,
neither **waning nor mundane**,
unseen by the **worldly**—
these are the **supreme beauty**,
which the *Radiant-Night Jade Maiden* still could not fathom.

Thus, the **Heavenly Sovereign’s** **Supreme Compassion** revealed to her what she had not yet understood:
the **Jade Consorts’** **forms and divine fragrance**,
and the **principle** of their **exquisite and refined** **bodies**.

The humble one reflects:
*"All worldly blessings and karmic deeds*
arise from the **heart’s** creation.
The **heart** governs **Nature and Virtue**,
and **Nature** possesses nothing it does not contain.
The **Mysterious Transformation** of **Yin and Yang**—
everyone inherently possesses it.
Without **Daoic cultivation**,
one aligns with **Yin** and falls into **darkly mundane states**,
becoming a **rotting corpse and decaying bones**—
the **root of cyclic rebirth**.

But when one **awakens to the Dao** and **cultivates True Practice**,
then **Yin** is also the **body’s** **upright Qi**,
and the **Six Celestial Powers** reveal their **wondrous essence**,
illuminating **Heaven’s Light** in stillness.
The **Jade Maiden’s** **True Fragrance** is the **exquisite manifestation** of her **body**.

Her **entire being** is **pervasively numinous**,
ascending to the **Crimson Terrace’s** **Jade Towers**,
the **Six Yang’s** **Secret Domain**,
where the **True King** **reigns in due season**.
Her **Law-Body** **broadly transforms**,
commanding **Tigers** and **Dragon** **Spirits**;
she **refines the Jade Fluid** in the **Mysterious Palace**,
and the **Jade Consorts** **stand at her right side**;
she gathers the **Secret Treasures** of **Dan Elixir**,
and the **fragrance of the Celestial Maidens** drifts pure.

This is also how the **Heavenly Emperor’s Light** manifests the **Ten Directions of Heavenly Domains**.
There are the **Heavenly Emperor’s Responsive Law-Bodies**,
the **Jade Maidens** as **attendants**,
**Mysteriously Transferred** by **Divine Communication** to dwell in the **Qingwei Heaven**.

For all humans possess **Nature**,
containing **Yin and Yang**,
embracing **all wondrous essences**—
their **bodies** align with **Heaven’s**.
The **Jade Consorts’** **Divine Communication** and **wondrous range**—
those who hear of them all understand,
yet why did the *Radiant-Night Jade Maiden*, now **saintly and attending the Emperor**,
still fail to grasp it?

For **cultivation and attainment** have **ranked distinctions** of **high and low**,
and the **saintly body** arises from the **Dao’s** **Mysterious Transformation**.
Whatever **fruit** one attains,
one’s **Divine Communication** will match—
only **saints** know **saints**, only **virtuous ones** know **virtuous ones**—
not a **single particle** can be falsely borrowed.

The **Jade Consorts** and **Jade Maidens**, by their **Heavenly True Essence**,
**Divinely Transform** to save people—
thus their **radiant and numinous** **forms**,
and their **pure and wondrous** **fragrance**,
are beyond the *Radiant-Night Jade Maiden’s* understanding.

Her ignorance stems not from **retreat or concealment**,
but from the **initial stages** of her **saintly body**,
and the **difference in rank**—
she had not yet reached their level.

Alas, even the **Jade Consorts** are difficult to comprehend—
how could the **Heavenly Emperor’s Light** and **Divine Transformation** be measured?

The *Radiant-Night Jade Maiden* could not yet know—
how could others?

**Heavenly and mundane beings share one Nature**,
and humans stand **equal in rank** to the **Heavenly Emperor**.
Yet even to **know** this is beyond them—
how could they attain **sainthood**?

People should **reflect upon it** and **strive earnestly**.

**Chapter Twenty-Three of Divine Communication**:
At that time, the **Heavenly Sovereign** spoke to the *Radiant-Night Jade Maiden*:
"You have indeed **entered the stream of sainthood**,
though possessing **wisdom**, you still cannot **fully comprehend** it.

These **Jade Maidens**—
from **countless eons past**—
**cultivated all wondrous virtues**,
**mastered the gates of liberation**,
and shared **pure faith**, **pure understanding**, **pure contemplation**,
**pure conduct**, **pure body**, **pure heart**, **pure intention**,
and **pure fruit and retribution**.

They shared **Great Compassion** and **Great Mercy**,
protecting all **sentient beings** like a **mother tenderly cradling her children**,
and **loving them as her own flesh**.

The **Heavenly Sovereign** spoke to the *Radiant-Night Jade Maiden*:

*"You have devotedly upheld the **precepts**, your mind immersed in the **Great Dao**,
and with **pure fasting** and **grand vows**, for countless eons you have revered the **Jade Emperor**."*

The **Vacuous-Emptiness Emperor** declared:
*"When you, *Radiant-Night*, sought **saintly blessings** and your **unawakened mind** was opened,
the **Primordial Heavenly Sovereign** spoke to the *Jade Maiden*:
'You have indeed **entered the stream of sainthood**.
You—**you**—are now aligned with the **saints**, becoming one with their **flow and kind**.
Since you are **saintly**, you should know **all things**.
Yet as one who has **only just entered the stream of sainthood**,
though you possess **acute wisdom and keen insight**,
you still cannot **fully penetrate and comprehend** it.

These **attendants of the Jade Emperor**—
they did not **suddenly attain** such **divine powers**.
From **past eons beyond measure**, they **cultivated all wondrous virtues**,
**fully mastering the gates of great awakening and liberation**,
**untainted through eons**, their **orthodox faith** never wavering.
The Jade Emperor, **from ancient times**, has always held **pure faith**.
The *Jade Maidens*’ **wondrous practices** across eons also share this **pure faith**.
They **transcend sensory forms**, achieving **great liberation**.
The Jade Emperor, **from ancient times**, has always held **pure understanding**.
The *Jade Maidens*’ **wondrous practices** across eons also share this **pure understanding**.
Their **true contemplation** is **beyond birth**, severing all **realms of existence**.
The Jade Emperor, **from ancient times**, has always held **pure contemplation**.
The *Jade Maidens*’ **wondrous practices** across eons also share this **pure contemplation**.
Their **wondrous conduct** is **sublime and unblemished**, forever without fault.
The Jade Emperor, **from ancient times**, has always held **pure conduct**.
The *Jade Maidens*’ **wondrous practices** across eons also share this **pure conduct**.
Their **Dao-body** is **untainted by defilement**.
The Jade Emperor, **from ancient times**, has always held **pure body**.
The *Jade Maidens*’ **wondrous practices** across eons also share this **pure body**.
Their **heart is the Dao**, their **Dao is the heart**—**serene and unobstructed**.
The Jade Emperor, **from ancient times**, has always held **pure heart**.
The *Jade Maidens*’ **wondrous practices** across eons also share this **pure heart**.
They **transcend inner and outer**, **abandoning all contrivance and artifice**.
The Jade Emperor, **from ancient times**, has always held **pure intention**.
The *Jade Maidens*’ **wondrous practices** across eons also share this **pure intention**.
They **dwell in the Upper Clarity**, never regressing.
The Jade Emperor, having **attained sainthood**, has achieved **pure fruit**.
The *Jade Maidens*’ **wondrous practices** across eons also share this **pure fruit**.
Through **vast eons**, their **merits are immeasurable**.
The Jade Emperor, **Most Exalted**, has achieved **pure retribution**.
The *Jade Maidens*’ **wondrous practices** across eons also share this **pure retribution**.
Their **compassion extends to the sands of the world**, their **benevolence permeates eons**.
The Jade Emperor possesses **Great Compassion**.
The *Jade Maidens*’ **wondrous practices** also share this **Great Compassion**.
They **compassionately regard all beings**, sparing none.
The Jade Emperor possesses **Great Mercy**.
The *Jade Maidens*’ **wondrous practices** also share this **Great Mercy**.
The *Jade Maidens*’ **Great Compassion and Mercy** align with the Jade Emperor’s.
How so?
They **shelter and protect all sentient beings**,
like a **loving mother tenderly nurturing her cherished infant**,
with **sincere, boundless affection**.
Moreover, they **uphold the Mystic Precepts** with **unwavering devotion**.
Some say:
*'With **reverent-hearted** and **strictly disciplined** minds,
**concentrated and undivided**, they thus **immerse their hearts** in the **Great Dao**.*
This meaning is even more profound.

The *Jade Maidens*’ **return to the Great Dao** is not fleeting;
they are **pure, devout, and expansive in their grand vows**,
revering and respecting the Jade Emperor through countless eons.

**My reflection:**
If one possesses **orthodox faith**, naturally **awakening**,
with **contemplation severed** and **conduct pure**,
the **body untainted**, the **heart clear**, and the **intention pure**,
they will **attain the True Reality**, **realize the fruit**, and **gain retribution**.
If they **practice Great Compassion and Mercy**,
**strictly uphold the wondrous precepts**,
and **face the Supreme Emperor** without wavering through ages,
then **ascension to the celestial realm is attainable**.

Worldly beings, **misled by deluded views**,
**distracted by杂念** and **errant conduct**,
cannot **cultivate the body**, their **hearts are agitated**, their **intentions disordered**,
their **fruit and retribution entangled**—
all because they lack **compassion and do not trust the Dao**.
Thus, though *Radiant-Night* has **just entered the stream of sainthood**,
she still cannot **fully grasp the *Jade Maidens’* wondrous practices**,
let alone **align with them**.
**Intention**—everyone possesses it.
If **refined**, then the *Jade Maidens’* **wondrous practices** reside within you."*

**Chapter Twenty-Four of Divine Communication**:
These *Jade Maidens* are **not truly female**—
they are **Heaven’s True Ones**,
manifesting as *Jade Maidens* to **guide and transform all beings in the Dharma-realm into the Dao**.
Thus, their **forms, colors, and divine powers**,
their **wisdom—both revealed and concealed**,
and their **transformations** are **identical to the Emperor’s**.

At that time, upon hearing this, *Radiant-Night*’s **mind opened in awakening**;
she **bowed in reverence**, **rejoiced**, and **silently returned to her place**.

**Guan Yinzi** declared:
*"These *Jade Maidens* who attend the Jade Emperor—
those who cultivated **wondrous virtues** across **countless eons**—
are **not truly female bodies**;
they are **Heavenly Immortals**, **True Ones of the Dao**,
manifesting as *Jade Maidens* to **transform and guide all beings in the Dharma-realm into the Way**.
Since they are **embodiments of the True Ones**,
their **forms are not female by nature**—
thus their **forms, colors, divine powers, and wisdom**,
whether **concealed or revealed**, are **not shallow or fleeting**,
but **align with the Emperor’s**.

All mortals possess **bodies**,
but the **color-body** is an **illusion**, unable to **diversify and transform**,
making it difficult to **align with the Emperor’s body**.
As for **transformed bodies of demons and spirits**,
they are **deceptive illusions**—
even less worthy of mention.

There are **celestial beings** above—
some **five *li*** distant, some **several *li***, some **one or two *yojanas***,
some **hundreds of billions of *zhang***,
