some in **heavenly palaces**, some in **true realms**, some in **human worlds**.
They may **manifest here**, but cannot **transform elsewhere**.
Some may **appear through hearing or sight**, yet cannot **wondrously guide**.
They are **confined to a place**, **bound by time**—
none of these are the **supreme wondrous transformations of the Dharma-body**.

The *Jade Maidens*’ **transformed bodies** appear **throughout all worlds**,
**gathering and dispersing at will**, **transcending all peers**—
their **bodies align with the Emperor’s**.

All **bodies are forms**,
but if their **forms are not wondrously pure**,
or if they are **beautiful yet fleeting**,
they do not **align with the Emperor’s forms**.

The *Jade Maidens*’ **transformed bodies** possess **wondrous, strange, and beautiful forms**,
**perfectly manifesting wherever they appear**,
**unchanging forever**.
Thus, their **forms align with the Emperor’s."*

The **celestial beings, human deities, and demonic Daoists** all possess **divine powers (shén tōng)**, yet their **transformations are limited**, and their **powers do not encompass the Six Perfections (liù tōng)**—thus, their **divine powers do not align with the Emperor’s**.

The *Jade Maidens’* **divine transformations are boundless**, and they **all master the Six Perfections**—thus, their **divine powers align with the Emperor’s**.

Mortals and **spirit-people** all possess **wisdom**, yet they are **obstructed by barriers**, their understanding **incomplete**. Some **borrow forms to illuminate**, yet cannot **fully grasp the truth**—this is not **wisdom aligning with the Emperor’s**.

The *Jade Maidens* **pierce all obscurations without remainder**, their **foresight unobstructed**—thus, their **wisdom aligns with the Emperor’s**.

Those who know **divine powers** all **skillfully conceal themselves**, yet their concealment **leaves traces**—this does not align with the Emperor’s.

The *Jade Maidens*, when dispersed, **return to the Great Emptiness (Tài Xū)**, not merely **swallowing Mount Sumeru as a mustard seed**—this is **wondrous concealment without trace**, their **concealment aligning with the Emperor’s**.

To **conceal is to manifest**; if the **manifestation is not the Great Radiance**, it does not align with the Emperor’s.
The *Jade Maidens* **wondrously reveal the Pure and Subtle**, their **divine forms seen across all realms**—thus, their **manifestation aligns with the Emperor’s**.

To possess **divine powers, wisdom, concealment, and manifestation**—this is the **ability to transform**.
If **transformation relies on contrivance**, it does not align with the Emperor’s.
The *Jade Maidens* **transform wondrously without intent**, their **divine transformations arising naturally**—thus, their **transformation aligns with the Emperor’s**.

At this time, **Yèguāng** heard **Yuánshǐ** speak of the *Jade Maidens’* **wondrous transformations**, and their meaning **fully unfolded**. His heart **suddenly opened and awoke**, comprehending the **source of the *Jade Maidens’* wondrous transformations**. He **kneeling, paid homage**, rejoicing and celebrating in silence, **forgetting speech**, then **returned to his original station**.

**My humble reflection:** The **human body’s yin and yang** are not **distinctly two substances**, but **one becoming two**—**yin nourishes yang, yang generates yin**—this is the **ultimate root**.

When **cultivating the True and attaining the Dao**, the **Six Ding yin-spirits manifest as the *Jade Maidens*’ wondrous transformations**.
Their **marvelous mechanisms** share the same function as the **original spirit’s profound essence**.

This **yin-transformation reveals the numinous**—how could it be limited to the **earthly substance (kūn)**? It **extends to the heavenly body**, **nourishing and gestating**, the **transformation of the Brahmanic qi and yang-light**.

Moreover, the **celestial deities’ transformations are boundless**, their **teachings and guidance of beings** each **adapted to circumstances**.
When **a male form is needed**, they **manifest as male

At that time, the **High Void, Pure Clarity Celestial Sovereign (Tiānzhǔ)** and his **divine retinue** rode in **Eight Auspicious Dragon Chariots**, beneath **Nine Radiant Treasure Canopies**, playing **sacred melodies of the Mysterious Song** and chanting **Sūtras of the Boundless Treasures from the Three Caverns**. They scattered **Celestial Treasure Flowers**, sprayed **Heavenly Pure Fragrances**, and traversed the void in lofty strides, arriving before the **Daoist Assembly**.

By the **virtue/power** of the **Celestial Venerable Emperor (Yùhuáng Dàdì)**, the **Eight Auspicious Dragon Chariots**—the **Eight Scenic Marvels**—manifested as a **Treasure Canopy** in the empty space, sheltering all the gathered **dharma-assembly (fǎhuì)**, without fail or omission.

**Red Pine (Chìsōngzǐ)** remarked: *"When the Jade Maidens of the Night Radiance return to their stations, it is the High Void, Pure Clarity Celestial Sovereign and his retinue from the Original Heaven who come, not the Sovereign of the Distinct Heaven and his retinue."*

When the **High Void, Pure Clarity Celestial Sovereign** and his **divine retinue** arrive, each rides an **Eight Auspicious Radiant Dragon Chariot**, beneath a **Nine Glow Illuminating Treasure Canopy**.

**Eight Auspicious (Bā Jǐng)** has alternate readings: **Eight Auspicious Treasures and Marvels (Bā Bǎo Miào Jǐng)**, **Eight Divine Trigrams’ Scenes (Bāguà Shén Jǐng)**, or **Eight Colored Radiant Scenes (Bā sè Guāng Jǐng)**. Essentially, the **divine chariots of Heaven** encompass the **scenic wonders of the eight directions**, harmonizing the **eight seasonal rhythms**, hence the term **Eight Auspicious**.

They play **sacred melodies of the Great Mysterious Song**, chant **Sūtras of the Boundless Merit and Three Caverns’ Treasures**, scatter **Celestial Marvelous Flowers**, spray **Heavenly Pure Fragrances**, traverse the void in lofty strides, and arrive before the **Daoist Assembly**, respectfully bowing to the **virtue/power** of the **Celestial Venerable Emperor (Yùhuáng Dàdì)**. At that moment, the **Treasure Flowers** coalesce into a **Canopy**, sheltering the entire **dharma-assembly**, without exception.

**My humble reflection:** When **humans cultivate the True (Zhēn)**, they **pay homage to the Celestial Sovereign**, **offer reverence to the Primordial Emperor**, **recite the True Scripture in silence**, and **transform the Pure Void’s divine light**. In the **morning assembly of the Mysterious Realm**, they display **secret marvels of jade flowers**, **encircling and sheltering all the divine beings**. These are all **manifestations of the Primordial Emperor’s secret guidance**, as the **original spirit’s benevolent influence** reaches out. When the **High Void, Pure Clarity Celestial Sovereign** arrives at the **dharma-feast**, he presents **sacred melodies**, rides **divine chariots**, and the **celestial flowers** he scatters, under the **virtue/power** of the **Celestial Venerable Emperor (Yùhuáng Dàdì)**, coalesce into a **Canopy sheltering all without remainder**.

Those with **aspiration**, observing this **scriptural precedent** and **grasping its essence**, will find that the **auspicious transformations of Heaven** are entirely embodied within **one’s own person**.

**Chapter Twenty-Five of the *Divine Transformations* (Shéntōng Pǐn)**

At that time, the **High Void, Pure Clarity Celestial Sovereign**, witnessing this **rare and wondrous event**, bowed his head and knelt respectfully, addressing the **Celestial Venerable Emperor (Yùhuáng Dàdì)**: *"Your lowly servant has been negligent, arriving late at the dharma-feast. Today’s auspicious occasion coincides with the **Encountering of the Sacred Bridge of Compassionate Salvation**. Both the **hidden and the manifest**, the **sage and the common**, all partake in the **blessings of the Sage**. The **great radiance** is revealed, manifesting **rare and wondrous forms**, illuminating the **Heavens above**. The **Four Brahmā (Fàn) Realms** and **Six Desires (Liùyù)**, all the **lands of delight** and **divine assemblies of the True and Sage**, beholding this **radiance**, gather in their entirety. Below, it illuminates the **World of the Boundless Void (Wújí Shìjiè)**, akin to the **Pure Clarity Realm (Xuándū Jìng)**, approaching the **Nine Heavens**, where **spirit winds play melodies** and **tone and pitch harmonize**, resonating through the **cloud courts**, all forming **sacred scriptures**. All beings attain **Daoist transformation**."

Even the **Yin-Tu (Yòudū) Iron Enclosure**, the **endless night of the Nine Abysses**, and all **suffering beings in the underworlds**—they all receive the **light’s virtue/power** and are reborn in the **Heavens**, experiencing **joy and delight**. Today’s **celestial marvelous flowers** coalesce into a **Canopy**, sheltering the entire **dharma-feast**. All the gathered **divine assemblies** receive this **radiance’s virtue/power**.

The **thousand aeons’ merit** of your servants, the **Nine Heavens’ destiny**, the **Dao’s resplendent path**, and the **orthodox dharma’s flourishing**—today’s great auspiciousness fulfills the **lofty aspiration of sacred function**.

**The True Lord of the Fire Sovereign (Huǒdì Zhēnjūn)** declared: *"At the moment when the **Treasure Flowers coalesce into a Canopy**, sheltering all the gathered **divine assemblies**, the **High Void, Pure Clarity Celestial Sovereign** witnesses this **rare and wondrous event**, bowing his head and kneeling, then humbly reports to the **Celestial Venerable Emperor (Yùhuáng Dàdì)** and the **Great Jade Emperor (Yùhuáng Dàdì)**, saying: ‘Your lowly servant has been negligent and remiss, arriving late at the **dharma-feast**. Today’s auspicious hour and festive heavens coincide with the **Encountering of the Sacred Bridge of Compassionate Salvation**.’*

**Bridge (Qiáo)** refers to what **mortals construct** to **cross rivers and streams**, avoiding **barefoot wading**. However, all **worldly bridges** require **wood or stone** to form, and their **salvage is limited**, prone to **damage and destruction**—even the **Great Yangtze, mighty rivers, and vast seas** cannot be crossed by such means.

Yet the **scriptural merit and sacred function’s virtue/power** **salvage the boundless eons**, **encircle the sand-realm (shājiè)**, without need of **construction or form**. Through **subtle transformation and divine mechanisms**, they **guide beings out of the River of Love**, **away from the Sea of Desire**, **free from the Blood Lake**, and **dispel the Flood Disaster**, enduring forever without decay—thus the term **Sacred Bridge of Compassionate Salvation**.

Both the **hidden and the manifest**, the **sage and the common**—all partake equally in the **blessings of the utmost sage**.

The Jade Emperor emitted the **Universal Radiant Great Bright Light**, manifesting the **rare and wondrous divine form**, illuminating all the **realms of the heavens**—the **Four Brahmā heavens, the Six Desire realms**, and every **pure land of bliss**. All **celestial beings, immortals, divine saints, and sacred assemblies** beheld this **Great Bright Light**, and **clouds swiftly gathered in assembly**.

The clouds converged—**suddenly filling the sky**, unknown in origin.
The **sacred assembly gathered like clouds**, hence the term **"cloud-gathering"**.

Its light shone downward upon the **boundless worlds of the Lower Realm**, all aligned with the **Pure and Subtle Heavenly Pure Domain**, drawing near to the **Nine Sovereign Celestial Heights**. Within the light, **divine winds played celestial harmonies**, blending like **palace-scale and commercial tones** in perfect accord.

Though **music’s five tones**—**metal, wood, water, fire, earth**—are divided into **pure and impure**, aligned with the **Five Phases**, their **natural marvels** may yet be hard to replicate. Yet the **Heavenly Divine Winds** harmonize effortlessly, surpassing mortal music. Their **resonant, vibrant sounds** in the **Cloud Court** all coalesce into the **Three Caverns’ Precious Chapters**.

All beings in the **Lower Realms** attained the **Great Dao’s profound transformation**. The **Yin-Tu prisons**, the **Iron Encircled City**, the **Eternal Night of the Nine Abysses**—all tormented souls in the **Nine Hells** now **reverently submit to the Jade Emperor’s Great Bright Light’s power**, ascending to **celestial palaces** and receiving **bliss**.

Today, the **Heavenly Treasures’ wondrous flowers** I scattered **swirled and formed a canopy**, **overshadowing the sacred law-assembly’s gathering**, all **reverently submitting to the Heavenly Sovereign Jade Emperor’s mighty virtue and divine power**.

I, the **Clear and Bright Heavenly Sovereign**, and others—this is not merely fortune for one age. Encountering this **rare marvel**, we have cultivated **meritorious causes across countless eons**, now meeting the **Nine-Heaven’s auspicious convergence**. The **Heavenly Dao’s boundless expanse** flourishes, the **Supreme Mysterious Law** thrives in grandeur.

One says: *"The Primordial Sovereign’s enlightenment unfolded the **Supreme Law**, the **august winds** were pure and vast, the **Dao** spread evenly—no heretical paths existed, just the **flourishing of the True Law**."* This is acceptable.

Today’s **auspicious hour** is **greatly fortunate**. All **celestial beings and myriad creatures** attain the **Supreme Mysterious Transformation’s blessings**.

One also says: *"All aspire to revere the **Mysterious Function**, humbly presenting the **Dao’s essentials**."* This too is acceptable.

In reflection: Though the **human body is small**, it **embodies heaven and earth**, containing all things, encompassing all marvels. The **pure, empty, and refined qi** governs the **Six Yang**, and there exists the **High and Pure Clear-Bright Heavenly Sovereign**.

If the **original spirit wanders unmastered**, the **profound transformation remains unseen**, one **sinks into the waves of grace**, the **mechanism drowned in the sea of suffering**. The **great currents and monstrous tides** surge endlessly—how can one **avoid drowning**, **rescue the deluded**?

If **one alone is immersed**, they **plunge others into ruin**, harming self and others—this need not be discussed. Those **stagnant in the lesser vehicle**, **bewildered by tangential paths**, their **flow without source**, **inevitably dry up**—this too is unworthy of mention.

Sometimes, the **spiritual source is deepened**, the **Dao’s pulse connected**, nearly **transformed**. Yet if one **hoards their essence**, the **grace descends not**, and this is **far from ultimate attainment**.

Thus, some **realize the fruits of the Four Brahmā and Six Desire realms** but **fail to reach the Nine Sovereign’s Seven-Treasured Domain**, receiving **human blessings** or becoming **prison wardens and demon kings**, even **sinking into the Three Evil Paths** and **Nine Abyssal Realms**—**woe beyond measure!**

When the **profound transformation is not manifest**, the **wondrous resonance unseen**, the **true scriptures fail to circulate**, the **jade flowers lack luster**—this stems from **not planting meritorious causes**, **not trusting the True Law**. Unable to **hear the boundless, even Dao**, one **cannot revere the Mysterious Function**.

If one **concentrates the Mysterious Spirit**, becomes the **Heavenly Sovereign**, the **pure, empty, and refined essence**—when the **later stages unfold**, they **penetrate Caoqi’s grove**, **absorb the Western River’s essence**, **merge with the Golden Elixir**, and **ascend to the Dao’s shore**. The **sea of suffering and karmic pits** are **forever annihilated**; one **transcends the Six Desires**, **rises above the Four Brahmā**, **gathers all spirits**, and **illuminates the hidden realms**.

The **divine winds stir the true**, the **wondrous resonance is unparalleled**—the **true scriptures circulate without cessation**, all things **receive endless grace**. The **Yin-Tu prisons are broken**, the **Nine Abysses illuminated**, the **hells transformed into pure lands**, and **sinful beings attain bliss**. One’s **darkness turns to radiance**; the **jade flowers bloom in crimson hues**, **overshadowing all marvels**. This is the **real and void’s essence**, the **original spirit’s power**.

Without **cultivating virtuous causes**, **firmly trusting the True Law**, how could one **hear the Heavenly Dao’s refreshing winds**, **revere the Mysterious Function**?

Ah! This **body’s true marvel**—**witnessing the Clear-Bright Heavenly Sovereign’s later law-assembly**, **celebrating the Sacred Bridge’s encounter**. **Proclaiming the Sacred Transformation**, **extolling the Mysterious Function**—this is the **Dao’s salvation for both hidden and manifest beings**.

To **cultivate meritorious causes**, **broaden wondrous deeds**, **not seeking swift transformation**—the **marvel is natural**. This too **verifies the Sacred True Precepts**.

Let those who **seek the Dao** savor this **of their own accord**.

---
**Chapter Twenty-Seven: The Divine Powers**

At that time, during this **sacred assembly**, all **revered the Mysterious Function**.

The **High and Pure Clear-Bright Heavenly Sovereign**—as explained before—**with verses praised the Jade Emperor**:

*"Clear-Bright Heavenly Sovereign,*
*With verses, the Jade Emperor is praised.*

*The Golden Gate’s Primordial Vault Sovereign,*
*(Note: Some texts read ‘Sovereign’ instead of ‘Vault.’ Examining the scripture’s intent, the Jade Emperor is the Heavenly Sovereign, the **Buddhas’ teacher**, ruling the **Yellow Golden Gate**, the **Pure Vault’s Azure Expanse’s ancestral elder**—hence ‘Sovereign.’ Some read ‘Sovereign,’ referring merely to the Heavenly Emperor.)*

*The Highest Jade Sovereign’s Venerable One,*
*(As explained before.)*

*Whose wondrous form surpasses all heavens.*
*(All celestial beings and gods possess beautiful forms—some decayed or limited by their heavens’ transformations, unable to fully manifest. The Jade Emperor’s **form and beauty are boundless**, his **appearance uniquely surpassing all heavens.**)*

*The merciful light illuminates the Three Realms.*
*(The **great compassionate light** pierces **heaven, earth, and humanity**—hence ‘universally illuminating the Three Realms.’)*

*The True and Sacred Mysterious Dao’s Master."* *(The **one true, supreme sacred, divine, and wondrous Dao’s master**.)*

The Jade Emperor’s conduct is the **True and Sacred Mysterious Dao’s Master**—
the **Way’s sovereign teacher**.

Heaven and humanity rely upon this teacher.
The Jade Emperor is the **preceptor of heaven and humanity**, the **sovereign of all gods**, the **sacred deity of the Highest Heaven**.
All beings in the world revere and depend upon him, relying upon his **virtue and transformative power**—
he is the **teacher of heaven and humanity**.

The **Great Vehicle’s teachings** descend in speech,
the **Dao’s Three Vehicles**, divided into **high, middle, and low**.
There is also the **supreme single Vehicle**, transcending stages,
exalted above the three grades, encompassing all without remainder—
this is the **Great Vehicle**.

The gods’ teachings vary with their wisdom and insight.
The Great Vehicle is rare to hear.
The Jade Emperor’s teachings clearly demonstrate the **true宗 (zong)**, penetrating both high and low,
embracing all grades.
All beings benefit from his instruction, all attain liberation—
this is the **Great Vehicle’s descending speech**.

The **True One points out the lost path**.
The Jade Emperor, with the **true宗 (zong) and mysterious unity of wondrous principle**,
clearly illuminates and awakens those lost—
this is the **direct pointing, single transmission**, preventing beings from falling into minor, tangential teachings.
It is to guide them along the **great path**, so they do not stray into false ways.

His **virtue and power are as boundless as the void**.
All things under heaven have limits.
Only the void endures through kalpas without change.
The Jade Emperor’s **great virtue and supreme power** are immeasurable, like the void—
inexhaustible, beyond reckoning.
Other gods possess virtue and power, some distant, some near, some small, some great,
but they can only be compared proportionally.
The Jade Emperor’s virtue and power have no equal—
thus, like the void, they are **praiseworthy without end**.

Praise for the Jade Emperor, like the void, is inexhaustible.
Reverence for him is boundless.
Praise is without limit.
His **august virtue cannot be named**.

Yellow Stone Master said:
*"The Highest, Clear, and Illuminating Heavenly Sovereign,
though he may appear later at the Law Assembly,
truly saw the Jade Emperor’s wondrous transformations—
divine mien and marvelous sights—
and, filled with reverence, composed this wondrous verse
to praise the Jade Emperor."*

In ancient times, Zai Wo, Zi Gong, and You Ruo praised Confucius with profound insight,
demonstrating wisdom sufficient to know the Sage.
Now, the Clear and Illuminating Heavenly Sovereign praises the Jade Emperor’s virtue as boundless,
his praise without end—
no other eulogy matches this depth.
This is the wisdom of Zai Wo, Zi Gong, and You Ruo in recognizing Confucius.
This verse may truly be called **profound speech**.

**My humble reflection:**
The **original spirit of the human body** remains unaltered through kalpas.
The **true master of the four limbs** is the **source of all things**.
Its wondrous excellence surpasses the six yang,
its compassion protects the Three Elements.
It is the **true teacher of the self**—
the **qi and spirit** upon which all depends.

Its **illuminating light and resonant sound** are the **supreme Law**,
directly shattering delusion,
guiding one to **universal practice**,
embodying **mysterious essence and wondrous function**.
Where its **virtue extends**, it equals the void.
How could praise for it ever be exhausted?
If one cannot **turn inward and reflect**, failing to recognize this **true宗 (zong)**,
how could they know the Jade Emperor’s virtue?
How much less could they grasp the **benefits of the scriptures**?
It is no wonder they fail to **secretly awaken to the true body**.

The Clear and Illuminating Heavenly Sovereign, gazing upon the Jade Emperor’s virtue,
composed this wondrous verse to praise him—
not only to exalt the **Heavenly Blessing**,
but also to **command humanity to turn inward**.

If one truly **harmonizes with the original truth**,
knows the **power of the Law**,
follows Heaven without partiality,
and shares in the Emperor’s virtue,
they will not be confused by other paths,
will not lose Heaven’s treasure,
and may aspire to the **supreme Sage**.
**Aspiring scholars, take heed!**

**Chapter on Divine Transformations (Twenty-Eight Sections):**
He is the **Sovereign of the Vaulting Sky**, the **Exalted One of kalpas**,
possessing **wondrous vision and wondrous knowledge**,
unequaled, unmatched.
He is **profoundly still and purely true**, neither absent nor present,
the **supreme Sage and supreme Spirit**,
the **great divine transformation**,
the **treasure-house of light**,
the **great man** who **enlightens heaven and humanity**,
teaching without end,
with **great compassion and great mercy**,
rolling forth the **Law Wheel**.

For the sake of **delivering all beings**, he is called the **Jade Emperor**,
the **True Elder of the Vaulting Sky**,
**pure and clear**, **wise and eloquent**,
the **supreme Dao and supreme Sovereign**.

He opens the path for all beings—
thus, he emits this light.

At that time, the **Highest, Clear, and Illuminating Heavenly Sovereign**
finished his verse of praise and sat in silent stillness.

Wei Boyang said:
*"The Highest, Clear, and Illuminating Heavenly Sovereign extolled the Jade Emperor’s virtue—
not merely with ten lines of praise.
This Jade Emperor is the **august and solemn Sovereign of the Vaulting Sky**,
the **Exalted One of kalpas**.
All kalpas have their numbers—
whether billions or myriads—
yet none can truly be called ‘vast.’
The Jade Emperor has, from antiquity, been the **preceptor of the ten thousand heavens**,
enduring kalpas beyond count,
his breadth and depth beyond measure—
thus, he is the **Exalted One of kalpas**.

His radiance is without remainder,
his divine transformations wondrous and clear,
his penetration unobstructed,
his enlightenment profound and wondrous—
none can equal or compare to him.
He shines **purely luminous and profoundly still**,
**towering and unmoving**, yet **quiet and boundless**,
his Dao **true and unchanging**, **unstained and unsullied**,
his **virtue supremely pure**.
If he seems **vanished**, it is not true vanishing—
merely the **natural emptiness of the void**.
If he seems **present**, it is not clinging to existence—
merely the **wondrous non-duality of the formless**.
If he seems **both present and vanished**, it is **indescribable and beyond analysis**.

All **immortals, Buddhas, and gods** revere the Jade Emperor as the **supreme among Sages**.
No god’s **spiritual penetration** matches his.
He is the **supreme Mysterious Spirit**,
his transformations **sixfold and transcendent**, surpassing all.
Truly, he possesses **great divine transformation**,
his light **pervasive and enduring**,
pure and unstained, ever brighter, never dimmed—
the **true treasure-house of light**, storing boundless radiance.

None surpasses him in **supreme sovereignty**.
The Jade Emperor’s **Law is natural and spontaneous**,
vast and immeasurable, without end.
Truly, he is the **great man**—
the world’s **worthy ones** perfect their bodies and natures,
rectify themselves to rectify all,
encompassing heaven and earth.
Who among **great men** could surpass the Jade Emperor,
who **transforms heaven and earth**, gives birth to all things,
whose beginning is unseen and whose end is unknown?
He is the **most exalted among Sages**, the **greatest among gods**.
Which great man could rival him?

He **enlightens and transforms all beings and heavens**,
his teachings **perfect and his Dao revealed**—
without end.
His **compassion covers all things**, his **mercy pities all beings**—
boundless and without limit."*

The **great compassion and great mercy** are faithfully upheld,
and the **Law-wheel of transformation** shines ever-bright,
so that none are stagnant or concealed.

*"Huàn"* may also be read as *"zhuǎn"*—but that is too restrictive.

To **enlighten and deliver** all beings,
thus the title **"Jade Emperor"** is bestowed.

The **august and venerable Origin of the Azure Vault**—
divine, mysterious, and perfectly boundless—
**pure and pristine**, of **great wisdom and great insight**,
his **eloquence surpasses all measure**,
his **virtue/power** never exhausted,
his **transformative efficacy** never spent—
the **supreme Dao** is beyond quantification,
his **exalted sovereignty** unmatched.

Now he **enlightens and delivers** all beings,
thus he manifests the **great compassion and universal luminous virtue/power**.

At that time, the **High and Void Pure-Luminous Heavenly Sovereign** spoke this **gāthā** in praise,
then sat in **silent stillness**.

**My humble reflection**: The **original spirit** of the human body is the **Jade Emperor of the Highest Heaven**,
also called **True Sovereign**, **Mysterious Ancestor**, **Ancestral Reality**, **Heavenly Lord**, **Essence of Nature**, **Ancestral True Sovereign**, **Dharma-nature**, **Wondrous Luminous True Mind**, **Pure Nature**, **Playful Spirit**, **True Master**, **Playful Light**, **Great Staff**, **Dharma King**, **Wondrous Treasure**, **True Root**, **Buddha-nature**, **True Seed**, and **Elixir Origin**.

The **True Sovereign** of one’s being—
**divine, wondrous, and peerless**—
**luminous essence** without end,
**enlightening yin and yang**,
whose **spiritual intelligence** is beyond measure.

He **compassionately nurtures** all wonders,
**responds universally** with perfect clarity.

Most **exalted and noble**, his **transformative efficacy** is endless.
Silently merging with **refined qi**,
he **nurtures the true spirit**.

Thus, the **true light** occasionally reveals itself,
and the **wondrous mechanism** perpetually generates.

Those who truly grasp this
will **spontaneously produce the divine embryo**,
and share the **Jade Emperor’s merit and virtue/power**—
his **Dao-transformation** is boundless.

Only when one **affirms the Pure-Luminous Heavenly Sovereign’s gāthā** in praise of the Jade Emperor
does one attain **true knowledge and genuine awakening**.

Otherwise, the **true wondrousness** is unattained,
and the **Jade Emperor’s transformation** remains unrecognized.

The **Pure-Luminous gāthā**—
if recited as though in a dream,
how could one gain the **fruit of the scriptures**,
or attain **real benefit**?

Alas! The **Dao of Nature** resides within us—
the **true wondrousness** is self-sufficient.

If one **comprehends the wondrous luminous mechanism**,
then one truly **responds to and upholds the Jade Emperor’s radiant virtue/power**.

**Chapter Twenty-Nine on Divine Powers**

Thus, the **Heavenly Sovereign** again instructed the **Four Assemblies**:

"This **Jade Emperor’s body** is the **Dao-body** itself—
**not an ordinary form**.

This is the **body of boundless merit/virtue**,
the **body of pure and pristine naturalness**,
the **firmly luminous, unshakable true void, supreme Dharma-body**.

His **awe and spirit** are vast and profound,
his **name and reputation** spread universally—
no darkness escapes his illumination,
his **divine mystery** stands towering and majestic,
beyond all description.

**The Barefoot Immortal** said:
"The **Pure-Luminous Heavenly Sovereign** praised the Jade Emperor in a gāthā,
then sat in silent stillness once more.

At this moment, the **Originating Heavenly Sovereign** again instructed the **Four Assemblies** in the **Dharma-gathering**:

"This **Jade Emperor’s wondrous transformation** is the **Great Dao-body** itself—
**not an ordinary form**.

The **Dao** is formless—
how can one speak of a **body**?

Though the **Dao** is **void and formless**,
boundless and endless,
it **transforms all things**,
achieves the **beginning and end**,
stirring **yin and yang** without pause—
**true void yet with substantial essence**,
not merely empty.

The Jade Emperor’s **merit/virtue** is like the **void**,
his **spirit** aligns with the **Dao**,
thus it is said: *‘The Emperor’s body is the Dao-body—*
**not an ordinary form.’**

This is the **body of boundless merit/virtue**,
the **body of true purity and pristine naturalness**, unconstrained.

**Merit** has limits,
**virtue** has bounds—
how could they be **endless**?

The Jade Emperor **transforms all worlds**,
unchanged since ancient times—
where are the limits?

**Colored forms and images** are **constrained and stagnant**,
not **pure, pristine, and naturally free**.

The Jade Emperor is **never stained or attached**,
achieving **great ease and freedom**—
is this not **naturalness**?

This is the **divinely luminous, firm, and unyielding**,
the **true void that never decays**,
the **supreme, unmatched wondrous Dharma-body of transformation**.

All **manifested things** in the world will perish,
yet the **void** remains eternal.
The **perishing** are not **firm and unyielding**,
nor **divinely luminous**.

The **Great Void** exists,
and thus the **void** becomes **true reality**.

The Jade Emperor’s **spirit and penetration** endure through all ages unharmed,
his **playful light** shines across **kalpas** undimmed—
not only **most divine and luminous**,
but **firm as unpolished jade**,
**unbreakable as the void itself**,
**never destroyed**, **eternally unshaken**.

This is the **abiding true void**,
the **unscattered wondrous essence**,
the **supreme, peerless wondrous Dharma-body**.

His **awe and virtue/power**, his **spiritual radiance**—
how could they be **easily fathomed or explored**?
Vast and magnanimous,
boundless and great—
his **name and reputation** are beyond thought,
**pervading and filling** all ten directions.

His **light illuminates** even the finest dust,
no darkness escapes his gaze.

His **divine powers** are **mysterious and profound**,
towering and immeasurable,
**resounding yet nameless**,
beyond all description.

**My humble reflection**: The **human nature’s luminous spirit**—
**divine, mysterious, and self-sufficient**—
the **Three Bodies** are complete,
the **Four Wisdoms** are fulfilled.
The **vast and sincere qi**,
the **true and singular essence**—
all **ten thousand goods and wonders**,
what is not possessed?

Truly, in this **humble body**,
the **Three Noble Positions** are **fulfilled**,
and the **Four Great Responsibilities** are **accomplished**—
no **questions** or **rest** can be attained.

Its **origin is not ordinary**—
it is the **Dao-body**,
the **body of boundless merit/virtue**,
the **body of pure and pristine naturalness**,
the **firmly luminous, unshakable true void, supreme Dharma-body**.

Yet **common people** indulge recklessly,
**wasting this body** in vain.
Their **hearts burdened**, their **spirits exhausted**,
their **essence drained**, their **qi scattered**,
the **Dao of Nature** remains **unclear**.

Who could **grasp the vital essence**,
or **comprehend the Dao’s core**—
lost in **illusory forms**, their **void exhausted**,
they **fritter away this life**,
existence and annihilation like a dream—
**nothing known**, **nothing understood**,
how could they **attain transformation**?

Some **claim to exhaust divine virtue/power** in perfecting nature,
yet they **do not ultimately preserve** their attainment.

Thus, **people cannot exhaust the spirit** to **attain transformation**,
nor **return to the void** to become **immortal**,
nor **merge with the Dao** to realize **true reality**.

Only the **name of supreme sovereignty** is **never destroyed**—
the Jade Emperor, who **takes the Dao as his body**,
whose **merit/virtue** is **boundless**,
whose **nature is pure and pristine**,
whose **spirit is firmly luminous**,
whose **true void never decays**,
whose **supreme Dharma-body** stands **unmatched**.

For those **first entering the sacred stream**,
who have **not yet crossed the single barrier**,
who **observe yet do not penetrate**,
whose **words remain unawakened**,
whose **thoughts do not align with life and death**,
who **do not know** the **spirit’s source of divinity**,
whose **studies fail to harmonize** with **heaven and humanity**,
who **do not know** the **transformation’s essence**—
they **abandon themselves to the Dao’s ineffability**,
hoping to **glimpse** the **mysterious and profound**,
seeking the **noble scholars** of **void and luminosity**.

「The Primordial Sage takes pity on sentient beings’ long-standing delusion,
and proclaims the **virtue/power** of the Sovereign’s boundless reach,
fully awakening the deaf and blind of all worldly ages,
to manifest the **mysterious and profound** efficacy of **divine transformation**—
truly great in **compassion** and deep in **benevolence**,
desiring sentient beings to enter **perfection**,
also expanding His **awe-inspiring and spiritual** might,
pervading His **renown**,
illuminating the **profound and hidden**,
**divine and wondrous**, **majestic and unshakable**,
whose **virtue** defies **naming**.
This is the **Great Wish** of the **Celestial Sovereign**.
Yet, the realm of the world drifts in chaos,
and human hearts sink in **mire**,
unable to follow the **Celestial Sovereign’s** ordinances—
how could they **bear** the Primordial Sage’s instructions?

Alas, the **principle** unites **heaven and humanity**,
and the **sage and the common** share the same **heart**—
yet they cannot **aspire to sainthood** or **heavenly transcendence**.
The **Dao/Way** unfolds **naturally**,
and to fail here is to **fall short** of the **true scriptures**,
the **great Dao/Way**,
the **parental origins**,
and the **living body** itself.
This is the **will of the enlightened**.

The **Thirty Chapters of Divine Perfections**—
this is the **Celestial Sovereign**, not **dependent** on **merit/virtue** cultivated through **deliberate actions**.
Though the **Celestial Sovereign** once descended into the mortal realm,
spanning countless **eons** to **manifest teachings**,
demonstrating **great divine powers**,
His **body remains pure and pristine**—
never ceasing to **abide in the Golden Palace**,
**dividing His form** across the **ten directions**,
**adapting His presence** to each realm,
**benefiting all sentient beings**,
**elevating them to the Dao/Way’s shore**,
**universally bestowing** the **teachings and methods**,
**awakening successors**—
if they **follow the instructions** and **practice diligently**,
they may **ascend to the highest truth** and **fulfill the great Dao/Way**.

By these **supreme and wondrous** **merit/virtue** and **efficacy**,
His **radiance** perpetually **fills all the heavens**,
His **divine wisdom** **reaches beyond measure**,
**ineffable and transcendent**.
The **Wondrous Conduct True Person** says:
This **Celestial Sovereign**—
**divine and wondrous**, **majestic and unshakable**,
whose **virtue** defies **naming**—
is not **dependent** on **deliberate actions** or **merit/virtue** cultivated through **strenuous effort**.
In the past, though He **descended** to **receive birth** among mortals,
spanning countless **eons** to **broadly manifest teachings**,
displaying **great divine powers**,
His **manifestation**—
like **abandoning kingship** to **practice**, severing **affection** to **seek the Dao/Way**,
administering **medicine** to **heal illnesses**, expounding **teachings** and **propagating transformation**,
**enduring suffering** and **delighting in renunciation**—
attained the **rank of Golden Immortal**,
and **taught Bodhisattvas** across **many eons**.

Thus, the **scriptures of liberation** record the **cause and effect** of **Buddhas and living beings**,
saying that from **Tushita Heaven**,
He **rode the fragrant elephant** and **descended** into the **womb of Maya**,
thereby giving birth to **the Sage of the World**.
This too is but one **manifestation** of the **Celestial Sovereign’s** **adaptive teachings**.

Elsewhere, He **attended the assembly of the floating lotus**,
**presided over the gathering of the precious pearl**,
**transformed into the form of common folk**,
**transformed into the form of Dao/Way-seekers**,
**responding to encounters** with **spiritual efficacy**,
**universally liberating without ceasing**,
**acting as sovereign** of all **heavenly realms**,
His **divine powers** **beyond measure**.
Though He **manifested teachings** across countless **eons**,
displaying **great divine powers**,
His **Dharma-body** remains **pure and pristine**,
**majestic and unshakable**—
never ceasing to **abide in the Golden Palace**.
When the Primordial Sage was about to **proclaim the Jade Scripture**,
the **Celestial Sovereign** **emitted great radiance**,
**dividing His form** to **pervade the ten directions**,
filling all **great heavenly palaces**.
In every **world**—
**upper heavens**, **lower earths**, **mortal realms**—
all **beheld** His **radiance**,
each **received benefits**,
all **found joy**,
and **heard the Great Vehicle**.

This **dividing of His form** and **adaptive manifestation**,
**benefiting all sentient beings**,
**elevating them to the Dao/Way’s shore**,
**universally bestowing** the **teachings and methods**,
**awakening successors**—
if they **follow the instructions** and **revere the Sovereign’s commands**,
they may **ascend to the highest truth** and **fulfill the great Dao/Way**.
The **Celestial Sovereign**, relying on these **supreme and wondrous** **merit/virtue** and **efficacy**,
thus **emits radiance** that perpetually **fills all the heavens**,
His **divine wisdom** **reaches beyond measure**,
**ineffable and transcendent**.
The **Great Radiance** is not merely so—
His **virtue** is **vast**, and His **radiance** is **wondrous**.
The **divine wisdom** **reaches beyond measure**—
His **divine intelligence** is **wondrous**, and His **Dao/Way** is **manifest**.
Thus, it is clear that the **Celestial Sovereign** is not **dependent** on **merit/virtue** cultivated through **deliberate actions**.

I **reflect**: the **primordial spirit** of humanity
remains **vast and unchanging** as the **eons**,
its **divine radiance** **wondrous and profound**—
how could it be **named** by **words**?
Much less could it **arise** from **actions of the heart**!

**Perception, hearing, awareness, and knowledge**—
**actions of standing, sitting, or lying down**,
**eating, breathing, speaking, or remaining silent**,
**responding to stimuli** with **effortless grace**—
though **adapting to circumstances** with **wondrous efficacy**,
its **pure and pristine** **essence** never **abandons the Golden Palace**,
**congealing** into the **mysterious and profound** **spiritual embryo**,
while **true and real** as it is,
never **departing** from itself.
**Thousands, hundreds of millions of transformations**,
**adapting to each realm** to **benefit all**,
**giving birth** to **ascension on the Dao/Way’s shore**,
**broadly proclaiming** the **spiritual treasury**,
**awakening the later heavens**.
**Guarding secrets** and **holding fast to truth**,
**transcending the common** to **attain sainthood**,
**all transformations** **fulfilled**,
**no fruit** **left unattained**.
By this **wondrous conduct**,
a **single glimmer** of **mysterious radiance** suffuses all,
**beyond measure**—
the **Dao/Way’s efficacy** is **strange and verified**,
how could it be **calculated or quantified**?

To **observe** the **Celestial Sovereign’s** **saintly virtue** and **divine efficacy**,
**independent of cultivation** and **beyond measure**—
are there not **many instances** of this?

Though **attaining true nature** may be **uniform**,
those who **recklessly abandon** it are **countless**,
allowing the **pure and pristine** **true nature** to be **obscured by lust and delusion**,
like **dust burying a bright mirror**,
so that **radiance** does not **shine**,
and **beauty and ugliness** go **unseen**,
while **wondrous intent** **fails to manifest**.
Yet, if **dust is scraped away** and **radiance polished daily**,
**new and ever-growing**,
**responding to stimuli without effort**,
**true reality** **abides freely**—
in the **Golden Palace** and **Purple Realm**,
the **primordial spirit** **dwells eternally**.
**Ever-responsive, ever-still**,
**undisturbed by anything**.
In **wondrous discernment**, it **unifies all** with **one thread**,
and in **manifest actions**, it **follows naturally** without **emotion**.
**Great compassion** and **great benevolence**—
His **wondrous intent** **never wanes**,
**all transformations** **radiant and profound**,
**beyond enumeration**.
His **cultivation** is **boundless**,
His **true radiance** **universally pervades**,
His **merit/virtue** **beyond conception**—
ah!

This is the **inherent nature** of **Dao/Way-practitioners**,
not **dependent** on **deliberate actions**,
nor **achievable** by **stubborn emptiness**.
It is **both present and absent**—
**neither having nor not having**.
The **good scholar** **embodies** it.

The **Thirty-First Chapter of Divine Perfections**—
**this is the radiance of His body**,
all **possessing wondrous names**.
The **Great Divine Perfections Radiance**—
the **Great Compassionate Radiance**,
the **Great Joyous Renunciation Radiance**,
the **Great Enduring Suffering Radiance**,
the **Great Equanimous Radiance**,
the **Great Gentle Harmony Radiance**,
the **Great Autonomous Radiance**,
the **Great Beneficial Radiance**,
the **Great Wish-Fulfilling Radiance**,
the **Great Wisdom Radiance**,
the **Great Auspicious Radiance**,
the **Great Liberation Radiance**,
the **Great Refuge Radiance**,
the **Great Merit/Virtue Radiance**,
the **Great Perfect Radiance**,
the **Great Unobstructed Radiance**,
the **Radiance No One Can Surpass**.
The **Great Wisdom True Person** says:
All the **great radiance** **emitted** by the **Celestial Sovereign’s** **body**
**possesses supreme and wondrous names**.」

The **Great Radiance** names are thus: the **Great God-Transcending Radiance**, the **Great Compassionate Radiance**, the **Great Joyous Renunciation Radiance**, the **Great Enduring Suffering Radiance**, the **Great Equanimous Radiance**, the **Great Gentle Harmony Radiance**, the **Great Autonomous Radiance**, the **Great Beneficial Radiance**, the **Great Wish-Fulfilling Radiance**, the **Great Wisdom Radiance**, the **Great Auspicious Radiance**, the **Great Liberation Radiance**, the **Great Refuge Radiance**, the **Great Virtue/Power Radiance**, the **Great Perfect Radiance**, the **Great Unobstructed Radiance**, and the **Radiance No One Can Surpass**—these are the seventeen great radiance lights.

The **Celestial Sovereign** universally extends and illuminates all things, with wondrous deeds and accumulated proofs, possessing great **virtue/power** and **qi** and attaining the six **god-transcending** abilities. The **Great God-Transcending Radiance** is resplendent, pervading all. This is the first radiance name.

Next, the **Celestial Sovereign** possesses great compassion and great pity; compassion and pity are boundless, and the radiance is wondrous and vast. The **Great Compassionate Radiance** is the second.

Again, the **Celestial Sovereign** truly rejoices in renunciation; renunciation is boundless, and the wondrous radiance universally shines. The **Great Joyous Renunciation Radiance** is the third.

The **Celestial Sovereign** has endured great suffering through countless eons; endurance is limitless, and the radiance is unceasing, with no obstruction. The **Great Enduring Suffering Radiance** is the fourth.

The **Celestial Sovereign** has practiced great equanimity in the past; equanimity is unending, and the radiance is unassailable. The **Great Equanimous Radiance** is the fifth.

In past eons, the **Celestial Sovereign** has also cultivated great gentle harmony; gentle and yielding, yet tranquil and harmonious, this vast **Dao/Way** never alters, and the radiance pervades all, inexhaustible. The **Great Gentle Harmony Radiance** is the sixth.

The **Celestial Sovereign’s** **virtue/power** is serene and unchanging, transcending all and autonomous. The radiance is vast and boundless, with no end. The **Great Autonomous Radiance** is the seventh.

The **Celestial Sovereign’s** benevolence is boundless, encompassing all and benefiting them eternally; the benefits are endless, and the law’s radiance universally illuminates. The **Great Beneficial Radiance** is the eighth.

The **Celestial Sovereign’s** body transcends all proofs and attains wondrous awakening, pure and natural. The **Celestial Sovereign** is the **Dharma King** of the **Buddha’s** coming, and after countless eons of cultivation, the **Celestial Sovereign** attains this station. Thus, the greatest **virtue/power** emerges from the mindless, and **god-transcending** transformations align with wishes. The **Great Wish-Fulfilling Radiance** is the ninth.

The **Celestial Sovereign** possesses great wisdom and great **palpitating insight** (大慧). Wisdom and insight surpass all kinds, and the radiance is peerless. The **Great Wisdom Radiance** is the tenth.

The **Celestial Sovereign** is fundamentally the most exalted goodness, forever auspicious. With this radiance, all is illuminated without cessation. The **Great Auspicious Radiance** is the eleventh.

The **Celestial Sovereign** has long understood and attained great liberation; liberation is natural and unconstrained, and the golden radiance endures. The **Great Liberation Radiance** is the twelfth.

The **Celestial Sovereign** aligns with the **Great Dao/Way**, and the wondrous law is natural and unchanging. The **Celestial Sovereign** has maintained true faith through countless eons, never generating doubt or regression. All beings in the ten directions and future ages universally revere and submit to this eternal radiance, never dimming. The **Great Refuge Radiance** is the thirteenth.

The **Celestial Sovereign** universally saves all beings without exception, with **virtue/power** most vast, and the radiance shines eternally without depletion. The **Great Virtue/Power Radiance** is the fourteenth.

With **virtue/power** complete and the **Dao/Way** fulfilled, the **Celestial Sovereign’s** **virtue/power** is perfect, and the radiance endures forever in splendor. The **Great Perfect Radiance** is the fifteenth.

Though stained by dust, the **Celestial Sovereign** is inherently pure; **god-transcending** transformations are complete and radiant, and the **Celestial Sovereign’s** **virtue/power** shines eternally without obstruction. The **Great Unobstructed Radiance** is the sixteenth.

Among **god-transcending** beings, this is the most noble; among sages, this is the most revered. The **Celestial Sovereign** is the master of all heavens, the teacher of all **Buddhas**, and no being in the vast **Dao/Way** of the **Dharma Realm** can compare to the **Celestial Sovereign**. Therefore, the radiance perpetually fills all realms, and the **god-transcending** transformations are beyond measure. Is not the **Radiance No One Can Surpass** the seventeenth great radiance?

As for these seventeen great radiance lights of **god-transcending** and wondrous meaning, only the **Celestial Sovereign** of today can truly perceive them. How can **god-transcending** beings measure this?

The fool notes: In the mortal world, upright nature is the root. Therefore, the **Dao/Way** of immortals is actualized, with this as the **Great Radiance** seed. Yet though all true seeds are possessed, none preserve them. Thus, in the field of delusion, one must cultivate and purify the **karma** of causes and conditions.

Therefore, there is one kind of supreme excellent cause, and there is one level of **god-transcending** and wondrous radiance. The **Celestial Sovereign** has cultivated countless wondrous deeds, which are beyond measure. Why speak of seventeen great radiance lights? It is because the **Dao/Way** is profound and difficult to comprehend, and the transformations are intricate, making the **Dao/Way** dim.

The **Celestial Sovereign’s** seventeen radiance lights are like the **Buddha’s** manifestation of the **Dharmakāya** (丈六身), with the crown emitting the **Great Auspicious Radiance**. Moreover, the **Celestial Sovereign’s** radiance is supremely wondrous, transcending all kinds. Who can trace the wondrous deeds or recognize the seventeen great meanings?

Alas, this is rare and difficult to attain! The **Dao/Way** is inherently within oneself; neglect leads to dimness, while diligence brings clarity. Cultivate the **Way** of **non-action** (无为) with steadfast effort, and do not seek swift **god-transcending** transformations. The **Dao/Way** will naturally be obtained.

Thus, the thirty-second chapter of the **God-Transcending** section states: Therefore, you mortals who desire to see the **Celestial Sovereign** yet cannot do so, it is because you still cling to the **body** and **mouth** (身口), failing to abandon your **karmic habits** (结习). Your **afflictions** and deeds are ever-present.

Because of these obstructions, you cannot behold the **Celestial Sovereign’s** compassionate visage. Now, I proclaim the **Dharma** of breaking through these obstructions for you, the assembly of the **Dharma**. You, the great assembly, should each earnestly follow this.

At that time, all the great assembly rejoiced and leapt for joy, bowing their heads before the **Highest Venerable One** (至尊) and the **mortal** (凡) alike, all desiring to hear the teachings.

The **Thunder Sage** (雷师), **Bright Old Man** (皓翁), said: The **Celestial Sovereign** emits seventeen great radiance lights, transcending all measure. Therefore, you lofty, pure, and clear **Celestial Sovereigns** and **masters of the heavens** (高虚清明天主等), who desire to truly see the **Celestial Sovereign** yet cannot do so, it is because though you have no dusty stains, you have not yet attained the station of the **Celestial Sovereign**. The **Great Vehicle** (大乘) of supreme wondrousness has not been truly understood.

You still cling to the **body** and **mouth** (身口), failing to abandon **karmic habits** from countless eons, **ignorance** and **afflictions**, **mortal** deeds and transgressions. Because of these obstructions, you cannot behold the **Celestial Sovereign’s** compassionate visage.

**Karmic habits** (结习), **emotional desires**, and dusty **mortal** things: all delusions and entanglements are fundamentally not to be coveted. Yet due to insufficient wisdom and excessive attachment to thoughts, the rise of perceptions leads to gradual staining and clinging. Interacting with things and beings, these entanglements grow ever deeper, forming **karmic toxins** (结毒) that solidify into **habits** (习气).

Like a man binding himself with ropes, it is difficult to untangle in a moment. Deep-rooted **karmic habits** and past stains are hard to remove once they have taken hold. The **karmic seeds** and **roots of deeds** are inherently impure; clinging to **mortal** desires may either harbor **afflictions** or accumulate transgressions, or plant **karmic seeds**, entangling one in endless **karma**, restless and chaotic. The **afflictions** and disturbances have not yet been dispelled, and the **karmic deeds** of past lives continue to obstruct.

Even though you govern the **Brahma realms** (梵天), you have not yet attained ultimate clarity, nor do you fully comprehend the **Heavenly Mysteries** (重玄). How could you then behold the most supreme **Celestial Sovereign**? This is why you cannot see the **Celestial Sovereign**.

Now I proclaim to you, the gathered assembly, the method for cutting through and removing obstructions. You, the great assembly, should each uphold and practice it with sincerity.

At that time, the great assembly, overcome with joy and exultation, all knelt before the **Celestial Sovereign’s** jade case, bowing their heads and prostrating, reverently offering their respects, all desiring to hear the secret discourse on dispelling obstructions.

*"I"* refers to **Primordial Beginning** (元始), *"case"* (几) means *"table."* A note: From birth, each has inherent predispositions. Though the **Great Cycle** (元会) begins anew and the **Great Harmony qi** (太和之气) flows, the accumulated habits of past eons are not easily forgotten. Thus, the scriptures liken predestined **karmic affinities** to accumulated toxins—a true insight.

Therefore, those with **affinities for joy** will find kindred hearts across distant realms, while those bound by **malevolent affinities** may stand face-to-face yet remain a thousand miles apart. Do not dismiss the *Dao Canon*’s **functional frameworks** or Buddhist scriptural records as heretical—even in Confucian texts, Yan Ying’s opposition to Confucius was later attributed to **fate’s decree**. The great scholars Cheng Yi and Su Shi split into the **Shu** and **Lu factions**, another case of **incompatible affinities**. Yet even those who must rely on one another often meet with estrangement—a lament shared across ages. Can the doctrine of **affinities** then be entirely discarded?

Thus, the **Ten Perceptions** are inexhaustible, the **Five Aggregates** unfathomable, the **Thirteen Disciples** and **Twenty-Five Magical Seeds** endless, the **Seven False and Three True** transformations intricate—who can easily escape them all?

The **Celestial Sovereign**, having attained the **Pure and Bright Heavenly Lord’s** imperial throne, though freed from earthly defilements, still bears the **accumulated karma of past kalpas**, not yet fully transcended. His essence lingers in the **lofty void**, known as **Pure and Bright**. Past virtuous causes remain untouched by the **void’s embrace**. How could one who embodies **Void-Luminous Perfection** like the **Celestial Sovereign** be seen at once?

The Buddhist scriptures note that even **Bodhisattvas**, in their practice, may see the face of the **Tathāgata** yet fail to truly behold him. When the **Dharma-body Buddha** expounds the **supreme truth**, the Bodhisattvas listen in silence—this is the same principle. The **Most Sage** is not easily seen; the obstructions of **body and speech habits** are not easily dispelled.

Yet this truth is most difficult to grasp. To *"see"* the **Celestial Sovereign** is not to see him with the eyes; to **comprehend** his **Way** is to **penetrate** his **virtue**. As in Confucius’ door—those who truly receive the **Master’s transmission of the heart-mind**, one in essence—though times and worlds differ, the principle remains the same. **Spiritual communion** and **heart-meeting** alone yield true vision.

Even **Yan Hui**, the bright and discerning disciple, failed to grasp the **subtle interval**; how then could the **Pure and Bright Heavenly Lord** see the **Celestial Sovereign**, and why doubt it?

The **Primordial Beginning’s** method of **breaking through obstructions** lies in **luminous predestined practice**, **penetrating the heart’s essence**, and **repelling and harmonizing**—once the outer obstructions dissolve, the **Celestial Sovereign** is seen. Thus, the assembly longs to hear it.

Alas! Obstructions arise from the heart; breaking them depends on the **self**. The **Great Unimpeded Way** is within your **original spirit**—do not grow weary in crossing. **Coarse traces of speech and hearing** should not become hindrances. Is the **Great Dao** not within you? Strive onward.

**Chapter Thirty-Three: The Perfection of Spiritual Penetration**
The **Celestial Worthy** spoke: *"The method of cutting through obstructions lies in generating **great wisdom**, free from doubt, free from **greed and anger**, free from **lustful desires**, free from **envy and jealousy**, free from **harm and killing**, free from **mundane emotions**, free from **mundane thoughts**, free from **delusion and filth**, free from **sounds and colors**, free from **right and wrong**, free from **hatred and love**, free from **discrimination**, free from **arrogance**, free from **attachment**."*

**Master Guangcheng** said: *"The **Primordial Beginning Celestial Worthy**, responding to the Pure Assembly’s request for the **mystery of unobstructed perfection**, spoke thus: To cut through obstructions and behold the **Celestial Sovereign’s** wondrous transformation and luminous visage, the **Way** is none other than generating **divine wisdom and great enlightenment**, firmly believing in the **True Path**, free from **doubt, wavering, and confusion**. The **Great Dao** is supremely upright; **True Unity** admits no duality—there is nothing to doubt or confuse.

If **clarity** is insufficient to discern the **subtle signs**, one may cling to **contradictory extremes**, lacking steadfast vision, and **demonic knowledge** seizes the opportunity. Once one knows the **Great Dao** resides within, **knowing and guarding firmly**, do not waver with **duality**, nor mix with **triplicity**—what more is there to doubt? Without doubt, there is no confusion; the **Dao** can be entered.

Thus, the **great wisdom** that cuts through obstructions and purifies **accumulated habits** must first be free from doubt. Seekers of the **Way** must not measure progress by **worldly gains**, nor rely on external means. **Anger, resentment, indignation, and grievance** must all be abandoned.

The second obstruction to cut: **greed and anger**. Let the mind be **single-minded in the Dao**; its sincerity will follow naturally. **Nurturing private desires** and **wandering thoughts** easily arise—even a hair’s breadth of **lewd indulgence or craving** greatly disturbs the **True**.

The third obstruction: **lustful desires**. The **Dao** encompasses all; the **virtuous and unworthy** are both my teachers. If you harbor the slightest **resentment toward the capable** or **disdain for the foolish**, it is a grave error.

The fourth obstruction: **envy and jealousy**. The **Great Dao** is supremely compassionate, **unbearingly tolerant**. If, out of **hostility or malice**, you nurture **destructive intentions**, you stray far from the **Way**.

The fifth obstruction: **harm and killing**. Though the *Yin-Xing Classic* speaks of **"killing the mechanism"**, it means subduing **evil demons** so that **ultimate truth** may act freely. As in **autumn’s killing frost**, when plants return to the roots and **life’s vitality withdraws**, one sees the **compassion of Heaven and Earth**—this is not the **world’s** notion of killing. It is also said: *"Harm gives rise to kindness."* This reflects the **mind-intent of Heaven and Earth**, not the **world’s** notion of harm.

The **Great Dao** acts without action; **emotions and perceptions** are not employed. A single **mundane impulse** leads to boundless error.

The sixth obstruction: **mundane emotions**. The **Dao’s intent** requires **pure thoughts**. Any **dust-thought** brings boundless ruin.

The seventh obstruction: **mundane thoughts**. The **Dao** is **unblemished purity**; the slightest **delusion or filth** betrays the **ultimate truth**.

The eighth obstruction: **sounds and colors**. To seek the **Dao** through them is to distance oneself from it. Those who embody the **Dao** do not merely avoid **external sounds and colors**—they remain untouched by the **world**, standing beyond the **Dao’s ripples and shores**, seeking and clinging to nothing.

The ninth obstruction to be severed: **no arising of sounds and colors**.

The **Dao** is **Great Unity** in its essence. The slightest affirmation or negation betrays its **original true nature**.

The tenth obstruction: **no arising of right and wrong**. Though Mencius says, *"The mind of right and wrong, all people possess,"*—**great wisdom** is like **foolishness**; why would one cling to distinctions of right and wrong?

The **Dao** knows no preference or rejection. Love or hatred obstructs the **true**.

The eleventh obstruction: **no arising of hatred or love**. The **principle** is **without duality**; applying **discriminating intelligence** is not the **Dao**.

The twelfth method of severing obstructions: **no arising of distinctions**. Seeing the **Dao** clearly, transcending the **mundane**, disdaining worldly affairs—**arrogance** greatly violates the **Way**.

The thirteenth method of severing obstructions: **no arising of prideful or contemptuous thoughts**.

The **Dao** is **lively and boundless**; its **ultimate essence** cannot be grasped. Severing the thirteen obstructions, the **Dao** is attained. Though called *"attainment of the Dao,"* in truth, there is nothing to attain. If one clings to any **fixed possession**, the **principle** remains obstructed, bound by **dharma**.

The fourteenth and final method of severing obstructions: **no arising of attachment**.

**My humble reflection**: The **Dao** in humanity is **innately unobstructed**. Only when **worldly affairs and discriminating thoughts** veil it does one lose the **Way**. Thus, the **Primordial Origin** compassionately instructs the *Gate of Severing Obstructions* to the **Pure Assembly**, enumerating all obstacles, urging all to **resolutely aspire** and not be hindered by difficulties. To break free from **worldly obstructions** and transcend **dharma’s confines**, then the **Jade Emperor’s divine radiance** will reveal itself—**my wondrous essence** will shine forth, and **Yue** will see it clearly. Though so, severing these two obstructions opens the **Dao’s gate**. The **Divine Transformation** and **Mysterious Depths** are yet to be expounded in later teachings.

**Chapter on the Divine Passages (34th Chapter)**:
Concentrate the **divine essence**, clarify the **thoughts**—all **spirits** are subdued. The **heart** becomes **Primordial Void**, **inner and outer** untainted and pure, containing all without exclusion, accepting all without reservation. Do not allow **external evils** to disturb your **Supreme Dao**, drag you away from the **True Principle**, ruin your **numinous root**, or steal your **Ultimate Treasure**, lest you fall into **endless mundane existence**, trapped in the **world’s net**, assailed by **ten thousand demons**, and for **hundreds of thousands of kalpas** hear no **wondrous dharma**, while **ghosts and spirits** seize the chance to condemn you, from birth into death.

Thus, you must **resolutely cultivate**, safeguard the **True Principle**, and never let it be lost. As previously stated, all these obstructions must be **severed by you**. With **body pure and thoughts clear**, you transcend all **difficulties**—this is the **Dao’s Treasure**, the **pillar of upholding the Law**.

Liu Haichan says: *"The Primordial Origin teaches the method of severing obstructions; it generates **great wisdom** and cuts off the **fourteen paths of karmic inclination**."* What is its **ultimate fruition**?

Severing obstructions and removing veils, **divine clarity** and **pure thoughts** arise. **Silently dwell** in the **Primordial Spirit** and **Mysterious Origin**, **concentrate the Primordial Spirit**, and **clarify all thoughts**—all **spirits** harmonize and **submerge**. The **heart** is like **endless void**, **inner and outer** steadfast, pure, and white. All **mundane dharmas** and **living beings** are contained without limit, embraced without exclusion.

Moreover, **fix the vision and guard it firmly**, never wavering—do not let **external evils** confuse your **Supreme Rectitude** and **Great Dao**, nor drag you away from the **True Primordial Principle**, lest you ruin your **Ultimate Numinous Root**, steal your **inherent, unshareable, indestructible Treasure**, and cause you to **accumulate kalpas** in **endless mundane existence**, sinking deep into the **net of worldly dust**, with **demonic afflictions** relentlessly assaulting you. For **hundreds of thousands of kalpas**, you will be ensnared by **demonic deeds**, hearing no **Supreme True Wondrous Law**, while **ghosts and spirits** seize the opportunity to **condemn and slay** you, from birth into death.

Thus, you **Law Assembly** must **sincerely resolve**, **self-protect the innate True Principle**, and never let it be **lost or abandoned**. As previously stated, all **doubts and obstructions** must be **exterminated and severed**. The **fourteen obstructions**, including **external evils**, **birth and death**, and **mundane inclinations**, are all encompassed within.

Once all obstructions are **severed and cut off**, the **body attains true purity and clarity**, transcending the **three realms’ karmic cycles** and **sufferings**. This is the **method of severing obstructions**—the **Dao’s Ultimate Treasure**, the **great pillar supporting the True Law**.

Temples, halls, pagodas, palaces, gates, and dwellings—without **pillars and beams**, their construction is difficult. Cultivating the **Dao** to **perfection**, entering **sainthood** and transcending **mundanity**—without **severing obstructions**, liberation is impossible. Severing all obstructions ensures **eternal freedom from ruin**, and the **True Law** flourishes.

Thus, the **Celestial Sovereign** regards **severing obstructions** as the **pillar upholding the Law**.

**My humble reflection**: Humanity’s **inherent true nature** and **Primordial Spirit** are **pure and untainted**, **unbroken through kalpas**, naturally **serene and content**, and **never cease to be luminous**, undivided from **sainthood and truth**. If **clarity** persists without end, how could the **Jade Emperor’s divine transformation** and **wondrous light** not be **witnessed clearly**?

Yet, **thoughts** cling to the **heart**, perpetuating and unchanging. Those who **slightly understand the Dao** still hope for **rapid results**, so **deep-seated habits** linger, **afflictions** persist, and the **Imperial Light** remains unseen. If **true enlightenment** and **mysterious penetration** are **perfectly achieved**, the **ultimate fruit** is **unshakable**—knowing **nature and life** as **true**, recognizing **all things** as **illusionary**, one **sees the Dao** and **forgets things**, then **walks the Dao** and **forgets people**, **attains the Dao** and **forgets self**, **completes the Dao** and **forgets the heart**, and **delights in the Dao** and **forgets inclinations**.

Then, **forgetting forgets to forget the true**, **affairs and principles merge**, **true and false are both abandoned**, neither clinging to **sainthood nor mundanity**, nor needing **five ranks of masters and disciples**. **Attainment without attainment**, **guardianship without clinging**, **emptiness yet not empty**, **not divine yet divine**—then **ancient habits are purified**, **accumulated karmas vanish**, **subtle defilements are extinguished**, and one **enters the Supreme**. No longer **drifting in silence** toward the **Celestial Emperor**, sharing **divine essence**; no longer **ringing the bell** of the **Dao’s natural law**, merging with **true principle**—what need is there for **three vehicles** or **all teachings**? The **most exalted in sainthood**, whose **virtues** are **unparalleled**?

All can **achieve it**—only the **purity of root and dust**, the **perfection of mysterious practice**, and the **wondrousness of effortless action** matter. **No doing, no questioning**.

「The rigid and false cannot truly escape; yet the fusion is not yet complete, nor the transformation divine—still, one has not fully attained sainthood. Only those who have transcended the **Daoist** *Xuanzhong* **Earthly Immortal**, the **Buddhist** *Phosat* **Bodhisattva**, and the **Confucian** *Daxian* **Great Sage** and above can achieve this.

Now, mortals seeking the **Dao/Way**, still adhere to the **Most Exalted in Sainthood** (至聖), not deeming the **Great Vehicle** (大乘) as sufficient. In the **Thirty-Fifth Chapter of Divine Powers** (神通品三十五章), you must further cultivate and revere this sacred text, as if standing before the **Celestial Emperor** (玉皇尊帝). Nurture a heart of reverence and awe, focus your contemplation on the **Emperor’s Noble Form** (尊容), and proclaim the **Emperor’s Glorious Titles** (尊號). Only then will you behold the **Compassionate Face** (慈颜), all receive the **Emperor’s Protection and Liberation** (護度), universally hear the **Wondrous Law** (妙法), and personally offer **Devoted Reverence and Sustenance** (祗奉供養), forever free from **rebirth’s cycles** (輪轉).

**Eastern Hua Wood Official** (东华木公) declared: *"The **Primordial Beginning** (元始) revealed to the multitudes the Law of Severing Obstacles (断障之法), which, being called the **Dao/Way’s Treasure** (道寶) and the **Pillar of the Law** (持法栋梁), was further demonstrated to all as the **Enduring Practice and Devotion** (持久服膺之義). You, the **Pure Assembly** (清眾), having heard the **True Teaching** (正法) today, must further uphold and revere this *Jade Emperor’s Original Conduct Scripture* (《玉皇本行經》). By personally reciting this scripture, you stand near the **Jade Emperor’s Noble Sovereign** (玉皇尊帝), generating a heart of **reverence and safeguarding** (尊敬保重).

Knowing the **Noble Scripture** (尊經) prevents profaning the **Dao’s Natural Law** (天道); honoring the **Scripture** (重經) prevents belittling the **Dao’s Treasure** (天寶). Eternal reverence ensures no **disrespect or negligence** (悖慢), and the **Great Dao/Way** is naturally attained.

This aligns with the *Analects* (《論語》) saying: *"Revere the **Heavenly Mandate** (天命), and revere the words of the **Sage** (聖人)."* Yet, to stand near the **Emperor** (是帝) is not to truly behold the **Celestial Sovereign** (玉帝); if one cannot yet **cross over and meet** (對越) the **Emperor**, then one cannot yet generate **true reverence** (尊重).

Focusing one’s attention and contemplating the **Emperor’s Noble Form and Wondrous Aspect** (尊容妙相) is not merely an act of **imagination** (想像). It is as if the **Emperor** were truly present—then, **devotedly serving the Celestial Sovereign** (昭事上帝), one **unites in virtue with Heaven and Earth** (與天地合德) and becomes the **Most Exalted in Sainthood** (至聖).

By proclaiming and extolling the **Emperor’s Most Noble Titles** (至尊徽號), you will behold the **Celestial Sovereign’s Great Compassionate Radiance** (玉帝大慈光颜), all receiving the **Emperor’s Protection and Liberation** (護持拔度), universally hearing the **Supreme True Wondrous Law** (無上至真妙法), and personally offering **Devoted Reverence and Sustenance** (祗奉供養) to the **Emperor** (是帝) and the **Scripture** (是經), forever free from **rebirth’s cycles and decline** (輪灭轉移之失).

Another teaching says: *"Seeing this sacred text, hearing this wondrous law, and beholding the **Emperor’s Face** (是帝颜), if one can personally and sincerely uphold and offer **reverence and sustenance** (崇奉供養), then one will forever escape the **mundane and profane** (尘凡), free from the **sufferings of rebirth and transmigration** (輪回轉生之苦)."* A deeper interpretation suggests that the **heart is forever steadfast**, and this is even more profound.

**Doubting Examination** (考疑) states: *"Confucian texts say, the **Divine** (神) cannot be summoned by mere thought. **Daoist** scriptures say, **Divine Transformation** (神化) requires no contrivance—it follows **Nature** (自然). **Buddhist** scriptures say, if one seeks the **Tathagata** (如來) through **form** (色) or **sound** (音声), one has strayed onto the **erroneous path** (邪道) and cannot behold the **Tathagata**. Yet today it is said: focus your contemplation on the **Emperor’s Noble Form** (尊容), proclaim the **Emperor’s Titles** (尊號), and then you will behold the **Compassionate Face** (慈颜).*

Does the **Primordial Beginning’s Mysterious Ancestor** (元始玄祖) deceive us? These words are not mere **fantasy or stagnant musings** (意想思存), nor are they **trapped in sensory traces** (滞迹口耳). To **unify in virtue with Heaven** (合德於天) and **inspire divine trust in the Emperor** (孚神於帝), to **blend and forget in transformation** (浑化相忘)—thus the ancients said: *"The **Heavenly威** (威) does not contradict the **Emperor’s Face** (玉帝颜), even at a distance of inches."* Through **reverent devotion and transformation** (敬恭而化), one naturally reaches the **ultimate praise**.

This is as the Confucian texts say: *"Speak the words of **Emperor Yao** (尧), and act in the manner of **Emperor Yao**—then you are **Emperor Yao**."* As the **Buddhist** teachings say: *"The **Dharmakaya** (法身) enters my **nature** (性), and my **nature** unites with the **Tathagata’s** (如來) **true principle** (真)."* And as the **Daoist** scriptures say: *"The **Divine** (神) merges with the **Dao/Way** (道), and the **Dao/Way** becomes one with the body."* Only thus can one **hear the wondrous law** (聞妙法), **offer reverence and sustenance** (奉供養), and be **forever free from rebirth’s cycles** (無輪轉).

If one merely **stores thoughts in the heart** (心存想) and **proclaims with the mouth** (口稱扬), yet cannot **submit one’s body** (皈身) or **submit one’s divine mandate** (皈神命), nor **converge in darkness with the Dao** (冥心會道), then this cannot be called **true reverence and sustenance** (真供養), and how can one **avoid rebirth’s cycles** (焉得無輪轉)?

The **uttermost perfection** (至無毁沦) and **unending steadfastness** (不迁转) prove that **contemplation, proclamation, and sustenance** (注想、稱揚、供養) transcend the **ordinary world’s understanding** (世俗之謂).

**Foolish Reflection** (愚按) states: *"All mortals possess **life and destiny** (性命) from **Heaven** (天), yet they fall into the **profane currents** (俗流) and thus are bound by **rebirth’s cycles** (輪轉). If one **masterminds the great Dao/Way** (經綸天下之大經) and **fulfills its nature** (能盡其性), then one truly **cultivates and reveres the Jade Emperor’s Scripture** (修奉玉帝經典); if one **crosses over and meets the Emperor in Heaven** (能對越在天), then it is as if one **stood near the Emperor** (即如近是帝). With **a humble and cautious heart** (小心翼翼), **devotedly serving without deviation** (祗事不違), one generates **true reverence** (生尊重心). The **body acts as Heaven’s work** (身代天工), the **mouth speaks as Heaven’s voice** (口代天言), **following Heaven without self-interest** (法天不私), and the **Emperor’s True Principle** (帝真) is **naturally present** (時御).

This is the **contemplation of the Jade Emperor’s Form** (想玉帝容), the **proclamation of the Emperor’s Titles** (稱帝號), and the **attainment of the Emperor’s Radiance** (得绪帝颜). **Virtue is singular** (德惟一), and **all actions are auspicious** (動罔不吉). **Exhausting oneself, exhausting others, exhausting all things** (盡己、盡人、盡物), **participating in the transformation and nurturing of all** (參贊化育), **submitting to destiny and sincerely surrendering** (皈命投誠), **embodying the form with utmost fidelity** (践形惟肖)—**supreme sincerity knows no cessation** (至誠無息), **eternal and boundless** (悠久無疆)—thus all receive **the Emperor’s Protection** (護度), universally hear the **Wondrous Law** (妙法), and personally offer **reverence and sustenance** (親奉供養), forever free from **rebirth’s cycles** (永無輪轉).

Ah! **The Dao/Way** in mortals must be **piercing and unbroken** (突不離). **The Dao/Way** has its **scriptures** (經), as **walking has its paths** (行有路). To **tread its full circuit** (践彼周行), how can one who walks the **Dao/Way** (行道者) not follow this path? **Confucius** had no **other way** (何莫由道) to deceive. The **Primordial Beginning** (元始) spoke truly: *"The profane cannot behold the Emperor"* (凡流不能見帝). If one **truly grasps this scripture** (果味是經), one **stands equal with the Jade Emperor** (自與玉帝齐肩).

In the **Thirty-Sixth Chapter of Divine Powers** (神通品三十六章), at that time, the **Fourfold Assembly** (四眾) heard these words and **rejoiced, leaping in delight** (歡喜躍跃), exclaiming that such had never been heard before. The **Grand Celestial Official** (天官大帝) declared: *"At the assembly of the Jade Scripture’s Law (玉經時), the Fourfold Assembly (法會四眾) heard the **Primordial Beginning’s Daoist Ancestor** (元始道祖) expound the *Jade Emperor’s Original Conduct Scripture* (《玉皇本行集經》), specifically the **Thirty-Fifth Chapter of Divine Powers in the Pure and Mysterious Celestial Palace** (□清微天宮神通品卷分已竟).*

They heard of the **Emperor’s extraordinary birth** (生長之奇异), the **accumulation of merits across countless ages** (多世之修因), the **limitless transformations** (變化之無量), the **inexhaustible virtues** (功德之難窮), the **natural divine responses** (神應之自然), and the **greatest of laws** (法之最大). The **attendants and guards, Jade Maidens** (侍衛玉女), **emanated from Heaven’s True Nature** (化自天真). The **boundaries of the sands** (沙界) and the **vast calamities** (浩劫) were all **relied upon by this scripture and law** (悉賴經法). They **understood the causes of crime and blessing** (明罪福之緣由) and **listened to the wondrous intent of severing obstacles** (聆斷障之妙旨).

The **Seventeen Great Radiant Lights** (十七大光明) have their **foundations** (洞之有基); the **countless eons of cultivating truth** (億萬劫修真) have their **key principles** (述之有要). **Taking the law as one’s own** (取法自在) makes **entering sainthood effortless** (入聖無難). They rejoiced at **escaping the mundane karmic burdens** (慶塵業之已脫) and **easily entering the Seven Realms** (幸七所之易入), all filled with **joy and delight** (悉皆歡悅喜樂), **exultant and leaping** (忻腾躍跃), **in unison praising** (同聲稱讚).

The present gathering of the **Law Assembly** (法会) is a **most auspicious and supreme opportunity** (良缘最胜), a **rare and extraordinary encounter** (奇逢非偶). This assembly, this teaching—**this is the Emperor, this is the Scripture** (此会此闻，是帝是经)—this moment, this instruction (兹时兹训) are **unprecedented since the eons** (历劫以来未曾有也).
