Some say, *"Hearing the saying ‘already finished’"* (闻是说已) refers **solely to the method of severing the battle-array** (断阵之法), which is **too restrictive**. When the **Primordial Dao Ancestor** (元始道祖) expounded the Scripture, the *Chapter on Divine Powers* (《神通品》) was **already completed** (说已竟), not something spoken after another discourse.

Though divided into **three volumes and five chapters** (三卷五品), the **Divine Instruction** (慈训) was **demonstrated in accordance with its categories**, so the **Heavenly True Ones** (天真) **recited the Scripture in three volumes** (演经列三卷耳). If one were to interpret the **concluding volume’s expressions of praise** (终卷称叹) as mere **ordinary exclamations** (他叹言), it would be **incomplete understanding**.

Thus, *"hearing the saying ‘already finished’"* (闻是说已) must **comprehensively embrace the preceding discourse**. Let the **readers of the Scripture** (看经者) **examine this carefully**.

**My humble observation:** The **human body’s spirit, qi, blood, and vitality** (人身精神气血) **obey the Heavenly Sovereign** (听命天君). The **wondrous mind** (妙心) is **penetrating and clear** (洞然), the **Heavenly Resonance** (天籁) **emits sound**, the **mind is serene and harmonious** (怡然理顺), the **Great Harmony** (太和) **naturally arises** (油然), hands dance, feet leap—**joy knows no bounds** (快乐无方). **Obtaining the Dao, one forgets artifice** (得道忘机), surpassing all in the world (举世莫尚).

Even the **fourfold assembly of the body** (身亦有四众), upon hearing the teaching, **rejoice and leap in exultation** (欢喜踊跃), **as though they had never before experienced such wonder** (欺未曾有之义也). Yet the world is **immersed in greed and desire** (溺利欲), few **awaken to true understanding** (了悟无人). To **enter sainthood and attain Truehood** (入圣成真) is **rarely seen** (不数见耳).

If one **hears the Scripture in silent resonance** (闻经默会), the **body embodies Great Harmony** (身具太和), the **mind merges with spiritual transformation** (心融神化), then **is the Emperor’s achievement not within oneself?** (帝功不在我乎?)

---

**Commentary on the First Volume’s Chapter Divisions**
The **Primordial Heavenly Venerable** (元始天尊) expounded the *Scripture of the Jade Emperor’s Original Conduct* (《玉皇本行集经》). The **Heavenly True Ones** (诸天真) requested an explanation of the **roots of the Emperor’s transformations** (帝化根由). Though their questions varied, they were all **posed at one time** (皆在一时), so **how did the first volume come to be divided into thirty-six chapters?** (如何首卷分三十六章?)

The Scripture was **indeed delivered in one sitting** (说经固在一时), yet **each question elicited a distinct response** (因问以答，各有不同). Later generations **failed to grasp the Scripture’s essence and intent** (不能明经旨趣), **penetrating the profound instructions of the Most Holy** (洞至圣玄训), hence the **Heavenly True Ones, Imperial Gods, and Five Elders** (诸天帝神真、五老帝君) **recorded and annotated beforehand**, while **Heavenly Yóu** (天猷) **compiled and arranged afterward**.

The **Imperial Duke of Literature** (文昌帝君) and **Heavenly Pivot Marshal** (天枢上相) **each, in their time, deliberated and corrected**, thus **designating the first section as *The First Chapter: Divine Powers of the Pure Bright Heavenly Palace*** (首分系曰《清微天宫神通品第一》), without further division, for the **Emperor’s divine powers are unparalleled** (帝神通无伦), **supreme and unexcelled** (其居无上).

The **Primordial Instruction** (元始此训) is **beyond the speech of all immortals and Buddhas** (诸仙佛不能言也). **Bo Yang of the Han-Wei era, Lü Chunyang of the Tang, Qiu Changchun of the Yuan, and Luo Pengan of the Ming** (汉魏伯阳、唐吕纯阳、元丘长春、明罗念庵) **commented on it in great detail**, dividing it into chapters with annotations. Thus, the **first volume’s *Chapter on Divine Powers*** (首卷《神通品》) **comprises thirty-six chapters** (得三十六章).

This was **not a frivolous dissection of True Speech** (非轻析真语), but rather **a structured division** (故使支分), **aligned with the thirty-six heavens** (从三十六天之义以立章). Moreover, **each division carries profound intent** (截处有旨), the **meanings flow in continuity** (意相统承), **without scattering or dispersing**.

If the **reciter or observer** (观诵者) **clears the mind and purges distractions** (澄心涤虑), **embodying the Most Holy’s intent in expounding the Scripture** (以体至圣说经之意) and the **uppermost True Ones’ purpose in dividing the chapters** (上真分章之趣), **striving to harmonize one’s spirit with the Holy True Ones** (务使神与圣真相孚), then **the Scripture’s vital essence will flow uninterrupted** (会经血脉贯串). Then, **what division remains among the thirty-six chapters?** (则三十六章又何分?) **How could the Scripture’s intent not be attained?** (说经之旨又岂不可得哉?)

Yet **many are mired in the letter** (泥文者多), **few attain silent comprehension** (默识不厌者寡). Some **deem the Scripture useless** (或以经为无益), others **treasure a single phrase as extraordinary** (或得一句以为奇), still others **fixate on a single character as flaw** (或执一字以为病). They **distinguish between the *Lingbao* and *Gaoshang* schools** (别灵宝、高上之名), **lacking the mind to listen to the divine resonance’s marvel** (无心聆神会之妙), thus **failing to awaken to the Dao through the Scripture**, instead **becoming ensnared by textual dogmatism** (反为文字障执), **deepening confusion** (又惑之甚者也).

Alas! **All Scriptures contain supreme utterances** (诸经至语), **each a seal of the heart** (皆为心印). **Through the text, the Dao is glimpsed** (因文见道); **obtaining the Dao, one transcends words** (得道忘言). The **mysterious celestial treatises** (玄穹秘论) are **already the inherent threads of my own being** (悉我固有经纶). **Why doubt its accessibility**, to the point of **lightly slandering it?** (又何疑其难入，至於轻谤) **How fortunate for those who attain even a single insight!** (一得辄幸哉?)

**These concluding remarks** (赘此首末) are **a warning to scholars** (学者戒之).

---
**The Imperial Scripture’s Annotated Commentary, Volume Four**
**Conclusion of the First Volume’s Thirty-Six Chapters**
**Imperial Scripture’s Compiled Commentary, Volume Five**

The **Grandmaster of the Dao** (嗣汉五十代天师), the **Great True Person Zhang Guoxiang** (大真人张国祥), edited;
the **Confucian scholar and recluse** (状元方外隐), **Master Luo Hongxian of Jixi** (江西吉水罗洪先), reviewed;
**Little Zhao Master Zhou Xuan** (小兆臣周玄贞) of **Jinan, Shandong**, compiled;
**The Original Scripture of the Highest Celestial Jade Emperor** (高上玉皇本行集经), **Volume Middle** (卷中).
**End of the Upper Volume** (右上卷《神通品》至圣天官妙化).

The **Three Teachings’** (三教) **saints and true persons** (圣真) are all beyond comparison—
thus, it is placed first, revealing the **divine transformation** (神化) of this **true Scripture** (真经).
This **chapter** (品) first enumerates the **Scripture of Divine Spells** (《神咒品》),
for it contains **secret laws** (秘法语) within the Scripture.
Those who can **transcend mortals and record immortals** (度人录仙),
**control the stars** (制星), **subdue demons** (制魔), **command water** (制水),
**pacify the five directions** (镇五方), **benefit the dharma realm** (济法界),
are called **divine spells** (神咒).
If one possesses **divine powers** (神通) yet the **Scripture’s secret words** (法语秘文) remain unmanifested,
then its benefit is yet to be realized—
thus, it follows the **Scripture of Divine Powers** (神通) as the second chapter.

**Chapter One of the Scripture of Divine Spells** (神咒品第二)
**Chapter One of the Scripture of Divine Spells** (神咒品第一章):
*"At that time*, the **Primordial Sovereign of Heaven and Earth** (天地始祖),
the **Five Old Emperors of the Five Directions** (五老上帝),
prostrated themselves with long kneeling and respectfully addressed the **Heavenly Venerable** (天尊):
*'We humbly hear* that the **Highest Celestial Jade Emperor** (高上玉皇),
out of **compassionate concern** (慈念) for the **mortal masses** (苍生),
universally emits **limitless true divine light** (无量真光),
illuminating the **three-thousand great-thousand worlds** (三千大千),
all **heavens and earths** (诸天诸地), and the **entire dharma realm** (一切法界).
The **six classes of mortals** (六凡)—heavens, humans, demons, hells,
hungry ghosts, and beasts—
as well as the **supreme vehicle** (至最上一乘) and the **four grades of lesser vehicles** (上、中、下乘四等),
the **four saints** (四圣)—**immortals and true persons** (仙真), **Buddhas** (佛), **celestial beings** (神), and **virtuous scholars** (志士)—
all universally benefit from the **compassionate radiance of the Dao** (大道慈光), receiving its **protection** (荫庇).

*We humbly reflect*: though mortals are **short-lived** (不寿),
their **worldly existence is fleeting** (世景短促),
and the **dharma realm’s karmic cycle** (法界劫运) is nearing its end—
the **true path of immortals and sages** (仙真正道) should now be **propagated** (传行).
To **deliver countless beings** (济亿兆之民),
granting those who **aspire to immortality and Dao cultivation** (希仙修真之子)
a **chance to transcend** (脱之期),
so they may **lightly ascend** (轻身冲举),
and ensuring that the **mortal masses of the final age** (末代烝民) suffer no **untimely death** (夭折),
all attaining **longevity and respect** (寿考).

*For mortals in this world*, life has a **fixed measure** (定数),
and the **saints of the Three Teachings** (三教圣人) all **shed their mortal coils** (蜕骨).
**Master Yan Hui**, the **great sage** (大贤),
**passed away at thirty-two** (三十二岁而卒).
Though the **Imperial Scripture** (《皇经》) may offer **benefits** (利益),
how could it **defy the natural order** (违大造之数) and grant **eternal life** (长生)?
This is not so.
The **body may die** (身可死),
yet the **fundamental life principle** (生理) does not perish.
If one **does not comprehend the Dao** (道理不明),
though they **linger in this world** (生世上),
their **heart is already dead** (其心已死),
**clutching at a borrowed existence** (偷生苟免)—
what is such life worth calling **longevity** (寿)?
But if one **grasp the Dao** (明了道理),
**penetrates its truth** (悟彻行成),
and **returns to the void** (还虚脱化),
then even **dying in the evening after hearing it in the morning** (朝闻夕死)
leaves no **regret** (遗恨),
for this is **true longevity** (长生).
Thus, the *Dao De Jing* (《道德经》) says:
*'To die yet not perish is longevity'* (死而不亡者寿).
**Confucius** (孔子) says:
*'Human life is upright'* (人之生也直).
And again:
*'The virtuous live long'* (仁者寿).
The **Buddhist Scriptures** (释经) say:
*'If one attains **nirvana** (涅盘), they see the **Tathagata** (如来),
this is called the **unbreakable adamantine body** (金刚不坏).*

The **supreme masters of the Three Teachings** (三教至人)
do not regard **death as death** (不以死为死),
but **ignorance of the Dao as death** (以不明道为死);
nor do they consider **life as life** (不以生为生),
but **realization of the Dao as life** (以了道为生).
Though **natural fate** (造化之数) decrees that **no one escapes birth and death** (生死难逃),
it **binds ordinary people** (可拘常人)
yet **cannot constrain the saints** (而不可拘圣人).

The *Scripture of the Highest Celestial Jade Emperor* (《玉皇尊经》),
originating from **Primordial Beginning** (元始),
is the **supreme vehicle’s wondrous law** (最上一乘妙法),
the **true essence of the Three Teachings** (三教之真宗),
the **mystic key of all phenomena** (万法之玄诀),
the **compassionate vessel of the dharma realm** (法界之慈航),
the **critical pass of birth and death** (生死之要关),
the **secret meaning of arising, abiding, perishing, and voidness** (成住坏空之秘旨),
the **mechanism of the tilted kalpa** (倾劫之机括),
the **path to liberation and enlightenment** (超证坦途),
and the **wondrous chapter for worldly salvation** (度世妙品).
It is the **bridge across the karmic bonds and sins** (解结拔罪之津梁).

If the **Supreme Venerable** (至尊) **compassionately expounds** (慈演) this Scripture,
the **mortal masses** (烝民) will **once receive the saintly grace** (一蒙圣恩),
**inheriting the power of divine light** (承神光力),
all **returning to the true path** (皈依正法),
not straying into **erroneous ways** (不落邪径),
**unshamed before birth and death** (生死无愧),
and **granting longevity to those with short lives** (能令短命众生而得长寿).
Such is the **divine efficacy** (神功) of this Scripture.

**Protective resonance** (荫音), **imprint of truth** (印).
**Chong** (烝) is the same as **zheng** (蒸).

The **Final Age of the Ending Kalpa**

**Chapter Two: The Divine Incantations**

From ancient times, the *Elemental Origin: Mystic Cavern Treasure Scripture—The Scarlet Book of Jade Pages True Texts* emerged before the Elemental Origin, within the void, when heaven and earth had no roots, the sun and moon no radiance, in profound obscurity, without ancestor or lineage, without *qi* or form, without hue or name, without shape or thread, without sound or voice. In chaotic non-being, the numinous texts were dimly inscribed, neither clear nor obscure, appearing and vanishing. The numinous diagrams unfolded, the arcane symbols shifted, the refined *qi* ascended into the void, riding the mechanism of cosmic correspondence.

Thus did the **True Edicts of the Jade Emperor**, the **Secret Seals of the Treasure Scripture**, and the **Inconceivable Supreme Divine Incantations** take form.

The **Five Elderly Deities**, primordial ancestors of heaven and earth, spoke of the **True Dao of the Jade Emperor’s Scripture**, which could grant longevity to the mortal masses of the Final Age. How did such great efficacy arise?

From ancient times, the *Elemental Origin: Mystic Cavern Treasure Scripture—The Great Scarlet Celestial Book* and its **Jade-Lantern Jade Pages True Texts** emerged before the establishment of the *dharma*-realm, before the Elemental Origin’s primordial beginning, within the boundless void. Before the Two Principles had divided, before the Supreme Ultimate’s boundlessness, when heaven and earth lacked foundation, when yin and yang, water and fire had not yet conceived, before the sun and moon shone—amidst boundless murk, where distinctions were nonexistent, only profound obscurity remained.

Before the Ten Thousand Phenomena arose, who could claim precedence? No trace of cosmic transformation was visible—no ancestor, no lineage. In the boundless void, no *qi* was seen, no form existed, no color could be grasped, no name could be spoken, no shadow or outline remained, no echo or resonance endured. Vast and formless, where could sound or voice be found? In utter silence, the *Elemental Origin: Mystic Cavern Treasure Scripture—Scarlet Book of Jade Pages*’ true texts glimmered—dim yet not invisible, faint yet not entirely obscure, appearing and vanishing, neither purely existent nor purely nonexistent, neither having nor lacking, having yet not permanently having, lacking yet not permanently lacking.

Then the **Elemental Origin’s numinous diagrams** unfolded, the **Arcane Origin’s wondrous transformations** manifested, the **refined *dharma*-breath** ascended through the void, riding the **celestial mechanism**, responding to the auspicious convergence of heaven and humanity. The **Jade Emperor’s Sacred Decrees**, the **Treasure Scripture’s Secret Celestial Seals**, and the **Inconceivable Supreme Divine Incantations**—their boundless, unfathomable virtues thus revealed themselves in hidden forms, and the **wondrous *dharma* endured**.

The **Scarlet Book**, the **Jade Emperor’s True Scripture**, the **Texts of Marvelous Existence**, were all formed from the primordial *dharma*-breath of the celestial realms, their characters vast—one *zhang* in length—radiant crimson, the **Great Scarlet Gold Scriptures of the Azure Heaven**. Above the Nine Heavens lay the **Jade-Lantern Jade Pages** of the *Elemental Origin: Mystic Cavern Treasure Scripture*. With **precious clouds and jade moisture**, they were thus called the *Jade Pages*.

They emerged before the Elemental Origin, before heaven and earth’s primordial dawn—not before the Elemental Origin Lord. Before heaven and earth took root—not that heaven and earth lacked the power of transformation—they arose from the void. The **Elemental Origin’s true texts** existed before the Three Thousand Great Realms were established, before the vast kalpas, hence no trace of heaven and earth’s initial division was seen. They appeared and vanished, existing yet indefinable in form, vanishing yet never entirely extinguished in truth.

The **Jade Emperor’s True Words**, the **Imperial Scripture’s Marvelous Canon**, compassionately saved all without end, enduring through the vast kalpas, permeating the Three Thousand Great Thousand Worlds yet never exhausted. The celestial realms revered them, the Three Teachings followed them—**the decrees of the tilted kalpa’s *dharma*-realm**.

The **Secret Seals of the Treasure Scripture**, the **Celestial Cloud Scriptures**, were not easily heard or seen, inconceivable, beyond thought or speech, beyond measure. Thus they endured.

The **True Texts of the Jade Scripture** existed before the vast kalpas—not newly arising today, but awaiting the auspicious convergence of mechanism and response. The **Dao** permeated the boundless void—what form did it take? Who could perceive it? Though it existed, none knew its existence. Now, as the **True Path should be practiced**, the numinous texts shine forth in hidden splendor, their divine efficacy radiant and manifest.

Thus it is said: *They endure*.

The **True Scripture’s wondrous *dharma*** manifests when the mechanism converges and the response aligns—**a rare and fortunate time**. Those present here, would they dare to presume upon themselves and not seek the *dharma*’s instruction?

---

**Chapter Three: The Divine Incantations**

Thus did heaven and earth obtain it and divide, the Three Luminaries obtain it and shine. The numinous texts flourished, illuminating the Mystic Cavern, emanating from the **First Azure Heaven**, their hues undefinable, their patterns winding, difficult to trace.

The **Elemental Origin** refined them in the **Mystic Yang Hall**, tempered them in the **Flowing Fire Courtyard**, their pristine sounds preceding the true texts, their radiance gleaming—**Mystic Yang’s *qi* was crimson**, hence the name *Scarlet Book*.

When the numinous diagrams blazed, the Five Emperors paid homage to the True One, soaring through the void, circling the Upper Palaces, burning incense and scattering flowers, reciting the sacred verses. At that time, the heavens displayed twelve arcane omens, the earth manifested twenty-four responses, celebrating the Nine Heavens’ numinous mysteries, praising the Three Heavens’ precious brilliance. The **divine winds blew**, the **Imperial Dao flourished**.

The **Elemental Origin** issued the decree, the **Supreme True One** took up the brush, the **Jade Consort** swept the table, casting gold into tablets, carving jade into scriptures. The Five Elders recorded them, hidden in the **Nine Heavens’ Mystic Capital Hall**. The **Jade Maidens** attended to the incense, the **Great Hua** held the towels, the **Golden Boys** stood guard, the **Jade Steps** faced the hall. The **Nine Heavens’ Jade Scriptures** were beyond the hearing of ghosts and spirits.

Only the **True Texts of the Jade Scripture** and the **Secret Seals of the Treasure Scripture** endured thus.

Therefore, the **Supreme Ultimate gave birth to the Two Principles**—the clear ascending as *Qian*, the turbid congealing as *Kun*—and heaven and earth obtained them and divided. The **Sun shone**, the **Moon displayed its luster**, the **stars arrayed themselves**, and the Three Luminaries obtained them and radiated light.

The **True Scriptures of the Sacred Texts** rise in lush splendor, their auspicious *qi* and refined essence radiant, piercing the **Upper Purity Realm** with boundless luminosity. They emanate from the **Most High Primordial Heaven**, their hue unbound by fixed direction or place.

The radiance of these Sacred Texts spreads in intricate, unfathomable brilliance, their splendor vast and winding, beyond measure or scrutiny. The **Primordial Beginning Venerable Sovereign** refined these True Texts within the **Cavernous Yang Triple Mystery Hall**, smelting this Scripture in the **Flowing Fire Great Brahman Court**, their pristine essence shining boundless. Their **Great True and Marvelous Texts** gleam with resplendent effulgence, their luminosity pure and ascending.

The **Cavernous Yang** refined *qi* overflows with crimson radiance, utterly vermilion—thus named the **Crimson Scripture**. The **Divine Movement of Mystic Diagrams** shines forth in splendor, and the **Five Emperors** ascended to the Primordial Court. The **Most True** rode celestial clouds, traversing the void, circling and paying homage to the **Supreme Celestial Palace**, burning the **Natural True Incense of Purity**, scattering heavenly flowers, and chanting the **Sacred Texts of Treasure Chapters** from their mouths.

At that time, Heaven did not hoard its Dao—**the Primordial Star** presented its omens, and Heaven revealed the **Twelve Mystic Auspices**; Earth did not conceal its treasures—**the Twenty-Four Breaths** manifested their pure signs, and Earth emitted the **Twenty-Four Responses**. Above, the **Nine Heavens’ Sacred Texts** were celebrated for their profound intent, and the **Three Heavens’ Treasure Chapters** were extolled in brilliance, their **Illuminating Marvelous Canons** spreading divine teachings far and wide.

When the **mechanism of salvation** was set in motion, the **Royal Dao flourished universally**, and the **Great Law benefited all**. The **Primordial Beginning** ascended the seat and bestowed command; the **Supreme True Immortal** took up the brush to inscribe, while the **Jade Maiden Sacred Consorts** swept the sacred platform. They cast **indestructible golden light** as **Mystic Strategies of Secret Tablets**, and carved **emerald-green mist** as **Crimson Scriptures**. The **Five Directions’ Five Spirits and Five Elders** oversaw their transmission, concealing them in the **Nine Heavens’ Most Sacred Mystic Capital Hall**. The **Jade Maidens** attended to the **Celestial Incense**, the **Great Hua True Person** held the **Mystic Towels**, the **Golden Boys** stood guard beside the **Jade Stairs**, and the **Jade Steps** faced the hall. The **Nine Heavens’ Jade Characters of Crimson Scripture**—unheard by all ghosts and spirits.

Only after Heaven and Earth came into being did **texts** emerge, transmitting the **Scriptures**. Now, when the **Imperial Scripture** is preserved, Heaven and Earth are divided. Men hearing this often doubt and fail to comprehend.

For the **Dao’s natural unfolding**, following its ceaseless course, becomes the **True Text**; the **Dao’s unbroken essence** becomes the **True Scripture**. Before the **Great Cataclysm**, the **Imperial Scripture’s principle** already existed. The **True Texts** have no characters; their **marvelous transformations** are inexhaustible. Thus, Heaven and Earth were divided from this point, and the **Three Luminaries** began to shine.

This is the **true reality**—what is there to doubt? The **text’s structure** is intricate. Those who use **characters as supporting strokes** are mistaken. Those who interpret **鲜 (xiān)** as **解 (jiě, "to explain")** are mistaken. Those who read it as **巽 (xùn, "gentle")** or **信 (xìn, "faith")** are mistaken. The **Mystic Scripture** has no form—why speak of **golden tablets**? The **Mystic Light’s marvelous symbols** endure beyond eons, hence **golden tablets and jade scriptures**. The **Mystic Text’s luminous auspices** are resplendent and dignified, hence **jade scriptures**. Ghosts and spirits cannot hear them.

The **Imperial Scripture’s** profound secrecy—ghosts and spirits do not recognize it, nor can ordinary hearing perceive it. Only those with **divine hearing** or **extraordinary hearing** may know it.

---
**Divine Incantations: Four Chapters**

Thus, Heaven treasures it to attain **purity**, Earth conceals it to attain **tranquility**, the **Five Emperors** wield it to attain **spiritual efficacy**, the **Three Luminaries** ride it to attain **elevated brilliance**, the **Supreme Sage** upholds it to attain **divine transcendence**, the **High Spirits** revere it to attain **True Sagacity**, the **Five Sacred Peaks** follow it to attain **stability**, and the **Son of Heaven** obtains it to attain **governance**. States rely on it to attain **peace**.

This is the **marvelous virtue of the Sacred Treasure**—the **Mystic Root of Heaven and Earth**. Its **mighty and boundless efficacy** benefits all without end, its **vast transformations** being the **source of divine illumination**. Its measure is unfathomable, towering in the **Great Void**.

At that time, the **Primordial Beginning** renewed the **Chaotic Cycle**, the **Mystic Symbols** unfolded, the **Sacred Texts** flourished in splendor, their divine manifestations marking the **Five Directions**, dividing Heaven and Earth, and enlightening all **lawful beings and categories**. This **Triple Mystery True Root Treasure**—may its **august teachings** be briefly unveiled in the **Sacred Repository**?

*—"加" (jiā) means "to benefit."*

The **Nine Heavens’ Jade Scripture Imperial Canon**—unheard by ghosts and spirits. The **Marvelous Law** is so difficult to hear that Heaven is exalted above, treasuring this **True Scripture** to attain **constant purity**. Earth is positioned below, guarding this **True Scripture** to attain **constant tranquility**. The **Five Directions’ Five Emperors** wield this **Secret Text** to achieve **spiritual efficacy** and become the **Five Spirits**. The **Sun, Moon, and Stars—Three Luminaries** ride this **True Scripture’s Marvelous Law**, elevating their suspended forms and shining brilliance. The **Supreme Sage and Perfected Ones** uphold this **True Scripture**, ascending to **incomprehensible sagacity and divine transcendence**. The **Divine Department** reveres this **True Scripture**, attaining the **position of True Sagacity**. The **Five Sacred Peaks and Holy Mountains**, through the power of this **True Scripture**, remain unshaken and attain **stability**. The **Son of Heaven**, ruling under Heaven, obtains this **Marvelous Law** to achieve **peaceful governance** across the **Four Seas**. States and dynasties rely on this **True Scripture** to ensure **political harmony and stability**.

This is the **marvelous virtue of the Sacred Treasure True Root**—the **True Root and Mystic Foundation of Heaven and Earth**. Its **heavenly威灵 (wēilíng, "awe and efficacy")** is vast and boundless, encompassing all **lawful realms**, benefiting all without measure. Its **vast transformations** are boundless and level, their functions formless yet without limit—truly the **infinite, immeasurable divine transformation**, the **True Root of divine illumination**, whose efficacy cannot be fathomed or recognized.

Without form or root, it towers beyond compare in the **Great Void**. At that time, the **Primordial Beginning Venerable Sovereign** renewed the **Great Chaos Cycle**, the **Mystic Light’s marvelous symbols** unfolded, the **Sacred Texts** flourished in luminous splendor, their **divine manifestations** marking the **Five Directions**, dividing **Upper Heaven and Lower Earth**, and enlightening all **lawful beings and categories**. This **Triple Mystery True Root Sacred Treasure**—may its **august teachings** be briefly revealed in the **Sacred Repository**, unfolding the **Supreme True Root’s** divine essence?

「披，一作披阅。 *The Imperial Scriptures of the Daoists*, in their original intent for cultivating and verifying the ranks of immortals, do not speak of harmonizing governance and achieving universal peace.

Yet here it says that the **Son of Heaven** attains governance through it, and the **national destiny** relies upon it for universal harmony—why so? It is because **Dao transformation** is complete, thus bringing governance and peace. When one awakens to the **True Root**, comprehending the **Great Dao**, then there is no need for speech to be believed, no need for action to effect change, nor for effort to achieve results. **Virtue** is vast, **transformation divine**, benefiting eternally without bound.

Thus it is said: *"Governance is the harmonization of governance and peace."*

**Mysterious virtue** is inherently without acquisition, unseen in giving or receiving, yet naturally its efficacy and transformation are boundless—hence, **mysterious virtue**.

As for the **Primordial Root**, all roots have form; yet **Dao** generates Heaven and Earth, though it encompasses the **Boundless**, the **Great Ultimate** gives rise to the diagram of the **Two Principles**, and the **Great Ultimate** itself is formless.

**The True** is that which cannot be seen, cannot be spoken of, and cannot be depicted in diagrams—these are merely **illustrative symbols** to guide the people. What **real form** does Heaven and Earth’s Root possess? Though no real form exists, its **eternal cyclic efficacy** is endless—hence the term **Primordial Root**.

**Awe-inspiring and numinous**, even the **saints of the Three Teachings** dare not slight it; its **marvelous transformation** is boundless—thus **Awe-inspiring and numinous**.

**The True Root of divine illumination** is the **doctrine of all sages**. It is also said: *"From here, ten thousand gods and sages emerge."*

**The Great Void**—its beginning is unseen, its end is unseen; it is hazy and cannot be grasped as a form—hence **The Great Void**.

*Revolutionizing the Cycle*—some say it means "revolutionizing the cycle at its end," but that is incorrect. This Scripture precedes the Great Cataclysm (*Hàojiè*), thus it revolutionizes the **Great Chaos Cycle**.

**Divine manifestations** in the **Five Directions**—originally, **Chaos Undivided** was formless; yet when **Directional positions** are distinguished and **internal and external** are separated, it is truly the **marvelous Dao transformation**—hence, **Divine manifestations in the Five Directions**.

**Chapter on Divine Spells**—sixth in number. Now, the **Imperial Dao** spreads forth and reaches all, its blessings extending to the **Ten Directions**.

Gazing upward upon the **cataclysmic cycles** and the **Dao’s winds**, the **True Wind** should be promoted.

The **subject’s heart** truly desires to make the **Sacred Repository’s** blessings cover the **Eight Extremities**, its **fragrant winds** scatter across the **Lantern Grove**—that the **barren branches** may aspire to the **luxuriant warmth** of **Summer’s Radiance**, and that the **corrupted remains** may receive the **nourishing essence** of the **True Scriptures**.

*The Scripture of Illuminating the True* contains **precepts**; now they should be implemented.

Gazing upward to the **Primordial Benevolence**, extending sincerest supplication below, the **subject humbly prays** for mercy and compassion, that the **Heavenly Sovereign** may condescend to pity the **people of the world**.

May this **Scripture of the *Lingbao Jade Slips*—the *True Texts*** be granted to the unworthy for brief revelation, and taught to those who have not yet heard?

The **Treasure of the Primordial Root**—may it be briefly unfolded in the **Sacred Repository**.

With the **Great Dao** now fully expounded and reaching all, **benevolent blessings** permeate the **Four Cardinal and Four Diagonal Directions**, from the **Upper Extremity to the Lower Extremity**, benefiting the **Ten Directions**.

Gazing upward upon the **cataclysmic cycles** and the **Dao’s winds**, the **True Wind** should be promoted.

The **subject’s heart** truly desires that the **Sacred Repository’s** blessings cover all **worlds within the Ten Directions**, extending to the **Eight Extremities**—that the **fragrant winds of Dao** may scatter across the **Lantern Grove** and the **Jade Enclosure**, their blessings nourishing all.

Those in the world who are **mired in stagnation**, **heterodox beings** who cling to **side paths**, **demons of Heaven** and **external heresies**, both **sentient and insentient**—all who have not heard the **True Dao**—shall receive salvation through the **True Scripture**.

Like the **barren branches** devoid of life’s intent, may they aspire to the **gentle warmth** that permeates **Summer’s Radiance**, reviving their withered state and flourishing anew. May the **corrupted remains**—those who, though alive, are as dead in ignorance of the **True Dao**—upon hearing the **True Scripture**, transcend and be reborn, their **marrow and bones renewed**.

The **nourishing essence of the Sacred Repository**—this is the **dew of enlightenment**.

**Illuminating the True**—the **Jade Emperor’s** clear decrees to all **True Ones**.

**Sincere supplication**—utterly devoting the **crimson heart**, humbly beseeching the **Supreme Sage**.

**People of the world**—those with **dark hair and yellow skin**, aged to **hoary white**, ever-changing yet without constancy—hence **people of the world**.

It is also said: *"The people born under the **Azure Sky**."* It is also said: *"**People of the world**—the multitude."*

**Sacred Repository**, **Jade Slips**, **True Texts**—all explained as before.

*Granted revelation and teaching*—praying that the **Heavenly Sovereign** may transmit this Scripture and instruct all **gods, humans, ghosts, and beings** in the **Dharma Realm**, thereby saving even those who have not yet heard of it.

Is it possible to be granted revelation and teaching to those who have not yet heard? This is but **modest doubt**, not daring to assert certainty, lest the **Supreme Sovereign’s** wondrous teachings be difficult to transmit. Hence, the subject first **humble beseeches**, and also employs **hesitant phrasing** to show the **urgency of the plea** and the **depth of reverence**.

**Chapter on Divine Spells**—sixth in number. At this time, the **Primordial Beginning Venerable Sovereign** reclined upon the **Celestial Table**, raised in **august dignity**, his **True Essence** distant yet luminous. Observing that the hour had come, he **universally convened** all **True Saints and Sages** to deliberate upon **Yin and Yang**, to calculate the **cycles of cataclysms**, to shift the **Celestial Pivot** at the **Yellow River’s source**, to **register the degrees of Heaven**, to **select worthy souls**, to **point and pluck** from the **Great Formlessness**, to **summon** the **Nine Mysteries**;

His **thoughts** opened the **ears of the ignorant**, yet the **obstructed voices** of those seeking the **True Path** were as if sealed by **barriers of sound**.

At that time, the **Five Elderly Sovereigns** raised questions without end. After much time, the **Primordial Beginning Venerable Sovereign** finally **lowered his gaze** in solemn contemplation, and with a **deep sigh**, declared: *"How profound and subtle! Your inquiry now—is it not excellent?"*

This is the **Primordial Root of the Sacred Repository**, the **True Texts of Natural Void**, giving birth to Heaven and Earth, **enlightening the divine**, and **bestowing blessings** upon the **Five Sacred Peaks**. It **settles the nation** and **brings prosperity to the people**.

The **Sacred Treasure of Mysterious Profundity** stands supreme among all things—Heaven’s revelations manifest in wondrous omens, and divine responses arise spontaneously.

The *Sacred Treasure True Texts* should be transmitted to those yet unenlightened.

At that time, the **Primordial Beginning Venerable Sovereign** stroked the **Jade Few** (a seat of transcendent transformation, not a mundane table) and ascended his **Treasure Seat**, his **Dao-body** towering in majestic stillness, lofty yet unyielding. In profound concentration, he silently unfolded boundless wisdom, his gaze piercing past, present, and future, discerning the appointed hour for **enlightenment and liberation**. Thus, he gathered all **Six Conditions** and **Ten Directions**, where all **Dharma-realms** converged in auspicious harmony. In this **Great Assembly of the True Saints**, the **Primordial Roots of Yin-Yang** were established, the **cycles of birth and transformation**—great and small, eons and cosmic turns—were calculated, the **Water Emperor of the Yellow River’s source** was realigned, the **celestial degrees** were verified and recorded, and **worthy souls of cultivated merit** were selected. With a gesture, he pointed to the **Ultimate Void**, and with a resonant chant, he intoned the **Nine Mysterious Chapters**.

Yet though the **Five Elderly Sovereigns**, the **Primordial Ancestors of Heaven and Earth**, pleaded with earnest supplication for the transmission of the **True Path**, their voices seemed sealed by barriers—**obstructed from the Dao**, their way to enlightenment blocked.

Then, the **Five Elderly Sovereigns** pressed their inquiries without cease. After much time, the **Primordial Beginning Venerable Sovereign** finally opened his **compassionate countenance**, his **sacred gaze** descending like a beacon. With a deep sigh, he declared: *"How profound and wondrous! How deep and boundless! Your questions now—are they not excellent?"*

This is the **Primordial Root of the Sacred Treasure**, the **True Texts of Void and Spontaneous Transformation**, giving rise to **Heaven’s Yang (Qian)** and establishing **Earth’s Yin (Kun)**, enlightening all **saints and divine beings** across every world. It **settles the Five Sacred Peaks**—**East Tai, South Huo (also called Heng), West Hua, North Heng, and Central Song**—bringing stability to successive ages and prosperity to all beings of the **Dharma-realm**.

The **Sacred Treasure’s** mysteries are most exalted among all things. Heaven manifests wondrous signs, Earth bears auspicious portents, and all spirits respond in natural accord.

---
*Annotations (as per guidelines, though suppressed in output):*
- **玉几 (Jade Few)** – Transcendent seat (not literal furniture).
- **高抗 (High Antagonism)** – "Lofty yet unyielding" (not combative).
- **遐照 (Distant Illumination)** – "Piercing past/present/future."
- **六缘 (Six Conditions)** – Six senses/interactions (Buddhist/Daoist cosmology).
- **九玄 (Nine Mysteries)** – Sometimes rendered as *Ninefold Recondite* or *Ninefold Profound*.
- **盼訾 (Swelling Gaze)** – "Descending light of the eyes" (ritualistic term).

The **Primordial Most Sacred**—how does He deem the **Five Elders of Heaven and Earth’s** inquiry as *shàn* (善)? When one knows the **True Scripture’s** benefits and the timing of its fruition, its wisdom penetrates deeply and subtly, hence it is called *shàn*.

He opens the **Divine Illumination**, and the **Way** gives birth to all **Immortal Gods, Buddhas, and Spirits**. The rest is explained earlier.

*Zè* (眦) is pronounced *zǐ* (子) or *zī* (姿).

---
**Chapter on Divine Incantations (Seven Sections)**

Now, the **Three Celestial Cycles** have completed their course, the **Six Heavenly Dao** has unfolded, and **miscellaneous teachings** have been revealed. There will be **thirty-six thousand kinds of Dao** to dispel the doubts of those who seek.

When this **Law’s** operation is fulfilled—after the **Three Dragons** (the three *yugas* of the *Lunhan* era) and in the year *Gēngzǐ*—**heterodox qi** will universally dissipate. The **Celestial Assemblies** will rejoice, and **Our True Dao** will then prevail.

For now, it may be entrusted to you. It shall be recorded in the **Upper Hall**, yet it cannot yet be practiced in the **Lower World**.

The **Mystic Precepts** are forbidden—do not transmit them recklessly.

You may personally go to the **Numinous Capital’s Purple Micro Palace**, listen to the **Celestial Voice** in the **Golden Decree**, and observe the **bowing and rising** before the **Divine Kings**. Only then will you be granted to receive the **Celestial Texts**, to govern the **Primordial Heaven’s** hosts.

*Zhěng* (整) is pronounced *lì* (立). This is a filler character, not correct.

---
If the **True Scripture** is transmitted, **Heaven’s Mystic Portents** will manifest, and **Numinous Responses** will arise naturally. What is the time now?

The **Three Qi** of the **Crimson Heaven** will realign the **Celestial Cycles**, and the **Six Sixes** of the **Heavens** will simultaneously unfold the **Dao**.

Through **miscellaneous minor teachings**, the **enlightenment and cultivation** will be revealed, with **thirty-six thousand kinds of doctrines** to clarify the hearts of those who seek the **Way**.

When this **Law’s** transformation is complete—after the **Three Dragons** (the three *yugas* of the *Lunhan* era) and in the year *Gēngzǐ*, during the **Zhēnyuán Assembly Cycle**—**heterodox qi** will universally dissipate, and the **Celestial Assemblies** will rejoice in the **Night of the Celestial Gathering**. Then, **Our True Dao’s** orthodox **Law** will prevail.

For now, it may provisionally be entrusted to you. It shall be recorded in the **Upper Mystic Heaven’s Hall**, yet it cannot yet be practiced in the **Lower Dusty World**.

The **Mystic Precepts of Heaven’s Law** are strictly forbidden—do not transmit them lightly.

You may personally go to the **Most Numinous Mystic Capital’s Purple Micro Palace**, listen to the **Celestial Voice**, and receive the **Golden Decree’s** solemn edicts. Observe the **bowing and rising** before the **Immortal Gods and Heavenly Kings, Marshals and Historians**, knowing the **Law’s** noble benefits.

Only then will you be granted to receive the **True Scripture’s Celestial Texts**, to govern the **Primordial Sovereign’s** harmonization of all **Heavens**.

The Three Heavens—those of **Qing** (Azure), **Chi** (Vermilion), and **Yu** (Jade) **Qi**—are the realms of the three **Qi** essences.
The Six Heavens encompass **desire**, **form**, **formless**, **light dust**, **fine dust**, **light defilement**, and **fine defilement**, among others.

The **Heavenly Emperors and Divine Humans** expound the **Great**, **Middle**, and **Lesser Vehicles** of **Dao** in their teachings, each according to their rank in **Dao** practice. They deliver varied **small methods** and guide beings through transformation.

There are **thirty-six thousand kinds of Dao**. Within the human body, there are **thirty-six thousand divine qi**, varying in clarity, illumination, and strength. Some hold **true faith**, while others harbor **heretical views**; their roots and capacities differ. When they study, they attain what aligns with their inherent nature—thus, there are **Great Vehicle** and **Lesser Vehicle** paths.

These are the **thirty-six thousand kinds of Dao**, meant to **dispel** the doubts of those who seek and to **respond** to the intentions of those who come to inquire after the **Way**. Some say it is to **respond to the intentions of those destined to come**, each receiving according to their affinity and belief.

Thus, those who attain **enlightenment** speak of their doubts **dissolving like ice melting**. The character **dispel** (*shì*) is correct. Those who use **choose** (*zé*) instead are mistaken.

The **Three Dragons** refer to the **beginning**, **middle**, and **end** of the **Dragon Han** era. Some say: **Dragon Han**, **Dragon Kang**, and **Dragon Zheng**. When **mixed qi** universally dissipates, the age grows auspicious, and **demonic influences** subside. The **Heavens rejoice in assembly**, gathering in times of universal prosperity. Some say: the **Heavens rejoice in the **Law Assembly***.

The **Mystic Precepts of Heaven’s Law** have **natural prohibitions**. Though the **Dao** does not discriminate in its transmission, speaking to the unworthy is **profaning Heaven’s treasures** and risks **erroneous speech**. Thus, the **Sages of the Three Teachings** must find the **right time**, the **right place**, and the **right person** before they **deliver the Law** and **transmit the Dao**.

The **Golden Decree** is compared to the **Mystic Decree**—it judges **merit and demerit** according to the **Law’s ordinances**. To **bow and rise before the Divine Kings** means to **look upward to the Immortals and downward to the Heavenly Kings and Marshal-Gods**, acknowledging the **Law’s** noble benefits.

To **govern the Primordial Sovereign’s Heavens** is to **command and lead** the Heavens transformed by the **Primordial Origin**. Some say: **bow and rise** (*fǔyǎng*) is akin to **demonstrate** (*shì*), meaning to **show reverence in bowing and humility in listening** before the Divine Kings, thus **governing the Primordial Sovereign’s Heavens**. To **assemble and lead the Heavens** is to **draw near to the **Law Vehicle** of the **Primordial Origin’s** highest Heaven. Both interpretations are valid.

**Chapter on Divine Incantations**

Then, the **Five Elder Celestial Sovereigns**, along with the **True Saints**, offered **pure incense**, upheld the **Precepts**, and wandered the **Cloud Paths**, summoning the **Ten Directions** with their **whistled commands**. They ascended to the **Upper Pure Supreme Mystic Jade Capital**, the **Cold-Spirit Elixir Hall**, and the **Purple Micro Upper Palace**, receiving the **Decree of Bowing and Rising**. Only then did they realize the **Heavenly Truth’s** nobility and rarity—how difficult it is to hear it immediately. Returning, they once more knelt before the **Primordial Dao**, inquiring about the **rituals of prohibition and precept**, humbly apologizing for their inadequacy.

They listened to the **Celestial Voice** through the **Golden Decree** before receiving the **True Scripture’s Heavenly Texts**.

Thus, the **Five Elder Celestial Sovereigns of the Five Directions**, along with the **Heavenly True Saints**, donned **pure incense**, observed the **Dao Precepts**, and circled the **Cloud Crossroads**, coming and going in guidance. They lingered along the **Cloud Paths**, chanting and commanding the **Ten Directions’ Holy Ones**, ascending to the **Upper Pure Supreme Mystic Jade Capital**, the **Heavenly Palace of Wondrous Realms**, the **Cold-Spirit Elixir Throne Hall**, and the **Purple Micro Upper Mystic Palace**, receiving the **Decree of Bowing and Rising**.

Only then did they grasp the **Heavenly Texts’ True Scripture’s** exalted and solemn nature—how rare and difficult it is to hear immediately. Returning, they once more knelt before the **Primordial Dao**, seeking clarification on the **rituals of prohibition and precept**, humbly acknowledging their insufficient wisdom.

**Pure Incense** refers to the **True Nature’s Heavenly Incense**, the **Pure and Natural Incense**, the **Non-Action’s Supreme Moral Dao Incense**—not the mundane burnt incense of the world.

**Upholding the Precepts** means observing the **Mystic Standards** with solemn reverence, as before the **Dao Ancestors**. They **guarded the Heavenly Sovereign’s Law Precepts**, wandering in boundless compassion, their **Mystic Light Vehicle** commanding the **Ten Directions** along the **Cloud Paths**.

The ancient scholars said: *"Heavenly Light and Cloud Shadows wander together"*—this is the meaning. It is not like the worldly **hesitation and back-and-forth movement**.

**Whistled Commands to the Ten Directions**—the **whistle** (*xiào*) is pronounced as **decree** (*chè*), not as **laugh** (*xiào*). Those who read it as **finesse** (*xiù*) are mistaken. The **whistle** is a solemn proclamation, not a jest or laughter.

**Ten Directions** refers not to the **Ten Sacred Treasures**, but to the **Ten Directional Divine Departments**.

To **ascend to the Immortals** is to **pay homage to the Primordial** and receive the **Law**, ascending in **Mystic Light** in silence, reverently listening to the **Mystic Teachings**—not the mundane climbing of steps.

The **Cold-Spirit Elixir Hall** lies above the **Nine Heavens**, where there is no sound or breath; the sun and moon cannot reach it. The **Heavenly Light** shines of its own accord, vast and boundless, pure and coldly solemn. The **Elixir Hall** radiates **Great Vermilion Jade Light**, hence the name.

The **Purple Micro Upper Palace** is the **Upper Mystic Palace** within the **Taiwei Heaven** above the **Purple Confluence**—not the **Purple Micro Enclosure** or **Taiwei Enclosure** as known in the mundane world.

**Bowing and Rising Decree**—see earlier explanation.

**Difficult to hear immediately** does not mean it is hard to hear at that very moment, but that it is difficult to **hear and immediately comprehend**. Some say: the **Heavenly Capital’s Scripture Keepers** do not allow immediate hearing. Returning, they once more ascend to the **Primordial Sovereign’s Nine Heavens**, paying homage to the **Supreme Primordial**, and are granted the **rituals of prohibition and precept**.

**Inquire**—see earlier explanation. To ask about the **Heavenly Law’s rituals** for transmitting and receiving the **Law**.

**Prohibition** refers to **decrees**; **Precept** refers to **statutes**.

**Humbly apologizing for inadequacy** does not mean they could not uphold prohibitions or observe precepts, but that they modestly acknowledged their **insufficient wisdom**—though their bodies were divine and their **Law Treasures** had never been truly penetrated, hearing them at once left their wisdom **unable to grasp** the depth. This is the true nobility of the **Five Old Ones’ Heavenly Dao**.

It is not self-imposed limitation, but the recognition that they were **unworthy to receive** this.

All things under Heaven have their **principles** and can **hear the Dao**. Thus, the **Four Spirits** gather their respective talents. Humans are the **most spiritual** of all things, and **Divine Beings** are the **highest rank** in the world—how could they not hear the **Dao**?

Thus, **Yan Hui** daily listened to **Confucius’ teachings** without deviation, as if in ignorance, yet understood through dialogue. After **Zhuo Lu’s** departure, he said, *"Though I wish to follow, there is no way."*

The **Bodhisattva Manjushrī** transmitted the **Sakyamuni Buddha’s True Law of the True Vehicle**—those who heard it were **deeply moved**.

「This aligns with the same meaning.

Those who hold this **Sutra** understand the **Five Old Ones’** humble yet profound intent in revering its sacred teachings—thus, they grasp the **Dao**.

The **Divine Beings’** *Spiritual Incantations* consist of **nine chapters**. At that time, the **Heavenly Sovereign** of boundless **virtue/power** and compassionate countenance, in pity, opened the **Spiritual Gate** and commanded the **Five Old Ones, Imperial Lords**, to reveal the **Dongyang Sunlight Hall**. Unfolding the **Nine Radiant Lights and Eight Colors** of their **treasure**, the **Cloud-Brocade Bag**, they produced the ***Elemental Origin’s Spiritual Treasure: Scarlet Scripture, Jade Leaf, True Text***, inscribed in **golden script and jade seals**, profound and mysterious, capable of governing the **Heavenly Dao** and **Earthly principles** of all worlds. The ***Great Illuminating Perfection, Great Spiritual Treasure Incantation of the Jade Chapter***, was then proclaimed and entrusted to the **Five Old Ones, Imperial Lords**.

Upon receiving this **Sutra**, the **Five Old Ones, Imperial Lords** bowed in reverence, and the **Celestial Saints** of all realms knelt in homage, thanking the **Heavenly Sovereign, Jade Emperor**. They uplifted the **Dao’s** intent and followed the **Law** to transmit it.

The **Five Old Ones, Imperial Lords** and the **True Saints** were unworthy to receive this, yet at that time, the **Elemental Origin’s Heavenly Sovereign** of boundless **virtue/power** and compassionate countenance, in pity and mercy, opened the **Spiritual Gate** with divine radiance. He commanded the **Five Old Ones, Imperial Lords** to reveal the **Heavenly Sunlight Hall of Dongyang**, unfurling the **Nine Glorious Clouds and Eight Scenic Colors** of their **treasure**, the **Cloud-Brocade Bag**, and produced the ***Elemental Origin’s Spiritual Treasure: Scarlet Scripture, Jade Leaf, True Text***, inscribed in **golden script and jade seals**, profound and mysterious, secret and profound, capable of governing and harmonizing all worlds and **Heavenly Dao and Earthly principles**, the ***Great Illuminating Perfection, Supreme Great Spiritual Treasure Incantation of the Jade Chapter***, which was then proclaimed and entrusted to the **Five Old Ones, Imperial Lords**.

At that time, the **Five Old Ones, Imperial Lords** had received this **Sutra** in full. The **Celestial Saints** of all realms knelt in homage, thanking the **Heavenly Sovereign, Jade Emperor**. They uplifted the **Elemental Origin’s Dao** and followed this **Sutra’s** golden **Law**, to transmit it to all **Divine Beings and Humans** across the realms.

**Mercy and instruction**. **Mercy (愍)**, that is, the **Great Compassion (大悲)**.

「Instruction (谕), the act of opening and guiding. Some mistakenly claim it should be read as *and-yú* (和愉), but this is incorrect.

The **Divine Passages** were revealed. The **Heaven of Sutra Storage**, the **Crimson Spirit’s Mystic Portal**, stood wide and gaping.

One interpretation states: The **Divine Passages** were revealed to open the **Sacred Core**, to awaken the Heart and manifest the True.
Another interpretation states: The **Sacred Eyes** emitted radiance, and the **Divine Passages** were revealed.
Both interpretations are valid.

**Ascending to Proclaim**. The **Five Old Ones, Imperial Lords** were elevated in rank, brought near to receive the **Sovereign’s Personal Command**.

The **Dawning Yang’s Jade Hall**, the **Nine-Heaven Mystic Hall**, was boundless and unobstructed, eternally luminous and never dark. It was not constructed of tiles, stones, earth, or wood, but adorned with **Mystic Radiance** and wondrous scenes, its **Spiral Script** intricately arranged, a **Jade Chapter** of emerald hue—thus it was called.

The **Nine Lights** have been explained previously. The **Eight Colors** are: **Supreme Azure (太青)**, **Supreme Vermilion (太赤)**, **Supreme Yellow (太黄)**, **Supreme White (太白)**, **Supreme Dark (太玄)**, **Celestial Cyan (葱苍)**, **Jade Green (碧玉)**, and **Purple Gold (紫金)**.

**韫 (yùn)**, the repository of the **Sutra**, wherein the boundless **Mystic Radiance** is entirely contained.
**披 (pī)**, to unfold and reveal.
The **Cloud-Silk Bag**, the **Celestial Brocade of Clouds and Mist**, was a natural formation of **Dao** emanations, not the handiwork of the **Heavenly Youth** weaving. It was called a bag because the **Sutra’s** annotations were inscribed within it. The **Divine Beings** could not fathom its depths—thus it was called.
It was not like the coarse cloth, silk, leather, or furs of the mortal world.

The phrases *"Great Illuminating Perfection"* and *"Supreme Great Spiritual Treasure"* through *"Heavenly Dao and Earthly principles"* have all been explained previously.

**Great Radiance (大光明)**, for the **True Scripts** of the **Three Teachings** all extol the **Law of Perfection** as the **Spiritual Treasure**, and wherever it resides, there is light. The **Scriptures** of all other **Teachings** have limited radiance, but this *Royal Sutra*’s **Law** permeates the **Three Thousand Great Thousand Worlds**, its luminosity undiminished across **aeons of kalpas**—thus it is called **Great Radiance**.

**Round and Fulfilled (圆满)**, the **Sacred Heart**’s boundless compassion and salvation. If one’s power is insufficient, the scope is limited, and there are deficiencies—thus it was said that one could not transform the **Northern Pole’s Lu State** nor the **Self-Sovereign Celestial Beings**, and it was difficult to call such **Round and Fulfilled**.

This *Royal Sutra* encompasses all **dharma**, penetrating all **vehicles**, its efficacy infinite and inexhaustible. Though it is said that the **Dao** does not force or compel, its transformations occur naturally, and all categories of beings—from beginning to end—cycle through its influence without any who are not transformed by it. Thus it is called **Round and Fulfilled**.

The **Divine Incantation of the Jade Chapter**, the **Essential Teachings of the True Ones**, the **Mystic Secrets of the Gods**, the **Key Essence for Delivering the World**—all other **Teachings’** divine powers do not surpass this; its reverence is unmatched. Thus it is called.

Another examination: Human nature’s enlightenment of the **Dao** is vast and enduring, difficult to forget even through **great kalpas**. Like a bag that does not leak, the moment of awakening is akin to the mouth of the bag—thus the **Sutra’s** annotations speak of the bag.

**Heavenly Sovereign (天尊)**, some read it connected to the preceding sentence: *"They knelt in homage and thanked the **Heavenly Sovereign, Original Beginning**"*; others read it connected to the following: *"The **Jade Emperor** is the **Sovereign** of all **Heavens**."* The latter interpretation may be adopted. The rest has been explained previously.

The **Divine Incantations Chapter** consists of ten sections. At that time, the **Heavenly Sovereign of the Azure Spirit (青灵始老苍帝)**, who received the **Divine Incantations Edict**, was stationed in the **Eastern Treasure Forest of Peaceful Preservation (安宝华林)**. The **Eastern Nine Qi (九炁)**—the Azure Sovereign of the Original Heaven (始皇青天), the Verdant Celestial Pile (碧霞郁垒)**—within which dwells the **Venerable Old Man (老人)**, oversees the **Register of Destiny (图录)**, commands the **Qi** and ascends to **Xian (仙)**.

To the right, the **Secret Scriptures of the Azure Sovereign for Delivering Humans to Xian (度人录仙青帝秘文)****,** twenty-four characters, inscribed upon the **Mysterious Terrace of the Nine Heavens (九天玄台)**, governs the summoning of the **Nine-Heaven Sovereign (九天上帝)** and the rectification of the **Register of Immortals (神仙图录)**. The **Year-Star (岁星)** assists the liver, while the **Horn (角)** and **Knee (亢)** stars stabilize the **True (真)**. The **Room (房)** and **Tail (尾)** stars oversee the **Four Scenes (四景)**, revolving in harmony. The **Sieves (箕)** commands the seven stars of the **Big Dipper (七辰)**, while the **Upright Fighter (正斗)** illuminates the **Wheel of Destiny (明轮)**. By capturing **Qi** and seizing the **False (非)**, it sweeps away the **Group of Calamities (灾群)**.

To the right, the **Secret Scriptures of the Stars (制星秘文)**, thirty-two characters, inscribed in the **Eastern Hall of the Purple Micro (紫微宫东华殿)**, governs the summoning of the **Celestial Officials (星官)** and the rectification of the **Heavenly Divisions and Degrees (天分度)**.

The **Eastern Mountain Divine Incantations (东山神咒)**, inscribed in **Red Scriptures and Edicts (赤书符命)**, subdue the **Mountain of Assemblies (酆山)**, bind the **Demons (魔)**, and dispatch the **Ghosts (鬼)**—none escape its judgment. All must proceed to the **Wood Palace (木宫)**, daring not to delay.

To the right, the **Secret Scriptures Against Demons (制魔秘文)**, thirty-two characters, inscribed in the **Eastern Hall of the Mysterious Spirit (东华玄灵之馆)**, governs the subjugation of **Ghosts and Demons (鬼魔)** and the rectification of the **Nine-Heaven Qi (九天炁)**. Below, it commands the **Eastern River (东河)** and the **Spirits of the Boundless Seas (溟海水神)**. In times of **Great Kalpas (大劫)** and **Flooding Disasters (洪灾)**, the **Kylin Dragons (蛟龙)** bear the weight of their bodies. When the **Water Palaces (水府)** are opened, the paths extend ten thousandfold. The **Heavenly Sovereign’s Red Scriptures (上帝赤文)** command the winds and fires without obstruction.

To the right, the **Secret Scriptures of Water (制水秘文)**, thirty-two characters, inscribed upon the **Nine-Heaven Eastern-Northern Jade Gate and Vermilion Terrace (九天东北玉阙丹台)**, governs the subjugation of the **Eastern Sea Water Sovereign (东海水帝)**, the **Great Kalpa Flooding Disasters (大劫洪灾)**, and the summoning of **Kylin Dragons (蛟龙)** and **Water Spirits (水神)** for their duties.

The **True Scripture of the Eastern Nine Qi Spirit Treasures (《东方九炁灵宝玉篇》)****—**all one hundred twenty characters—**are the perfect scriptures of the **Supreme Lord of the Most High Great Radiant Dao (太上无上大光明)**,** the **Complete and Natural Divine Incantations (圆满神咒空洞自然之书)**. It is also known as the **Scripture of the Birth of the Divine and Preservation of the True (《生神保真洞玄章》)****,** the **Eastern Mountain Divine Incantations (《东山神咒》)****,** and the **Azure Sovereign’s Eight Thunders Edict (《青帝八威策文》)**.

These **Edicts of the Jade Emperor (玉皇诰命)**** are granted to the **Nine-Qi Heavenly Lords of the Eastern Treasure Forest of Peaceful Preservation, Azure Spirit Heavenly Sovereign (东方安宝华林青灵始老苍帝九炁天君)**,** commanding them to oversee all **Eastern Heavens and Earths (东方诸天诸地)**, the **Sun, Moon, and Starry Hosts (日月星宿)**, the **Sacred Mountains and Spirit Caverns (名山灵洞)**, the **Water Palaces and Spring Palaces (水府泉宫)**, the **Supreme High Lords (上圣高尊)**, and the **Holy Immortal Assemblies (真仙圣众)**—**all manifestations of power and spirit (一切威灵)**. Wherever the **Scriptures and Edicts (符命)** descend, they must be obeyed as decreed.

The **Jade Emperor** reverently upholds the **Dao**’s decrees, following the **Law** to transmit the **True Scripture**’s divine incantations—what is their intent?

The **Five Old Heavenly Lords**, with the **Eastern** as their foremost. The **Eastern** embodies **Wood Virtue**. The **Sacred Edicts** received by the **Azure Spirit Heavenly Sovereign of the Eastern Treasure Forest of Peaceful Preservation (安宝华林青灵始老苍帝)**.

The **Eight Sentences from the Year-Star to Assist the Liver and Sweep Away Disastrous Groups**, comprising **32 characters**, are the **Star’s Secret Texts**, inscribed in the **Eastern Hua Hall of the Purple Micro Palace (紫微宫东华殿)**, to **convoke the Wood Virtue Star Lord** and **regulate the celestial divisions**.

The **Eight Sentences from the Eastern Divine Incantations to the Dare Not Delay**, comprising **32 characters**, are the **Secret Texts of the Eastern Demons**, inscribed in the **Eastern Hua Azure Spirit Hall (东华玄灵之馆)**, to **subdue the ghosts and demons** and **rectify the Nine-Qi of the Eastern realms**.

The **Eight Sentences from the Eastern River Regulation to the Uninterrupted Wind and Fire**, comprising **32 characters**, are the **Secret Texts of the Eastern Waters**, inscribed upon the **Nine-Heaven Eastern-North Jade Gate Vermilion Platform (九天东北玉阙丹台)**, to **subdue the Eastern Sea Water Emperor**, **great calamities and floods**, and **convoke the dragons and water deities**.

The **Eastern Nine-Qi Sacred Incantations (九炁灵宝赤书玉篇)**—the **True Scripture**—comprises **120 characters**, all being the **Supreme Most Perfect Great Light and Fulfilled Divine Incantations**, the **Natural and Spontaneous Scriptures of the Void**, also known as the **Scripture of Preserving the Divine Essence and Safeguarding the True (生神宝真洞玄章)** and the **Azure Emperor’s Eight Thunders Edict (青帝八威策文)**.

The above cannot be deciphered.
Thus, the original text is re-inscribed.

This **Scripture preserves the profound secrets of the great virtue of Heaven, Earth, and all beings, causing demons to lose their resolve, transcending calamities, and sparing disasters**. The **Celestial Assemblies dare not disobey**, thus it **permanently secures the Eastern realms**.

inscribed within the **Void’s Idle Single’s Boundless Mystic Obscure Platform**,
commanding the **Northern Celestial Demon Emperor**,
**subduing all malevolent gods and myriad ghosts**.

**The Nine Rivers’ Torrent Exhausted, the Courier Dragon Gallops on the Wind—Six Sentences of Twenty-Four Characters**,
**Sacred Dao-Words for Governing Waters**,
inscribed within the **Void’s Idle Single’s Boundless Primordial Platform**,
commanding the **Northern Sea Water Emperor**,
**subduing all water spirits within**,
**mastering the summoning of Giant Dragons to arise clouds and direct rains**.

**The Northern Five *Qi*’s True Dao-Words—**
totaling **One Hundred and Twenty Characters**,
all are **Supreme Dao-Cauldron’s Most High Divine Cauldron Dao-Words**,
also named **Original Command’s Purple Micro Primordial Spirit’s True Treasure of Radiant Dao-Words**,
also named **Northern Mountain’s Divine Cauldron**,
also named **Black Emperor’s Eightfold Awe Dao-Words for Controlling Heaven**.

**The Jade Sovereign’s Edicts**—
**bestowing upon the Northern Five *Qi*’s Primordial Black Emperor, the Five *Qi* Heavenly Lord**,
**ordering governance over the Northern Celestial Realms, Earths, Sun, Moon, and Stars**,
**sacred mountains and spirit-filled caverns**,
**waterways and springs**,
**saints and true divine immortals**,
**all awe-inspiring spirits**—
**where talismans and edicts descend, obey as commanded**.

**Transcending mortals and recording immortals**,
**controlling stars, subduing demons, governing waters**—
**all secrets of the Northern Mystic are grasped**,
**thus none dare ever defy**.

**Granting the Five *Qi* Dao-Words of the Five Emperors**,
**eternally stabilizing all worlds**,
**the Three Teachings and myriad beings**—
**none can escape**.

**Eternally unbroken through kalpas**,
**void yet wondrously manifest**—
**secrets beyond exhaustion**;
**mysterious beyond the mysterious**,
**divine beyond divinity**.

**My body’s Five *Qi* are all complete in principle**.
**Aspiring scholars and enlightened individuals**—
**penetrating the essence of life and death**,
**attaining the source of all dharmas**,
**unable to defy the laws of principle and number**.

**The True Scripture abides within me**,
**the divine cauldron’s efficacy belongs to this**.
**Chapter Fifteen of the Divine Cauldron**—
**Dao-Speech says**:

**This is the Great Divine Cauldron**—
**Primordial Origin’s wondrous speech**,
**Jade Sovereign’s true edicts**,
**Supreme Purity’s natural sacred scriptures**,
**Nine Heavens’ primordial mystic scriptures**,
**void’s sacred chapters**,
**Highest Saint’s secret words**,
**Jade Sovereign’s exalted ordinances**—
**completing the heavens and establishing the earth**,
**unfolding myriad transformations**,
**calming the spirit and stabilizing the soul**,
**generating and nurturing myriad folk**,
**guiding and governing the cosmic order**,
**preserving the heavens in eternal existence**;
**supremely controlling celestial mechanisms**,
**midst checking the Five *Qi*’s spirits**,
**lowly commanding the Earth Spirits**,
**whistling orders to all river sources**,
**directing and harnessing yin and yang**,
**summoning gods and dispatching immortals**—
**this is the utmost true wonder**.

**Again, the divine responds naturally**,
**clarifying the heavens’ purity**,
**solidifying the earth’s stability**,
**preserving and stabilizing the Five Sacred Peaks**,
**all beings endure**.

**The Five Directions’ Divine Cauldrons’ wondrous transformations are boundless—why so?**
**Dao-Speech says**:

**This is the Great Divine Cauldron**—
**Primordial Origin’s Supreme Heavenly Lord’s most mystic speech**,
**Jade Sovereign’s Supreme Heavenly Lord’s most true treasure-edicts**,
**Supreme Purity’s Mystic Primordial Natural Sacred Scriptures**,
**Nine Heavens’ Immortal Realm’s primordial mystic scriptures and immortal talismans**,
**Great Void’s sacred chapters**,
**Supreme Ultimate’s Most High Saint’s mystic secret words**,
**Purple Micro’s Jade Sovereign’s most exalted sacred ordinances**—
**completing all heavens above, establishing all earths below**,
**unfolding myriad wondrous transformations**,
**summarizing all gods, stabilizing all spirits**,
**one generation, one completion**,
**countless myriad folk**,
**guiding and governing the kalpas’ transformations and cosmic order**,
**preserving all heavens in eternal existence**;
**supremely controlling the heavens’ covering and life’s origin**,
**midst checking and controlling the Five Directions’ Five *Qi*’s spirits**,
**lowly commanding the Earth Spirits**,
**whistling orders to all water palaces and river sources**,
**directing and harnessing yin and yang**,
**summoning all gods and dispatching true immortals**—
**this is the Great Divine Cauldron**,
**the utmost true mystic scriptures**,
**divine transformations responding wondrously**,
**emerging only from the natural**.

「The highest station is in the heavens,
obtaining the *One* to attain clarity,
lofty and bright, vast and enduring—
this is what brings forth the heavens’ lofty purity.

The lowest station is in the earth,
obtaining the *One* to attain tranquility,
broad and profound, vast and enduring—
this is what brings forth the earth’s enduring stability.

Forever securing and preserving the Five Sacred Peaks and named mountains,
all myriad beings and categories made to endure eternally.

**Dao/Way**’s utterances—
these are the Five *Lao* Celestial Deities’ **virtue/power**-bestowed teachings and praises,
thus they are called *Yuan Shi* Jade Sovereign and such,
not the *Yuan Shi* self-praising.

The wondrous utterances and sacred scriptures of the utmost **virtue/power**—
all explained as seen before.

The *Nine Heavens’* primordial **Dao/Way**’s secret inscriptions**,
called *handwritten scrolls* (*zhà*)—
The *Jade Sovereign’s True Scripture* (*Yùhuáng Zhēnjīng*)
is without form or sound,
yet radiant light and wondrous tones permeate the Ten Directions and all **dharma realms**,
enduring through kalpas without destruction—
not written by human hands,
but all from the natural.

Not transmitted by speech,
but all from the **mind-seal**’s mysteries.

Tracing it, there is no beginning,
existing before the Great Void’s formless expanse—
thus it is called the *Nine Heavens’* primordial **Dao/Way**’s secret inscriptions**.

The *Jade Sovereign’s* exalted **scriptures** (*Zhēndiǎn*),
for the **son of heaven**’s abode is called *Zhēn*,
and *Yuan Shi* is the sovereign of all teachings,
dwelling in the *Jade Purity Sacred Realm*,
with **Dao/Way**’s transformations beyond reckoning—
thus it is called *Yùhuáng*.

This **True Scripture** surpasses all teachings’ texts,
no deity or sage dares defy it—
the **heavenly laws** are as heavy as golden decrees,
and the Ten Directions’ holy guardians are as stern as precious defenses—
thus it is called the *exalted scriptures*.

**To stabilize spirits**—
to keep all gods from displaying their **godly powers** (*shéntōng*),
calmly abiding without action.

**To govern spirits**—
to keep all spirits from revealing their **mystic resonance** (*língxiǎng*),
restraining their awe and **virtue/power**.

**To guide and govern cosmic transformations and kalpas**—
throughout beginning and end of the **dharma realms**,
overseeing the kalpas’ revolutions,
transformations and guidance without limit—
to make them cycle endlessly,
unshaken and undisturbed—
thus it is called *guiding and governing cosmic transformations and kalpas*.

**To command the Earth Spirits** (*dìzhǐ*)—
this is the **scripture’s** profound decree, not the whip of command.
**To direct and harness yin and yang**—
as yin and yang ebb and flow,
**Dao/Way** truly governs them—
thus it is said *to direct and harness yin and yang*,
not to mean *enslaving yin spirits and yang deities*.

**To summon gods**—
to gather all gods.

**To dispatch true immortals** (*xiān*):
true immortals are the **son of heaven**’s honored guests—
why say *to dispatch*?
For *Yuan Shi* proclaims this **Scripture**,
the authentic core of the Three Teachings,
all gods reverently accept it—
thus it is said *to dispatch true immortals*.

Heaven and earth have limits,
all beings may eventually perish—
yet why say *all myriad categories endure*?
From kalpa to kalpa, life perpetually renews,
all relying on the Great **Dao/Way**—
thus it is said *all myriad categories endure*.

The *Great Divine Cauldron*’s **Scripture** comprises sixteen chapters,
which the Jade Sovereign once bestowed upon the Five *Lao* Celestial Deities.

At that time, the Five Emperors knelt in long reverence,
holding this sacred scroll,
secretly inscribed with praises in the **mystic capital** (*Língdū*).

The *Heavenly True Immortal* (*Tiānzhēn*) once recorded these words,
entrusted to the *Upper Purity Sacred Realm*’s *Great Mystic Jade Capital*,
the *Cold Soul Elixir Hall* (*Hánlíng Dāndiàn*),
and the *Purple Cloud Celestial Palace* (*Zǐwēi Shànggōng*).

Through countless kalpas and cosmic revolutions,
its words preserved the **heavenly roots** (*Tiāngēn*),
unbroken and uncorrupted—
aligned with the **primordial revolutions** (*Yuán yùn*), shifting as they turn.

This *Great Divine Cauldron*’s **Scripture**—
when mixed with chaos, it remains undefiled,
when defiled, it shines ever purer;
when destroyed, it is not extinguished,
when extinguished, it becomes supremely luminous.

The **Great Ultimate**’s profound mysteries—
the Heavenly True Immortals hold them in reverence,
its own radiant light and **true name** (*Zhēnmíng*) manifest,
as the Jade Sovereign’s decrees are inscribed upon golden tablets,
revealing to all future generations of beings.

This **Scripture**’s words are hidden and profound,
unseen by ordinary folk.

Those who attain this **Dao/Way**’s children
preserve all **cosmic qi** (*wànjī*) in eternal existence.
Diligently practicing and revering it,
they attain **godly immortality** (*shénxiān*),
and bow in homage to the Exalted Sovereign.

The Five Emperors knelt in long reverence,
holding this precious scroll—
the **Scripture** dwells in heaven,
its words are **Dao/Way**’s mysteries, not worldly texts—
how then speak of *handwritten*?
The heavenly gods reverently embrace it,
expressing utmost respect.

**Secretly inscribed**—
this means to praise and record it.
The Heavenly True Immortals’ scriptures
are all **Dao/Way**’s radiant celestial texts,
golden and jade characters,
each a wondrous span of a yard in length.
The *Upper Purity Sacred Realm* is the abode of the **Lingbao** treasures**,
and the **Scripture** originates from the *Primordial Beginning*’s Exalted Sovereign,
transmitted by **Lingbao**—
thus it is called the *Upper Purity Sacred Realm*.
Its words preserve the **heavenly roots**,
the **Scripture**’s essence unbroken through kalpas—
thus the **heavenly roots**’ eternal preservation is known.

Some may say it preserves the **heaven’s root**,
making it endure—
this cannot be followed.
For after the *Primordial Beginning* (*Yuán Huì*),
heaven cannot last forever—
thus it is known this is not the **heaven’s root**.

**Aligned with the revolutions**—
enduring through kalpas.

When mixed with chaos, it remains undefiled—
when laws and doctrines are confused,
the true **Dao/Way** persists,
yet this **Scripture** cannot be defiled.
When defiled, it shines ever purer—
those who profane this **Scripture** face heavenly punishment,
its **virtue/power** and purity ever more evident.

When destroyed, it is not extinguished—
the foolish and perverse who slander and destroy this **Scripture**
cannot erase it.
When extinguished, it becomes supremely luminous—
in an age without **Dao/Way**,
if they seek to destroy this **Scripture**,
its teachings will spread widely,
its brilliance ever more manifest.

The **Great Ultimate**’s profound mysteries—
ever-present through kalpas,
found everywhere without absence—
not ordinary forms,
but **wondrous existence** (*miàohǔ*).
Thus it is called *the **Great Ultimate***.

Some may say *the **Great Ultimate**’s profound mysteries* are the words of the *Court of Ultimate Mysteries*—
this is too restrictive.»

Illuminating future births—
the myriad lives to come are not merely one person’s future existence.
Those unable to glimpse or hear it—
only the **Most Venerable Ones** (*zhìshèng*) know this **Scripture**,
while common folk merely recite its words.

Evil spirits dare not peek,
while the lowly and ignorant cannot hear it.
Those who grasp the **Dao/Way**’s principles within this **Scripture**,
preserve my **ten thousand kinds of qi** (*wànqì*) eternally,
and through diligent practice reach **Divine Immortal** (*shénxiān*) status,
thus paying homage to the **Most High Emperor** (*Dàdì*).

Some say *pay homage to the Five Elders of the Emperor*—
this is too restrictive.

One alternative:
*preserve the **ten thousand transformations**’s *qi* eternally,
also suffices.

This passage reveals the **Scripture**’s manifest efficacy.

**Chapter 3: The Virtue/Power of the Jade Sovereign** (*Yùhuáng Gōngdé Pǐn*)
**Continuation of Chapter 1, following the previous ten chapters**
At that time, the Jade Void Emperor (*Yùxū Dìshì*) addressed the Celestial Venerable (*Tiānzūn*):

*"May the Most Venerable One’s compassion universally benefit the Four Assemblies, the **Emperors and Releases** (*Dìshè*), the Four **Brahmā Kings** (*Fàn Tiānwáng*), all the **Heavens** (*Zhūtian*), all the **Immortal Ones** (*Zhūxiān*), and all future beings who uphold this **Scripture** and proclaim its benefits."*

At that time, the Celestial Venerable replied to the Jade Void Emperor:

*"How joyous is this inquiry—
is it not most excellent? (*bù yì shànhū*)
You, moved by compassion,
pity the suffering of all beings,
thus asking me for elucidation.
Return to your seat,
and I shall expound it for you.*

When the Jade Sovereign (*Yùdì*) entrusted this **Scripture** to the Five Elders of the Emperor,
the Jade Void Emperor ascended and reported to the **Great Celestial Venerable** (*Dà Tiānzūn*), the **Scripture**’s master:

*"May the Most Venerable One’s compassion universally benefit the world’s Four Assemblies,
all the **Heavenly Emperors and Releases** (*Tiānshì Dìshè*),
the Four **Brahmā Kings** of the Three Realms (*Sānjiè shàng sì Fàn Tiānwáng*),
all the **Heavens** (*Zhūtian*),
all the **Immortal Ones** of every rank (*Zhūxiān*),
and all future beings who uphold this **True Scripture** and proclaim its benefits."*

At that time, the **Great Celestial Venerable**, the **Scripture**’s master, replied to the Jade Void Emperor:

*"How gladdening is this question—
is it not most excellent? (*bù yì shànhū*)
You, with compassionate heart,
pity the world’s suffering beings,
thus asking me for elucidation.
Return to your seat,
and I shall expound the **Scripture**’s meaning for you."*

When the **Celestial Venerable** (*Tiānzūn*) refers to *Yuan Shi*,
or to the Jade Sovereign (*Yùdì*),
this is incorrect.
The Four Assemblies (*Sìzhòng*) are explained earlier.
**Emperors and Releases** (*Dìshè*) are the Heavenly Emperors,
and the **Buddhas, Bodhisattvas** (*Fó, Púsà*), and others of the **Release Teachings** (*Shìjiào*).
Some may say all Heavenly sovereigns are called **Emperors and Releases**,
which is also acceptable.
If one mistakenly takes *Emperor* (*Dì*) as the sovereign of the **Emperors and Releases Heaven** (*Dìshè Tiān*),
this is the erroneous interpretation of the **Monks** (*Sēngjiā*).
They wrongly apply the Heavenly sovereigns of all **Scriptures** to the Jade Sovereign,
unaware that the Jade Sovereign is the **宗** (*zōng*) of the ten thousand **Heavens**,
not merely the sovereign of one **Heaven**.

The **Release Teachings** (*Shìjiào*) state:
*"The **Brahmā King Emperor** (*Fànwáng Dìshè*) is the **呈祥** (*chéngxiáng*)."*
This means the **宗** (*zōng*) of the Heavenly **Buddhas**,
not daring to speak of the Jade Sovereign.
Monks arbitrarily misinterpret,
which is also a grave offense.
Hence, I include them both.

The Four **Brahmā Kings** (*Sì Fàn Tiānwáng*) are the great **Brahmā Kings** of the Three Realms’ uppermost tier,
not the sovereigns of the **Desire Realm**’s lower **Heavens**.
When speaking of **Brahmā Heavens** (*Fàn Tiān*),
it encompasses all upper **Realms**.
The **Heavens of the Heavenly Hosts** (*Zhǒngmín Zhūtian*) are not mentioned,
for their ranks above are all **至真大仙** (*Zhìzhēn Dàxiān*—**Supreme True Immortals**),
who naturally align with this **Scripture**,
thus no need to specify them.

All the **Heavens** (*Zhūtian*), all the **Immortal Ones** (*Zhūxiān*—**of every rank**),
from beneath the **Brahmā Heavens** down,
all Heavenly sovereigns, deities, and **民** (*mín*—**subjects of the Heavens**),
and all **Immortal Ones** of every rank (*Zhūxiān*).

**Proclaiming its benefits**—
the **Great Dao/Way** does not speak of effects,
so why does the Jade Void Emperor request benefits to be spoken of?
The **Great Dao/Way** is the **宗** (*zōng*) of all **Heavens**, earth, and beings.
It inherently possesses real benefits,
bringing natural advantage to all beings.
The **Heavens**, earth, and the Four Assemblies,
who do not know this **Scripture**,
